# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Multidimensional cost geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06957)
*Jonathan Washburn,Milan Zlatanović,Philip Beltracchi*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了由典型互易成本函数（canonical reciprocal cost function）及其n维扩展诱导的几何结构，发现在对数坐标下该几何本质上是退化的1维结构，而在原始x坐标下则表现为伪黎曼度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在分析典型互易成本函数（canonical reciprocal cost function）及其自然n维扩展所诱导的几何结构，探究在不同坐标表示下该函数所定义度量的性质差异。

Method: 研究采用几何分析方法，在对数坐标和原始x坐标两种表示下分别分析函数的Hessian度量性质，并进一步分析仿射测地线（affine geodesics）和Levi-Civita测地线的行为。

Result: 在对数坐标下，势函数仅依赖于线性组合S=α·t，对应的Hessian度量在每个点处秩为1，几何本质上是退化的1维结构，具有(n-1)维零分布。而在原始x坐标下，相应的Hessian通常非退化，在显式奇异超曲面外定义了伪黎曼度量（pseudo-Riemannian metric）。仿射测地线在对数坐标下全局定义，而在x坐标下其行为受定义域和奇异集限制。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了互易成本函数在不同坐标表示下几何性质的显著差异，并将该构造与对称Itakura-Saito散度、Bregman散度联系起来，给出了对数Hessian度量的Fisher-Rao实现。

Abstract: In this paper we study the geometric structure induced by the canonical reciprocal cost function and its natural $n$-dimensional extension. In logarithmic coordinates, the potential depends only on the linear combination $S=α\cdot t$, and the associated Hessian metric has rank one at every point. The geometry is intrinsically degenerate and effectively 1-dimensional, with an $(n-1)$-dimensional null distribution.
  On the other hand, when the same function is expressed in the original $x$-coordinates, the corresponding Hessian is generically nondegenerate and defines a pseudo-Riemannian metric away from explicit singular hypersurfaces.
  We further analyze affine and Levi-Civita geodesics and compare their behavior. In particular, affine geodesics in logarithmic coordinates are globally defined, while in $x$-coordinates their behavior is restricted by the domain and the singular set.
  Finally, we relate the construction to symmetrized Itakura-Saito and Bregman divergences, and give a Fisher-Rao realization of the logarithmic Hessian metric

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.stat-mech'></div>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Higher Nishimori Criticality and Exact Results at the Learning Transition of Deformed Toric Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06324)
*Rushikesh A. Patil,Malte Pütz,Simon Trebst,Guo-Yi Zhu,Andreas W. W. Ludwig*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视了变形环面码波函数在弱测量下的相图中的学习诱导三临界点，发现该点位于一条独特的高阶西岛线上，具有规范不变表述。作者证明这是一个高阶西岛临界点，并获得了多个精确结果，包括爱德华兹-安德森关联函数的幂律指数与未测量伊辛临界点的自旋关联函数指数相等。通过c-有效定理工具，作者展示了卡西米尔有效中心荷在重整化群流中从高阶西岛临界点到未测量2D伊辛临界点会减小，数值模拟支持这一结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在重新审视变形环面码（toric code）波函数在弱测量下相图中的学习诱导三临界点（learning-induced tricritical point）。该设置与二维经典伊辛模型（2D classical Ising model）的经典贝叶斯推断相图完全对偶。研究动机是深入理解这一三临界点的本质及其在更广泛框架中的位置。

Method: 作者通过建立该三临界点位于一条独特的高阶西岛线（higher Nishimori line）上的联系进行研究。该方法具有涌现的规范不变表述，类似于普通西岛线，但在副本数R→2极限下具有更高的副本对称性。研究使用了c-有效定理证明工具[arXiv:2507.07959]，并进行了广泛的数值模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 研究证明学习三临界点实际上是一个高阶西岛临界点（higher Nishimori critical point）。作者获得了该临界点的多个精确结果，包括爱德华兹-安德森关联函数（Edwards-Anderson correlation function）的幂律指数与未测量伊辛临界点的自旋关联函数指数完全相等。数值模拟验证了这一结果。此外，卡西米尔有效中心荷（Casimir effective central charge）在从高阶西岛临界点到未测量2D伊辛临界点的重整化群流中减小，数值模拟得到c_eff = 0.522(1)。

Conclusion: 该研究成功识别了学习诱导三临界点作为高阶西岛临界点的本质，并获得了多个精确结果。分析结果还解释了在随机键伊辛模型中从普通西岛临界点到清洁伊辛临界点的重整化群流中卡西米尔有效中心荷增加的现象。论文还讨论了在一般维度D>1中的高阶西岛临界性。

Abstract: We revisit a learning-induced tricritical point, at which three phases with strong, weak, and broken $Z_2$ symmetry meet, in the phase diagram of a deformed toric code wavefunction subjected to weak measurements. This setting is exactly dual to a classical Bayesian inference phase diagram of the $2D$ classical Ising model. Here we demonstrate that this tricritical point lies on a distinct $\textit{higher Nishimori line}$, which has an emergent gauge-invariant formulation, just like the ordinary Nishimori line but with a higher replica symmetry as a replica stat-mech model in the replica number $R\rightarrow2$ limit, where disorder is averaged according to the Born rule. As such, the learning tricritical point is in fact a $\textit{higher Nishimori critical point}$. Using this identification, we obtain a number of $\textit{exact results}$ at this $\textit{higher}$ Nishimori critical point; e.g., we show that the power-law exponent of the Edwards-Anderson correlation function is exactly equal to that of the spin correlation function at the unmeasured Ising critical point and verify this in numerical simulations. Using the tools of the proof of a $c$-effective theorem [arXiv:2507.07959], we show that the Casimir effective central charge $c_{\text{eff}}$ $\textit{decreases}$ under renormalization group (RG) flow from the $\textit{higher}$ Nishimori critical point to the unmeasured $2D$ Ising critical point, and is thus greater than $1/2$. This is corroborated by extensive numerical simulations finding $c_{\text{eff}} = 0.522(1)$. The analytical result also explains, with a physically motivated assumption, the numerically observed increase of the Casimir effective central charge under the RG flow from the ordinary Nishimori critical point to the clean Ising critical point in the random-bond Ising model. We also discuss $\textit{higher}$ Nishimori criticality in general dimensions $D>1$.

</details>


### [3] [Extensive Spatio-Temporal Chaos in Non-reciprocal Flocking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06462)
*Chul-Ung Woo,Jae Dong Noh,Heiko Rieger*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了非互易相互作用（non-reciprocal interactions）活性物质系统中，小群体呈现手性有序（chiral order），大群体则发展为时空混沌（spatiotemporal chaos），两者通过有限波长不稳定性（finite wavelength instability）共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易相互作用在活性物质中产生多种有趣现象，包括无内在粒子手性（intrinsic particle chirality）的集体振荡态和活性湍流（active turbulence）。研究旨在探索这些现象在非互易集群（non-reciprocal flocking）模型中的共存机制。

Method: 采用双物种Vicsek模型（two species Vicsek model）作为非互易集群的范式模型，分析系统尺寸与手性轨道旋转半径（rotation radius of chiral orbits）的关系，通过Floquet指数（Floquet exponents）、Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）等工具表征混沌行为。

Result: 研究发现小群体呈现手性有序，大群体则发展为广泛的时空混沌，两者通过有限波长不稳定性分离。当系统尺寸超过手性轨道旋转半径时，时空混沌表现为不稳定的手性态具有大量Floquet指数、正Lyapunov指数、有限相关长度和混沌长度，以及宽能量谱（broad energy spectrum）。

Conclusion: 复杂湍流行为是粒子或场非对称相互作用系统中的普遍可能性，这一发现对理解非互易相互作用如何驱动活性物质中的混沌、类流体行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: Non-reciprocal interactions in active matter gives rise to a multitude of fascinating phenomena among which are collective oscillatory states without intrinsic particle chirality and active turbulence. Here we show that in a paradigmatic model for non-reciprocal flocking, the two species Vicsek model, these two states coexist: chiral order for small flocks, and extensive spatiotemporal chaos for large flocks, both separated by a finite wavelength instability whose scale is set by the rotation radius of the chiral orbits. For system sizes larger than this length scale extensive spatiotemporal chaos unfolds, as manifested by an extensive number of Floquet exponents for the unstable chiral state, a positive Lyapunov exponent, a finite correlation and chaotic length and a broad energy spectrum. Our results suggest that complex, turbulent behavior is a generic possibility in any system where particles or fields interact asymmetrically and may have significant implications for understanding how non-reciprocal interactions could drive chaotic, fluid-like behavior in active matter.

</details>


### [4] [Dimensional crossover in surface growth on rectangular substrates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06486)
*Ismael S. S. Carrasco,Tiago J. Oliveira*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了界面生长中维度交叉（dimensional crossover）现象的分析，从KPZ类扩展到EW、MH和VLDS普适类（universality classes）。通过大规模模拟，揭示了在矩形基底上界面粗糙度（roughness）从二维到一维标度行为的转变，并探讨了特殊指数δ*对时间交叉现象的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究发现Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）界面在矩形基底上存在从二维到一维的维度交叉现象。本研究旨在将这一分析扩展到其他界面生长普适类，包括Edwards-Wilkinson（EW）、Mullins-Herring（MH）和Villain-Lai Das Sarma（VLDS）类，以验证维度交叉现象的普遍性。

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟方法，研究不同长宽比（aspect ratio）ℛ=Ly/Lx的矩形基底上界面生长行为。特别分析了VLDS类的高度分布（height distribution，HD）随时间的变化，并探讨了特殊尺寸关系Lx=Ly^δ（0<δ<1）下的标度行为。

Result: 在所有研究的系统中，当长宽比ℛ足够大时，粗糙度W在生长阶段呈现明确的维度交叉：t≪tc时遵循二维标度W∼t^{β_2D}，t≫tc时遵循一维标度W∼t^{β_1D}，其中tc∼Lx^{z_2D}。VLDS类的高度分布也表现出类似的交叉行为。研究发现存在特殊指数δ*=z_1D/z_2D，当δ>δ*时时间交叉现象无法观测到。

Conclusion: 维度交叉现象在多个界面生长普适类中普遍存在，包括粗糙度标度和高度分布行为。特殊尺寸关系Lx=Ly^δ揭示了系统的非普适标度行为，其中饱和粗糙度Ws∼Ly^Λ，Λ=(1-δ)α_1D+δα_2D，展示了二维和一维标度指数之间的插值关系。

Abstract: In a recent work [Phys. Rev. E 109, L042102 (2024)], interesting dimensional crossovers [from two- to one-dimensional (2D to 1D) scaling] were found in the growth of Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) interfaces on rectangular substrates, with lateral sizes $L_y > L_x$. Here, we extend this study to other universality classes for interface growth -- specifically, the Edwards-Wilkinson (EW), the Mullins-Herring (MH), and the Villain-Lai Das Sarma (VLDS) classes. From extensive simulations, we demonstrate that, in all systems with sufficiently large aspect ratio $\mathcal{R}=L_y/L_x$, the roughness $W$ scales with time $t$ in the growth regime as $W \sim t^{β_{\text{2D}}}$ for $t \ll t_c$ and $W \sim t^{β_{\text{1D}}}$ for $t \gg t_c$, where $t_c \sim L_x^{z_{2\text{D}}}$ in most cases. For the VLDS class, this crossover is also observed in the height distribution (HD), which approaches its characteristic probability density function for the 2D case at short times ($t \ll t_c$) and then crosses over to the asymptotic 1D HD. Dimensional crossovers are also found in the steady state regime, both in the roughness scaling as well as in the VLDS HD, which interpolate between the 2D and 1D ones as $\mathcal{R}$ increases. The particular case $L_x = L_y^δ$, with $0 < δ< 1$, is also discussed in detail and reveals interesting features of the investigated systems. For instance, there exist a `special' exponent $δ^* = z_{1\text{D}}/z_{2\text{D}}$ such that the temporal crossover cannot be observed for $δ> δ^*$. Moreover, this leads the saturation roughness to display a nonuniversal scaling: $W_s \sim L_y^Λ$, with $Λ= (1-δ) α_{1\text{D}} + δα_{2\text{D}}$.

</details>


### [5] [Balancing Power, Efficiency, and Constancy under Broken Time-Reversal Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07099)
*Ousi Pan,Zhiqiang Fan,Shunjie Zhang,Liwei Chen,Jincan Chen,Shanhe Su*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究推导了线性响应区双端热电系统中功率、效率和恒定性之间的普遍权衡关系，揭示了时间反演对称性破缺如何改变稳态能量转换的基本约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立热电系统性能参数间的普遍权衡关系，特别是探讨时间反演对称性破缺如何影响稳态能量转换的基本限制，以深化对非平衡热力学性能极限的理解。

Method: 在线性响应区（linear response regime）内，对双端热电系统（two-terminal thermoelectric systems）进行理论推导，通过量化热机恒定性的涨落测量来建立普遍约束关系。

Result: 推导出功率、效率和涨落（fluctuations）的普遍界限，这些界限在时间反演对称性破缺时仍然有效，揭示了对称性破缺如何改变稳态能量转换的基本约束。

Conclusion: 时间反演对称性破缺的热机可以在保持有限功率输出和涨落的同时，实现接近卡诺效率（near-Carnot efficiency）的运行，从而超越传统热机的性能限制。

Abstract: We derive general trade-off relations among the power, efficiency, and constancy for two-terminal thermoelectric systems in the linear response regime. Constancy, which quantifies the steadiness of the heat engine, is measured by its fluctuations. The bounds of the efficiency, power and fluctuations are valid even when time-reversal symmetry is broken, revealing how such a symmetry breaking alters the fundamental constraints on steady-state energy conversion. Our results extend and refine previously established universal trade-offs, offering deeper insight into the performance limits in nonequilibrium thermodynamics. Guided by this bound, heat engines with broken time-reversal symmetry can be operated at near-Carnot efficiency while maintaining finite power output and fluctuations, enabling them to outperform their traditional counterparts.

</details>


### [6] [Critical scaling and supercritical coarsening in Active Model B+](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07247)
*Abir Bhowmick,P. K. Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过二维确定性模拟，分析了活性模型B（AMB）及其扩展版本AMB+的临界动力学和相排序动力学。研究发现两种模型在临界点具有相同的平均场标度行为，而在超临界淬火中，畴尺寸增长呈现对数修正的t^{1/3}规律，且AMB+中活性电流抑制了宏观团簇形成，最终导致微相分离态的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究活性模型B（Active Model B, AMB）及其扩展版本AMB+的临界动力学和相排序动力学，旨在理解非平衡活性系统中的标度行为和生长规律，特别是检验重整化群理论对二维边际活性行为的预测。

Method: 采用二维确定性模拟方法研究AMB和AMB+模型，通过广义等面积构造（generalized equal-area construction）确定AMB+的共存密度和相图，分析临界点和超临界淬火条件下的动力学行为。

Result: 在临界点rc=0时，两种模型均显示相同的平均场标度：序参量随时间衰减为m(t)∼t^{-α}（α=1/4），动力学指数z=4。超临界淬火中，畴尺寸增长遵循L(t)∼t^{1/3}(1+c/lnt)，呈现对数修正；AMB中修正显著，而AMB+中活性电流抑制宏观团簇形成，最终形成长寿命微相分离态。

Conclusion: AMB和AMB+在临界点具有相同的平均场标度行为，但超临界淬火中的生长动力学存在差异：AMB显示显著的对数修正，而AMB+中活性电流抑制宏观团簇形成，导致生长停滞和微相分离态的出现，这与二维边际活性行为的重整化群预测一致。

Abstract: We study critical dynamics and phase-ordering kinetics in Active Model B (AMB) and its minimal extension, Active Model B$+$ (AMB$+$), using deterministic simulations in two dimensions. At criticality $r_c=0$, both models display identical mean-field scaling despite nonequilibrium currents, with order-parameter decay with time as $m(t)\sim t^{-α}$, with $α=\frac14$, and dynamical exponent being $z=4$. A generalized equal-area construction yields the binodal densities and phase diagram of AMB$+$. For supercritical quenches, domain size grows as $L(t)\sim t^{1/3}(1+c/\ln t)$, revealing logarithmic corrections to the classic $t^{1/3}$ growth-law; moreover it is consistent with the functional renormalization group predictions for marginal activity in $d=2$. While the logarithmic corrections are quite prominent in AMB, in AMB$+$ they are suppressed as the active current acts against the formation of macro-clusters; the growth is eventually arrested when a long-lived microphase-separated state appears.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [DYNAMITE: A high-performance framework for solving Dynamical Mean-Field Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06309)
*Johannes Lang,Vincenzo Citro,Luca Leuzzi,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Dynamite框架，这是一个高性能求解器，用于解决无序平均场模型中的动力学平均场方程（DMFE），能够达到前所未有的长时间尺度（t=O(10^7)），相比现有方法实现了数量级的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解复杂崎岖能量景观中系统的动力学在物理学、经济学、生物学和计算机科学中至关重要。无序平均场模型提供了强大框架，但求解动力学平均场方程（DMFE）——一组双时间函数的耦合积分-微分方程——仍然是主要的数值挑战。目前缺乏解决DMFE在非常长时间尺度上的通用方法，限制了复杂景观中慢动力学的研究。

Method: 本文提出Dynamite（DYNAmical Mean-fIeld Time Evolution solver）框架，结合非均匀插值、自适应时间步长和记忆的数值"重整化"（renormalization），实现对历史积分的精确评估。该框架采用自适应Runge-Kutta方案确保稳定性，并通过周期性的过去稀疏化来管理计算复杂度。

Result: Dynamite实现了前所未有的长时间尺度求解（t=O(10^7)），相比均匀网格方法获得了数量级的速度提升，同时在CPU和GPU架构上保持准确性和可重复性。在玻璃态平均场模型（包括混合球形p-自旋系统）上的基准测试表明，该方法能够访问先前无法达到的老化和弛豫区域。

Conclusion: Dynamite框架为研究长记忆动力学系统提供了可重复且可扩展的基础，解决了无序平均场模型中长时间尺度动力学求解的关键瓶颈，使先前无法访问的老化和弛豫区域的研究成为可能。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamics of systems evolving in complex and rugged energy landscapes is central across physics, economics, biology, and computer science. Disordered mean-field models provide a powerful framework, as exact Dynamical Mean-Field Equations (DMFE) can be derived. However, solving the DMFE -- a set of coupled integral-differential equations for two-time functions -- remains a major numerical challenge.
  So far, large-time solutions of DMFE rely either on analytical approaches, such as the Cugliandolo--Kurchan ansatz based on assumptions like weak ergodicity breaking (which is known to fail in some cases), or on numerical integrations that reliably reach times $O(10^3)$ and extend further only via poorly controlled approximations. Consequently, no general method currently exists to solve DMFE at very long times, limiting the study of slow dynamics in complex landscapes.
  We present \textsc{Dynamite} (DYNAmical Mean-fIeld Time Evolution solver), a high-performance framework for solving DMFE up to unprecedented times $t=O(10^7)$. It combines non-uniform interpolation, adaptive time stepping, and numerical `renormalization' of memory, enabling accurate evaluation of history integrals. Its asymptotic runtime is linear, with sublinear memory scaling. Stability and precision are ensured via an adaptive Runge--Kutta scheme and periodic sparsification of the past.
  \textsc{Dynamite} achieves orders-of-magnitude speedups over uniform-grid methods while maintaining accuracy and reproducibility on CPU and GPU architectures. Benchmarks on glassy mean-field models, including the mixed spherical $p$-spin system, demonstrate access to aging and relaxation regimes previously out of reach. The framework provides a reproducible and extensible foundation for studying long-memory dynamical systems.

</details>


### [8] [Disorder averaging in random lattice models with periodic boundary conditions: Application to models with uncorrelated and correlated disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06400)
*Balázs Hetényi,Luís Miguel Martelo,András Lászlóffy*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文开发了在无序系统中应用周期性边界条件时，基于现代极化理论计算极化统计量的方法，包括方差、高阶矩和超值峰度，并提出了基于边界条件简并度的离域化指标，在两个一维无序模型中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无序系统研究中，周期性边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）可用于模拟热力学大系统，但此时无法直接获得极化及其累积量。现代极化理论（modern theory of polarization）将晶体系统中的极化表述为几何相位而非算符期望值，需要在此框架下开发适用于无序系统的计算方法。

Method: 本文在现代极化理论框架内开发了无序平均技术，能够计算极化的方差、高阶矩和超值峰度（excess kurtosis，又称Binder累积量）。同时推导了基于边界条件简并度的离域化指标，并将计算方法应用于两个一维无序模型系统。

Result: 在完全安德森局域化（Anderson localized）的一维无序模型中，计算结果验证了局域化特性。在de Moura-Lyra模型中，方法得到验证，并指出在参数范围α>2且接近能带中心（或接近半填充）时发现的成对简并具有重要意义，该区域被推测存在迁移率边（mobility edge）。

Conclusion: 本文成功开发了适用于无序系统的极化统计量计算方法，并在两个模型系统中得到验证。特别指出de Moura-Lyra模型中发现的成对简并现象对理解迁移率边具有重要意义，表明该方法能够有效分析无序系统中的极化特性和局域化行为。

Abstract: Periodic boundary conditions are not always used in the study of disordered systems, but it can be advantageous to apply them to mimick thermodynamically large systems. In this case, polarization and its cumulants can not be obtained directly, but through the tools of the modern theory of polarization. This theory casts the polarization in crystalline systems as a geometric phase, rather than an operator expectation value. We develop disorder averaging techniques within the context of this theory which can calculate the variance of the polarization, its higher order moments, and the excess kurtosis (or Binder cumulant). We also derive an indicator of delocalization based on the degeneracy as a function of boundary conditions. We apply the computational techniques to two model systems. To test localization, we use a one-dimensional disordered model which is fully Anderson localized. Our calculations verify this. We also apply our techniques to the one dimensional de Moura-Lyra model, developed to study power law correlated (controlled by a parameter, $α$) disorder. While this model is a pathological one, our method is validated. We also point out the significance of pairwise degeneracies found in the parameter range, $α>2$ and near the band center (or near half filling), where the model was conjectured to exhibit a mobility edge.

### [9] [Projector, Neural, and Tensor-Network Representations of $\mathbb{Z}_N$ Cluster and Dipolar-cluster SPT States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06741)
*Seungho Lee,Daesik Kim,Hyun-Yong Lee,Jung Hoon Han*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于P表示（P-representation）和受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machine）的方案，用于高效表达具有$\mathbb{Z}_N \times \mathbb{Z}_N$对称性的$\mathbb{Z}_N$簇态（cluster state）和偶极簇态（dipolar cluster state）波函数，并推导了闭式权重函数，将先前$Z_2$构造推广至$\mathbb{Z}_N$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $\mathbb{Z}_N$簇态波函数作为具有$\mathbb{Z}_N \times \mathbb{Z}_N$对称性的对称保护拓扑（symmetry-protected topological, SPT）序的范例，存在多种等价表达方式。研究旨在识别高效表达簇态和偶极簇态波函数的方法，并将先前$Z_2$构造推广至更一般的$\mathbb{Z}_N$情形。

Method: 采用基于投影算子的P表示（P-representation）作为高效表达方案，并运用受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machine）方案将P表示中的相互作用矩阵重写为神经权重矩阵。由此发展出相同量子态的神经量子态（neural quantum state, NQS）和矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）表示，两者区别仅在于权重矩阵在矩阵乘积中的拆分与组合方式。

Result: 对于$\mathbb{Z}_N$簇态和偶极簇态，推导了连接物理自旋$s$与隐变量$h$的闭式权重函数$W(s,h)$，将先前$Z_2$构造推广至$\mathbb{Z}_N$。对于受两个电荷和两个偶极对称性保护的偶极簇态，所开发方法导出了波函数的张量乘积态（tensor product state, TPS）表示，其中每个局域张量携带三个虚拟指标。通过密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）模拟将所得TPS构造与传统MPS表示进行基准测试，表明TPS可能为某些调制的SPT态提供更高效表示。

Conclusion: 作为研究的副产品，将先前$Z_2$矩阵乘积算子（matrix product operator）构造的Kramers-Wannier（KW）算子推广至$\mathbb{Z}_N$，并将其解释为$\mathbb{Z}_N$变量上离散傅里叶变换的偶极推广。这一新解释自然地说明了KW映射为何是非可逆的。

Abstract: The $\mathbb{Z}_N$ cluster-state wavefunction, a paradigmatic example of symmetry-protected topological (SPT) order with $\mathbb{Z}_N \times \mathbb{Z}_N$ symmetry, is expressed in various equivalent ways. We identify the projector-based scheme called the $P$-representation as the efficient way to express cluster and dipolar cluster state's wavefunctions. Employing the restricted Boltzmann machine scheme to re-write the interaction matrix in the $P$-representation in terms of neural weight matrices allows us to develop the neural quantum state (NQS) and the matrix product state (MPS) representations of the same state. The NQS and MPS representations differ only in the way the weight matrices are split and grouped together in a matrix product. For both $\mathbb{Z}_N$ cluster and dipolar cluster states, we derive in closed form the weight function $W(s,h)$ that couples physical spins $s$ to hidden variables $h$, generalizing the previous construction for $Z_2$ cluster states to $\mathbb{Z}_N$. For the dipolar cluster state protected by two charge and two dipole symmetries, the procedure we have developed leads to the tensor product state (TPS) representation of the wavefunction where each local tensor carries three virtual indices connecting a given site to two nearest neighbors and one further neighbor. We benchmark the resulting TPS construction against conventional MPS representation using density-matrix renormalization group simulations and argue that the TPS could offer a more efficient representation for some modulated SPT states. As a by-product of the investigation, we generalize the previous $Z_2$ matrix product operator construction of the Kramers-Wannier (KW) operator to $\mathbb{Z}_N$ and interprets it as the dipolar generalization of the discrete Fourier transform on $\mathbb{Z}_N$ variables. The new interpretation naturally explains why the KW map is non-invertible.

### [10] [Science of Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition Speed meter (CHRONOS)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06286)
*Yuki Inoue,Hsiang-Yu Huang,Vivek Kumar,Mario Juvenal S. Onglao,Daiki Tanabe,Ta-Chun Yu*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: CHRONOS是一种新型地面引力波探测器概念，旨在填补0.1-10Hz频段的观测空白，通过结合低温扭杆测试质量和萨格纳克干涉仪速度计读数，实现亚赫兹频段的量子非破坏测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 0.1-10Hz频段在引力波天文学中基本未被探索，因为地面探测器受到强烈的地震噪声、牛顿噪声和悬挂热噪声的限制。该频段位于空间探测器（如LISA）和地面干涉仪之间的观测窗口。

Method: CHRONOS结合了低温扭杆测试质量（cryogenic torsion-bar test masses）和三角形萨格纳克干涉仪（triangular Sagnac interferometer），采用速度计读数（speed-meter readout）来抑制量子辐射压力噪声，实现亚赫兹频段的量子非破坏测量（quantum non-demolition measurements）。

Result: 探测器目标是在2Hz附近达到应变灵敏度h ∼ 10⁻¹⁸ Hz⁻¹/²，并在2Hz处探测到Ω_GW ∼ 2×10⁻³的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）。

Conclusion: 该灵敏度在空间探测器和地面干涉仪之间开辟了新的观测窗口，能够观测中等质量黑洞双星、搜索随机引力波背景，并进行宏观量子测量测试。

Abstract: The frequency band between $0.1$ and $10\mathrm{Hz}$ remains largely unexplored in gravitational-wave astronomy due to strong seismic, Newtonian, and suspension thermal noise that limit ground-based detectors. The Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion-bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition Speed meter (CHRONOS) is a novel detector concept designed to access this frequency range from the ground. CHRONOS combines cryogenic torsion-bar test masses with a triangular Sagnac interferometer implementing a speed-meter readout, which suppresses quantum radiation-pressure noise and enables quantum non-demolition measurements in the sub-Hz regime. The detector targets a strain sensitivity of $h \sim 10^{-18}\mathrm{Hz^{-1/2}}$ around $2\mathrm{Hz}$ and stochastic gravitational wave background of $Ω_{GW} \sim 2\times 10^{-3}$ at $2\mathrm{Hz}$. This sensitivity opens a new observational window between space-based detectors such as LISA and ground-based interferometers, enabling observations of intermediate-mass black hole binaries, searches for stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds, and tests of macroscopic quantum measurements.

### [11] [Improving Neutrino Point Source Sensitivity with Source-Informed Event Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06509)
*Jeffrey Lazar,Carlos A. Argüelles,Pavel Zhelnin*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进中微子望远镜（neutrino telescope）事件选择的方法：在重建层级间优先保留与已知候选源方向一致的事件，相比均匀子采样可将点源灵敏度中位数提高约2-3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前中微子望远镜的多级重建链中，事件选择是源无关（source-agnostic）的，未优先考虑来自已知中微子源候选方向的事件。这限制了从已建立的多信使（multi-messenger）目录中识别源的能力。

Method: 提出对层级间事件选择的简单修改：优先保留早期重建结果位于预定义候选源方向角容差（angular tolerance）内的事件，同时以基线速率继续子采样剩余事件。使用具有能量依赖角分辨率（energy-dependent angular resolution）的逼真两级探测器模型进行评估。

Result: 相比均匀子采样（uniform subsampling），这种源知情选择（source-informed selection）可将点源灵敏度（point source sensitivity）中位数提高约2-3倍。改进程度取决于基线选择效率、角容差以及不同层级重建质量间的相关性。对于约100个源的目录，额外计算开销适中（约7-14%）。

Conclusion: 该方法为显著增强当前和未来中微子望远镜的发现潜力提供了一条路径，无需新的探测器能力。通过优先处理候选源方向的事件，可在适度计算开销下实现灵敏度的大幅提升。

Abstract: Neutrino telescopes employ multi-level reconstruction chains, where computationally expensive high-quality reconstructions are applied only to events that survive initial quality cuts based on fast, coarse directional estimates. Currently, event selection between reconstruction levels is source-agnostic, giving no priority to events from directions of known neutrino source candidates. We propose a simple modification to inter-level event selection: preferentially retain events whose early-level reconstruction places them within an angular tolerance of pre-specified candidate source directions from established multi-messenger catalogs, while continuing to subsample remaining events at the baseline rate. Using a realistic two-level detector model with energy-dependent angular resolution, we show that this source-informed selection can improve median point source sensitivity by factors of $\sim 2$--$3$ compared to uniform subsampling, with the improvement depending on the baseline selection efficiency, angular tolerance, and correlation between reconstruction qualities at different levels. For catalogs of $\mathcal{O}(100)$ sources, the additional computational overhead is modest ($\sim 7$--$14\%$). This approach offers a path to substantially enhance the discovery potential of current and future neutrino telescopes without requiring new detector capabilities.

</details>


### [12] [Biases in the Determination of Correlations Between Underground Muon Flux and Atmospheric Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06704)
*Bangzheng Ma,Katherine Dugas,Kam-Biu Luk,Juan Pedro Ochoa-Ricoux,Bedřich Roskovec,Qun Wu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究比较了分析地下宇宙μ子（cosmic muon）季节性变化与大气温度相关性的两种方法：无分箱法（Unbinned Method）和分箱法（Binned Method）。研究发现，在温度不确定性存在时，分箱法会产生显著偏差，而无分箱法在准确已知不确定性时保持稳健。为解决不确定性估计不精确的常见问题，作者提出了一种通过变化数据时间间隔和分配不确定性来评估相关性稳定性的新程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地下宇宙μ子（cosmic muon）速率表现出与大气温度相关的季节性变化，通常通过单一系数进行量化。研究旨在比较分析这种相关性的两种方法：标准无分箱法（Unbinned Method）和较少使用的分箱法（Binned Method），以解决μ子季节性调制研究中存在的方法论张力。

Method: 研究比较了两种分析方法：标准无分箱法（Unbinned Method）和分箱法（Binned Method）。针对不确定性估计不精确的常见问题，作者提出了一种新颖的程序，通过变化数据时间间隔和分配的不确定性来评估相关性稳定性。

Result: 研究发现，在假设完美温度知识的情况下，两种方法都是无偏的。然而，当存在温度不确定性时，分箱法（Binned Method）由于分箱引起的扭曲会产生显著偏差。相比之下，如果不确定性被准确已知，无分箱法（Unbinned Method）保持稳健。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了μ子季节性调制研究中的方法论张力，并为现实条件下稳健的相关性估计提供了一个实用框架。提出的新程序能够评估相关性稳定性，为处理不确定性估计不精确的常见问题提供了解决方案。

Abstract: Underground cosmic muon rates exhibit seasonal variations correlated with atmospheric temperature, quantified via a single coefficient. We compare two analysis methods: the standard Unbinned Method and the less common Binned Method. We find that while both methods are unbiased assuming perfect knowledge of the temperature, the Binned Method develops significant bias when temperature uncertainties are present, due to binning-induced distortions. In contrast, the Unbinned Method remains robust if uncertainties are accurately known. To address the common issue of imprecise uncertainty estimates, we propose a novel procedure that assesses correlation stability by varying data time intervals and assigned uncertainties. This resolves methodological tensions in muon seasonal modulation studies and provides a practical framework for robust correlation estimation under real-world conditions.

### [13] [Towards foundation-style models for energy-frontier heterogeneous neutrino detectors via self-supervised pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07037)
*Saúl Alonso-Monsalve,Fabio Cufino,Umut Kose,Anna Mascellani,André Rubbia*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种稀疏视觉Transformer框架，通过自监督预训练从异构探测器数据中学习可重用表征，显著提升了中微子物理分析中粒子识别、动量回归和顶点重建等任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于加速器的中微子物理正进入能量前沿领域，其中相互作用达到TeV尺度并产生异常密集、重叠的探测器信号。在此领域，传统重建方法的事件解释变得不切实际，特别是在标记数据稀缺且分析涉及多样化下游目标时。

Method: 提出了一种稀疏视觉Transformer（ViT）框架，用于从异构探测器数据中学习可重用表征。自监督预训练结合了掩码自编码器重建与关系体素级目标，用于层次结构、幽灵粒子和粒子识别。得到的共享编码器随后在分类和回归任务上进行联合微调。

Result: 在LHC提出的FASERCal概念模拟事件上评估发现，预训练相比从头训练持续改善了中微子味道（flavour）和粲夸克识别、动量回归和顶点重建性能，关系目标的加入在拓扑最复杂的通道中带来进一步增益。可解释性分析显示预训练产生了更结构化的潜在空间。

Conclusion: 数据效率研究表明，使用约10^3个标记事件，预训练编码器已能达到随机初始化模型使用一个数量级更多数据训练的味道分类性能。学习到的表征还能有效迁移到不同探测器技术和能量尺度的公开基准测试中，匹配或超过已发表的基线。这些结果支持在异构探测器数据上进行自监督预训练作为中微子和粒子探测器分析中可重用表征的可扩展途径。

Abstract: Accelerator-based neutrino physics is entering an energy-frontier regime in which interactions reach the TeV scale and produce exceptionally dense, overlapping detector signatures. In this regime, event interpretation becomes impractical for conventional reconstruction approaches, particularly when labelled data are scarce and the analysis spans diverse downstream objectives. We present a sparse ViT framework for learning reusable representations from heterogeneous detector data. Self-supervised pre-training combines masked autoencoder reconstruction with relational voxel-level objectives for hierarchy, ghost and particle identification, and the resulting shared encoder is then jointly fine-tuned across classification and regression tasks. Evaluated on simulated events from the proposed FASERCal concept at the LHC, we find that pre-training consistently improves neutrino flavour and charm-quark identification, momentum regression, and vertex reconstruction over training from scratch, with the addition of relational objectives yielding further gains in the most topologically complex channels. Interpretability analyses further show that pre-training yields a more structured latent space, while detector-subsystem ablations recover physically plausible channel-dependent roles for the heterogeneous inputs. A data-efficiency study shows that, with roughly $10^3$ labelled events, the pre-trained encoder already matches the flavour-classification performance of a randomly initialised model trained on an order of magnitude more data. The learned representations also transfer effectively to publicly available benchmarks spanning different detector technologies and energy scales, matching or exceeding published baselines. These results support self-supervised pre-training on multimodal detector data as a scalable route towards reusable representations for neutrino and particle-detector analysis.

### [14] [Measurement of Inclusive Charged-Current $\barν_μ$ Scattering on C, CH, Fe, and Pb at $\langle E_{\barν}\rangle \sim$ 6 GeV with MINERvA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07091)
*A. Klustová,S. Akhter,Z. Ahmad Dar,M. Sajjad Athar,G. Caceres,H. da Motta,J. Felix,P. K. Gaur,R. Gran,E. Granados,D. A. Harris,A. L. Hart,J. Kleykamp,M. Kordosky,D. Last,A. Lozano,S. Manly,W. A. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在测量不同核靶上的反μ子中微子包含性带电流截面，以探测从共振产生到深度非弹性散射的所有相互作用模式。通过比较不同核靶的截面比值，可以研究核效应对中微子相互作用的影响。

Method: 使用平均能量约6 GeV的宽能带反μ子中微子束流，测量碳、碳氢化合物、铁和铅靶上的包含性带电流截面。测量结果以反μ子横向动量（$p_{\mathrm{T}}$）的函数形式呈现，并与多个中微子相互作用模型进行比较。

Result: 绝对截面的总不确定度通常为5-10%，截面比值的总不确定度为2-5%。与多个中微子相互作用模型的比较显示，在$p_{\mathrm{T}}$依赖性方面存在显著差异，特别是对于较重核靶。差异在低$p_{\mathrm{T}}$区域最为明显，但贯穿整个$p_{\mathrm{T}}$范围。

Conclusion: 测量结果揭示了现有中微子相互作用模型在描述核效应方面的不足，特别是在$p_{\mathrm{T}}$依赖性方面存在缺失或错误建模的核效应。这些差异表明需要改进对核环境中中微子相互作用的理解和建模。

Abstract: We report MINERvA's first measurement of inclusive charged-current $\barν_μ$ cross sections on carbon, hydrocarbon, iron, and lead, and their ratios to the cross section on hydrocarbon, as functions of the antimuon transverse momentum, $p_{\mathrm{T}}$. Using a wide-band $\barν_μ$ beam with mean energy $\sim 6~\text{GeV}$, these measurements probe all interaction modes, including the transition from resonance production to deep-inelastic scattering. The total uncertainties are typically $5-10\%$ for the absolute cross sections and $2-5\%$ for the ratios. Comparisons with multiple neutrino interaction models reveal significant discrepancies in the $p_{\mathrm{T}}$ dependence, particularly for heavier nuclei. The disagreements are most pronounced at low $p_{\mathrm{T}}$ but extend across the full $p_{\mathrm{T}}$ range, indicating missing or mis-modelled nuclear effects.

</details>

### [15] [Joint Curvature and Growth Rate measurements with Supernova Peculiar Velocities and the CMB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06361)
*Camilo Crisman,Miguel Quartin,João Rebouças*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用Ia型超新星（SN）的视星等相关性，结合宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据，同时约束宇宙学参数σ₈、生长指数γ和曲率Ωₖ。结果显示SN与CMB数据高度互补，并发现可能存在正曲率的迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ia型超新星（SN）的视星等存在相关性，这是因为它们的本动速度（peculiar velocities）源于宇宙的大尺度结构。这一效应可用于约束与物质扰动分布和生长相关的性质。

Method: 分析Pantheon+和暗能量巡天（DES-Y5）超新星目录，结合普朗克PR4的宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据，在ΛCDM框架下约束σ₈，可选地包含曲率Ωₖ和修正的生长指数γ。

Result: SN与CMB数据集高度互补，能够同时测量σ₈、γ和Ωₖ。发现可能存在正曲率的迹象：Ωₖ = -0.011±0.006（Pantheon+）和-0.014±0.005（DES-Y5），在2.2σ和3.0σ水平上排除平坦性。生长指数γ与广义相对论预测一致。

Conclusion: Ωₖ、γ和H₀之间的强简并性导致CMB的H₀后验分布更宽。若加入SH0ES的H₀数据（在平坦ΛCDM中与CMB存在显著张力），则H₀张力被重新解释为显著负曲率和结构生长的抑制。

Abstract: Type Ia supernova (SN) magnitudes present correlations due to the fact that their peculiar velocities are sourced by the large-scale structure of the Universe. This effect can be used to constrain properties related to the distribution and growth of matter perturbations. We analyze both Pantheon+ and Dark Energy Survey (DES-Y5) SN catalogues in combination with CMB data from Planck PR4 to constrain $σ_8$ in $Λ$CDM, optionally including both curvature and a modified growth index $γ$. We show that SN and CMB datasets are highly complementary and capable of measuring $σ_8$, $γ$ and $Ω_k$ simultaneously. Using only SN, we find $σ_8 = 0.73 \pm 0.22$ ($0.87 \pm 0.31$) for Pantheon+ (DES-Y5) in the base flat $Λ$CDM model. Interestingly, allowing for free $γ$ and $Ω_k$, we find hints of positive curvature: $Ω_k = -0.011 \pm 0.006$ $(-0.014 \pm 0.005)$, which exclude flatness at 2.2$σ$ (3.0$σ$), for the combination of CMB with Pantheon+ (DES-Y5). Such hints do not degrade if we also include a modified amplitude of CMB lensing, parametrized by $A_L$. We find that $γ= 0.519^{+0.061}_{-0.099}$ ($0.461^{+0.085}_{-0.069}$), which are consistent with the predictions of General Relativity. In terms of $fσ_8(z)$, we find $fσ_8(0.024)=0.461^{+0.066}_{-0.035}$ ($fσ_8(0.038) = 0.498^{+0.045}_{-0.050}$) for CMB + Pantheon+ (DES-Y5). Finally, the strong degeneracy between all three $Ω_k$, $γ$ and $H_0$ results in a broader CMB $H_0$ posterior. However, if we include SH0ES $H_0$ data, which is in known strong tension with the CMB in flat $Λ$CDM, we find that the $H_0$ tension is recast in terms of a significantly negative curvature and suppressed growth of structures.

### [16] [Cosmological Dynamics of Exponential Quintessence Constrained by BAO, Cosmic Chronometers, and DES-SN5YR/Pantheon+ Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06941)
*Sanjeeda Sultana,Surajit Chattopadhyay*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文对指数势驱动的典型quintessence模型进行了全面的观测检验。该模型在高维理论、弦论启发的场景和修正引力中自然出现。研究使用最新高精度观测数据约束模型参数，发现其与ΛCDM基准线高度一致，且在统计上与ΛCDM可比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指数势quintessence模型因其在高维理论、弦论启发的场景和修正引力中的自然出现而具有理论动机。研究旨在通过最新观测数据对这一典型模型进行全面的观测检验，评估其与标准宇宙学模型的兼容性。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）框架，结合最新的高精度观测数据集进行参数约束，包括宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）、重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation）、Pantheon+和DES-SN5YR Ia型超新星数据。

Result: 组合数据显著收紧了对(H0, Omega_m0, eta0, gamma)参数的约束。模型对哈勃参数H(z)、距离模数mu(z)和标度化共动角直径距离的预测与观测高度一致，且紧密跟随ΛCDM基准线。状态诊断器（statefinder diagnostics）显示轨迹接近ΛCDM固定点，能量条件分析确认物理可行性。

Conclusion: 基于赤池信息准则（Akaike Information Criterion）的信息论模型比较表明，尽管指数quintessence模型具有额外参数，但在统计上与ΛCDM可比。模型成功再现了从物质主导到晚期加速的转变，保持w_tot > -1，并提供与Planck 2018一致的宇宙年龄。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive observational test of a canonical quintessence model driven by an exponential potential, motivated by its emergence in higher-dimensional theories, string-inspired scenarios, and modified gravity. Using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo framework, we constrain the model with the latest high-precision observational datasets including Cosmic Chronometers, Baryon Acoustic Oscillation, Pantheon+, and DES-SN5YR Type Ia Supernovae. The combined data significantly tighten the parameter bounds on (H0, Omega_m0, eta0, gamma) and yield predictions for the Hubble parameter H(z), the distance modulus mu(z), and the scaled comoving angular diameter distance that remain in excellent agreement with observations and closely follow the LCDM baseline. An information-theoretic model comparison using the Akaike Information Criterion shows that the exponential quintessence model remains statistically comparable with LCDM despite having additional parameters. The model successfully reproduces the transition from matter domination to late-time acceleration, maintains w_tot > -1, and provides an age of the universe consistent with Planck 2018. Statefinder diagnostics indicate trajectories approaching the LCDM fixed point with small deviations, and energy condition analysis confirms physical viability, with only the Strong Energy Condition violated at late times as required for acceleration.

</details>


### [17] [Observational Tests for Distinguishing Classes of Cosmological Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07244)
*Asta Heinesen,Timothy Clifton*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种区分不同宇宙学模型的观测测试方法，通过弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（FLRW）模型的曲率一致性检验，识别违反FLRW假设的两种情景，并开发新的零检验来隔离具有非FLRW观测关系的宇宙学模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着文献中宇宙学模型提案数量的增加，需要有效方法来区分不同模型以解释宇宙学中的张力、异常和暗物质问题。本文旨在提供清晰的途径来区分这些不同提案，利用精确宇宙学数据高效区分宇宙学模型。

Method: 采用弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（FLRW）模型的曲率一致性检验（curvature-consistency tests），研究其在两种情景下被违反的情况：一是宇宙学的光学性质偏离FLRW预期，二是宇宙学的大尺度膨胀与FLRW不同。提出新的零检验（null test）来隔离具有非FLRW观测关系的宇宙学模型。

Result: 识别了通过违反曲率一致性检验来确定这些替代情景性质的有用方法。发现的特征性签名可与近期和未来宇宙学观测结果结合使用，以探测和/或排除大量宇宙学模型类别。

Conclusion: 该方法为区分不同宇宙学模型提案提供了清晰路径，并提供了利用精确宇宙学数据高效区分宇宙学模型的新机会。随着宇宙学家试图解释宇宙学中的张力、异常和暗物质问题，这项工作变得越来越重要。

Abstract: We investigate observational tests that can be used to distinguish between broad classes of cosmological models. This is achieved using curvature-consistency tests of the Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) models, which we investigate in two scenarios where they can be violated; (i) when the optical properties of the cosmology deviate from the expectations of FLRW, and also (ii) when the large-scale expansion of the cosmology is different from FLRW. We identify useful ways to determine the properties of these alternative scenarios in terms of the violation of the curvature-consistency tests, and propose a new null test that can be used to isolate cosmologies with non-FLRW observational relations. The characteristic signatures we find can be used, together with the results of recent and upcoming cosmological observations, to probe and/or rule out large classes of cosmological models. This becomes an increasingly important task as the number of proposals in the literature increases, as cosmologists attempt to explain tensions, anomalies, and the dark sector of the Universe. Our approach provides a clear route for telling apart these different proposals, and offers a new opportunity for using precision cosmological data to efficiently discriminate between cosmological models.

### [18] [Crystallization in the Fractional Quantum Hall Regime with Disorder-Aware Neural Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06316)
*Jihang Zhu,Yi Huang,Xiaodong Hu,Di Xiao,Ting Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究首次在微观层面展示了无序钉扎的空穴维格纳晶体（hole Wigner crystal），为ν=2/3附近观察到的重入整数量子霍尔效应及其在分数量子陈绝缘体中的类似现象提供了自然解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释在填充因子ν=2/3附近观察到的重入整数量子霍尔效应（reentrant integer quantum Hall effect）及其在分数量子陈绝缘体中的类似现象，并探索跨越半填充的基本结晶不对称性。

Method: 采用神经网络变分蒙特卡洛方法（neural-network variational Monte Carlo, NNVMC），结合无序感知的自注意力神经量子态（disorder-aware self-attention neural quantum state），在单一无偏变分框架内同时描述分数量子霍尔液体和维格纳晶体。

Result: 首次微观演示了无序钉扎的空穴维格纳晶体，并在ν=2/3以上填充发现了一个新的交叉区域，该区域将空穴维格纳晶体与电子维格纳晶体连接起来，其特征是网络状电子密度结构。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了一个统一的相图，揭示了跨越半填充的基本结晶不对称性：在ν=1/3附近，增加朗道能级混合（LL mixing）和无序都会稳定电子维格纳晶体；而在ν=2/3附近，空穴维格纳晶体在弱朗道能级混合下占主导，最终在强朗道能级混合下让位于电子维格纳晶体。

Abstract: We present the first microscopic demonstration of a disorder-pinned hole Wigner crystal (WC), providing a natural explanation for the reentrant integer quantum Hall effect observed near $ν=2/3$, as well as its analogs in fractional Chern insulators. We further identify a novel crossover regime above filling $ν=2/3$ that connects this hole WC to an electron WC, characterized by a network-like electron density structure. To uncover these phenomena, we use neural-network variational Monte Carlo (NNVMC) with a disorder-aware self-attention neural quantum state that describes both fractional quantum Hall (FQH) liquids and Wigner crystals within a single unbiased variational framework. More broadly, our method establishes a unified phase diagram that exposes a fundamental asymmetry in crystallization across half-filling: near $ν=1/3$, increasing LL mixing and disorder both stabilize an electron WC, whereas near $ν=2/3$, the hole WC dominates at weak LL mixing and ultimately gives way to the electron WC at strong LL mixing.

### [19] [Topochemically-engineered coexistence of charge and spin orders in intercalated endotaxial heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06453)
*Samra Husremović,Wanlin Zhang,Medha Dandu,Berit H. Goodge,Isaac M. Craig,Ellis Kennedy,Matthew P. Erodici,Karen C. Bustillo,Chengyu Song,Jim Ciston,Sinéad Griffin,Archana Raja,D. Kwabena Bediako*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过纳米尺度亚稳态插层异质结构，在单一材料中实现了长程磁性与室温下稳定的公度电荷密度波（C-CDW）的罕见共存，为调控二维材料中的竞争量子相提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相关电子系统中多种电子序的竞争通常阻碍其共存，限制了多功能量子材料的发展。本研究旨在探索稳定磁性（magnetism）与电荷密度波（charge density wave）等竞争量子相共存的策略。

Method: 合成了二维亚稳晶体T/H-Fe$_x$TaS2，这是一种由1T-TaS$_2$和H-TaS$_2$组成的插层异质结构（intercalated heterostructure），其中Fe插层在范德华界面（van der Waals interfaces）中。通过拓扑化学方法（topochemical preparation）制备这种插层异质结构。

Result: 在T/H-Fe$_x$TaS2中，Fe插层提供了局域自旋，支持铁磁性（ferromagnetism）；同时1T层容纳了稳健的公度电荷密度波（C-CDW），该电荷密度波可维持至室温。Fe含量可同时调控自旋和电荷自由度的有序化。

Conclusion: 拓扑化学制备的插层异质结构可作为稳定和控制二维材料中竞争量子相的有效途径，为多功能量子材料设计提供了新策略。

Abstract: Correlated electron systems that host multiple electronic orders offer routes to multifunctional quantum materials, but strong competition between these orders often prevents their coexistence. Here we show that nanoscale, metastable intercalated heterostructures can stabilize a rare combination of long-range magnetism and a commensurate charge density wave (C-CDW) order in a single material. We synthesize a two-dimensional (2D) metastable crystal, T/H-Fe$_x$TaS2, which comprises an endotaxial polytype heterostructure of 1T-TaS$_2$ and H-TaS$_2$ with Fe intercalated in the van der Waals interfaces. In T/H-Fe$_x$TaS2, Fe intercalants provide localized spins that support ferromagnetism, while 1T layers host a robust commensurate charge density wave (C-CDW) that persists to room temperature. In these intercalated heterostructures, Fe content simultaneously tunes ordering of spin and charge degrees of freedom, positioning topochemically-prepared intercalated endotaxial heterostructures as a route to stabilize and control competing quantum phases in 2D materials.

### [20] [Floquet X-Ray Scattering as a Probe of Hidden Electronic Orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06496)
*Martin Eckstein,Eva Paprotzki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文开发了Floquet共振X射线散射的理论框架，结合Floquet理论和超短核空穴寿命展开，获得了散射算符的Floquet分量的紧凑表达式，证明该方法可直接探测传统衍射中不产生电荷布拉格峰的键和电流关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统X射线衍射技术难以探测不产生电荷布拉格峰的隐藏电子序或涨落，如键序和电流关联。需要发展新的理论框架来利用Floquet共振X射线散射作为对称性分辨的探针。

Method: 结合Floquet理论和超短核空穴寿命展开（ultrashort core-hole lifetime expansion），推导出共振非弹性X射线散射算符的Floquet分量紧凑表达式。将该框架应用于Kagome晶格上的电荷有序态。

Result: 不同对称破缺序在Floquet布拉格峰中表现出独特的偏振指纹。通过驱动频率可调控键和电流贡献的相对权重。Floquet X射线散射可直接探测传统衍射中不产生电荷布拉格峰的键和电流关联。

Conclusion: Floquet X射线散射可作为量子材料中隐藏电子序或涨落的对称性分辨探针，为探测传统衍射技术难以观测的键序和电流关联提供了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework for Floquet resonant X-ray scattering, using Floquet theory combined with the ultrashort core-hole lifetime expansion. We obtain a compact expression for the Floquet components of the resonant inelastic X-ray scattering operator, which shows that Floquet X-ray scattering provides direct access to bond and current correlations that do not directly produce charge Bragg peaks in conventional diffraction. Applying this framework to charge-ordered states on the Kagome lattice, we demonstrate that different symmetry-breaking orders exhibit distinct polarization fingerprints in the Floquet Bragg peaks. Moreover, the relative weight of bond and current contributions can be tuned through the drive frequency. These results establish Floquet X-ray scattering as a symmetry-resolved probe of hidden electronic order or fluctuations in quantum materials.

</details>


### [21] [Decomposing momentum scales in the Hubbard Model: From Hatsugai-Kohmoto to Aubry-André](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06588)
*Dmitry Manning-Coe,Barry Bradlyn*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种动量空间聚类方案，通过保留选定的相互作用通道来简化Hubbard模型的计算，特别适用于Moiré系统等低能物理由少数特征波矢主导的场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hubbard相互作用的全对全动量耦合使得相互作用晶格模型通常不可解。然而在许多物理场景中，从Peierls不稳定性到Moiré超晶格物理，低能行为主要由少数特征波矢的散射主导。

Method: 构建动量空间聚类方案，仅保留选定的相互作用通道。该方案可视为扭曲平均边界条件的推广，也是Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型的推广。当空间变化势选择主导动量通道时，该方案特别有效。

Result: 在相互作用Moiré系统的一维类比——Aubry-André-Hubbard模型中，对于足够强的在位势，小至两个位点的聚类可将基态能量误差降至DMRG基准的1%以下。新引入的"动量混合HK模型"对应特定的聚类极限。

Conclusion: 物理驱动的动量空间截断能以可行的计算成本提供准确的低能描述，为二维Moiré系统的可处理相互作用模型开辟了路径。HK模型的成功现象学源于其与有限位点Hubbard模型的对应关系。

Abstract: The all-to-all momentum coupling of the Hubbard interaction makes interacting lattice models generically unsolvable. In many settings, however, from Peierls instabilities to Moiré superlattice physics, the low-energy behavior is dominated by scattering at a few characteristic wavevectors. We exploit this by constructing a momentum-space clustering scheme that retains only a chosen subset of interaction channels. Our scheme can be considered a generalization of twist-averaged boundary conditions. In proving this, we also prove that our scheme can be considered as a generalization of Hatsugai-Kohmoto (HK) models, and all versions of the HK model previously considered in the literature arise as special cases. This shows that the surprising phenomenological success of HK models arises from their correspondence to the finite-site Hubbard model. In particular, the recently introduced "Momentum-Mixing HK" model corresponds to a specific choice of clustering limit, which is equal to the original finite-site Hubbard model with twist-averaged boundary conditions. Our scheme becomes particularly powerful when a spatially varying potential selects the dominant momentum channels. We demonstrate this on the one-dimensional analogue of interacting moiré systems: the Aubry-André-Hubbard model. We show that for sufficiently strong onsite potential, clusters as small as two sites can recover the ground state energy to below 1% error relative to DMRG benchmarks. This establishes that physically motivated momentum-space truncations can yield accurate low-energy descriptions at feasible computational cost, opening a path toward tractable interacting models of Moiré systems in two dimensions. Code for reproducing all numerical results is available at https://github.com/chainik1125/decomposing-hubbard.

</details>


### [22] [Investigating the intrinsic anomalous Hall effect in MnPt3 topological semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06619)
*Jing Meng,Hongru Wang,Kun Zheng,Yuhao Wang,Zheng Li,Bocheng Yu,Haoyu Lin,Keqi Xia,Jingzhong Luo,Zengyao Wang,Xiaoyan Zhu,Baiqing Lv,Yaobo Huang,Jie Ma,Yang Xu,Shijing Gong,Tian Shang,Qingfeng Zhan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁控溅射制备了不同厚度的MnPt₃薄膜，系统研究了其反常霍尔效应（AHE），发现内禀贝里曲率机制主导了反常霍尔电导（AHC），且应变效应增强了内禀AHC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 立方Cu₃Au型XPt₃家族（X = V, Cr, Mn）是具有反交叉能隙节线（anti-crossing gapped nodal lines）的拓扑半金属，可产生显著的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和反常霍尔效应（AHE）。虽然CrPt₃已被实验证实具有大的反常霍尔电导（AHC），但MnPt₃和VPt₃的研究仍不充分。

Method: 采用磁控溅射（magnetron sputtering）在MgO衬底上外延生长了厚度为20-70 nm的MnPt₃薄膜系列，并通过磁化、电阻率和霍尔电阻率测量进行了系统研究。

Result: MnPt₃薄膜在居里温度（Curie temperature）T_C处发生铁磁转变，且T_C随膜厚增加而升高，70 nm薄膜的T_C达到~344 K。反常霍尔输运性质（电阻率、电导率和角度）均与磁性密切相关。标度分析（scaling analysis）表明内禀贝里曲率机制主导了观测到的AHE，而外禀贡献很小。内禀AHC随膜厚增加而增加，外禀AHC与厚度无关。

Conclusion: MnPt₃薄膜中增强的内禀AHC很可能归因于应变效应（strain effect），这表明应变可作为调控XPt₃拓扑半金属电子能带拓扑的有效方法。

Abstract: The cubic Cu$_3$Au-type $X$Pt$_3$ family ($X$ = V, Cr, and Mn) is a topological semimetal characterized by anti-crossing gapped nodal lines near the Fermi level, which give rise to significant Berry curvatures and thus to the anomalous Hall effect (AHE). Among the three members, CrPt$_3$ has been experimentally verified to exhibit a large anomalous Hall conductivity (AHC), while its counterparts MnPt$_3$ and VPt$_3$ remain largely unexplored. Here, a series of MnPt$_3$ thin films with varying thicknesses (20--70 nm) was epitaxially grown on the MgO substrates using magnetron sputtering and was systematically investigated by magnetization, electrical resistivity, and Hall resistivity measurements. MnPt$_3$ films undergo a ferromagnetic transition at a Curie temperature $T_\mathrm{C}$, which increases as the film thickness increases, reaching $\sim$ 344 K for the 70-nm-thick film. All the anomalous Hall transport properties of MnPt$_3$ films, including the resistivity, conductivity, and angle, exhibit a strong correlation with their magnetic properties. The scaling analysis suggests that the intrinsic Berry-curvature mechanism dominates the observed AHE, while the extrinsic contributions are much smaller. The intrinsic AHC increases as the film thickness increases, while the extrinsic AHC is thickness-independent. Such an enhanced intrinsic AHC in the MnPt$_3$ films is most likely attributed to the strain effect, implying that it serves as an effective method to tune the electronic band topology in the $X$Pt$_3$ topological semimetal.

</details>


### [23] [Magnon harmonic generation in antiferromagnets: Dynamical symmetry enriched by symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06700)
*Yuto Jita,Minoru Kanega,Takumi Ogawa,Shunsuke C. Furuya,Masahiro Sato*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值和理论方法，分析了太赫兹激光或千兆赫波驱动的反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）谐波产生（harmonic generation）现象，发现磁序和相变会改变谐波光谱，且这些光谱能提供关于反铁磁体对称性或对称性破缺的新信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，强太赫兹激光技术使得实验观测反铁磁体中的非线性自旋动力学成为可能，因为磁振子（magnons）等元激发位于太赫兹到千兆赫范围，太赫兹激光可以直接激发它们。研究旨在探索反铁磁体典型有序相中的谐波产生现象。

Method: 采用数值和理论方法，研究太赫兹激光或千兆赫波驱动的反铁磁体谐波产生，包括奈尔相（Néel phase）、倾斜相（canted phase）和弱铁磁相（weak ferromagnetic phase）。分析由入射波驱动的磁振子动力学产生的辐射波（谐波产生）。

Result: 研究发现磁序和相变会改变谐波产生光谱，这与没有（自发）对称性破缺的金属、半导体或原子气体系统不同。在反铁磁体中，单色激光和双色激光驱动的磁振子谐波产生都表现出多种动力学对称性及相应的选择规则。

Conclusion: 磁振子谐波产生光谱能够提供关于反铁磁体对称性或对称性破缺的新信息，表明该技术可作为研究反铁磁体磁序和相变的有效手段。

Abstract: In recent years, techniques of intense THz laser have enabled us to experimentally observe nonlinear spin dynamics in antiferromagnets since the elementary excitations such as magnons reside on a THz to GHz range in antiferromagnets and THz laser thus can directly excite them. We numerically and theoretically investigate THz-laser or GHz-wave driven harmonic generations in typical ordered phases of antiferromagnets: Néel, canted and weak ferromagnetic phases. The radiation waves (harmonic generations) are created by the incident-wave driven magnon dynamics. We point out that magnetic orders and phase transitions can change the spectra of harmonic generations, differently from those of metallic, semiconductor, or atomic-gas systems without (spontaneous) symmetry breakings. We consider both the magnon harmonic generation driven by standard single-color laser and that by two-color laser in the antiferromagnets, and find several dynamical symmetries and the corresponding selection rules of the harmonic generations. These results indicate that the magnon harmonic generation spectra provide new information about symmetry or symmetry breaking of antiferromagnets.

</details>


### [24] [Magnetic-field switching of exciton-magnon coupling in LiNiPO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06785)
*Bei Sun,Zhuo Yang,Julian Shibuya,Koichi Kindo,Kenta Kimura,Atsuhiko Miyata*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子-磁振子跃迁（exciton-magnon transitions）是反铁磁体中耦合激子和磁激发的光学指纹，但通过外场控制此类耦合激发仍是一个关键挑战。研究旨在探索磁电反铁磁体LiNiPO₄中激子-磁振子耦合的外部场调控机制。

Method: 采用高达50T的脉冲磁场，系统研究了LiNiPO₄中激子-磁振子耦合的温度和磁场演化。通过分析磁振子边带（magnon sideband）强度在不同磁场条件下的变化，探究耦合行为的调控机制。

Result: 磁振子边带强度在磁场诱导的磁相中表现出急剧切换行为：在平台相（plateau phases）中强烈抑制，而在倾斜自旋态（canted spin states）中显著增强。这种行为归因于热磁振子布居（thermal magnon population）与自旋依赖的光学跃迁矩阵元（spin-dependent optical transition matrix element）之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过磁场对自旋自由度的控制，能够实现反铁磁体中激子-磁振子耦合的选择性切换（selective switching），为外场调控耦合激发提供了新途径。

Abstract: Exciton-magnon transitions provide a fundamental optical fingerprint of coupled excitonic and magnetic excitations in antiferromagnets. However, controlling such coupled excitations by external fields remains a key challenge. Here we report the temperature and magnetic-field evolution of exciton-magnon coupling in the magnetoelectric antiferromagnet LiNiPO$_4$ using pulsed magnetic fields up to 50 T. The magnon sideband intensity exhibits sharp switching across field-induced magnetic phases, with strong suppression in plateau phases and enhancement in canted spin states. This behavior is attributed to the interplay between the thermal magnon population and the spin-dependent optical transition matrix element. These results demonstrate that magnetic-field control of spin degrees of freedom enables selective switching of exciton-magnon coupling in antiferromagnets.

### [25] [Proximate quantum spin liquid state in the frustrated HoInCu$_4$ metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06867)
*I. Ishant,T. Shiroka,O. Stockert,V. Fritsch,M. Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过μ子自旋弛豫/旋转（μSR）技术对比分析了HoCdCu₄和HoInCu₄两种面心立方金属化合物，发现HoInCu₄中存在强磁挫败，仅30%的Ho磁矩参与静态磁有序，其余70%表现出类似量子自旋液体的动力学行为，表明其基态为邻近量子自旋液体态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在阐明HoCdCu₄和HoInCu₄两种fcc晶格金属化合物的磁性基态性质，并探究磁挫败（magnetic frustration）在稳定这些基态中的作用。通过对比分析，揭示不同化合物中磁有序行为的差异及其物理机制。

Method: 采用综合对比性的μ子自旋弛豫和旋转（muon-spin relaxation and rotation, μSR）技术对两种化合物进行系统研究。该方法能够探测磁性系统的静态和动态特性，特别是对磁有序和自旋动力学的敏感性分析。

Result: μSR结果显示，HoInCu₄中存在强磁挫败，仅30%的Ho磁矩参与低于T_N的静态磁有序，而70%的Ho磁矩表现出动态关联和持续的自旋动力学，类似量子自旋液体行为。此外，在顺磁态近T_N处观察到量子临界涨落，表明接近量子临界点。相比之下，HoCdCu₄中所有Ho磁矩都参与磁有序。

Conclusion: HoInCu₄的基态被确定为邻近量子自旋液体态，这是在受挫金属系统中首次报道的状态。该结论得到最近非弹性中子散射结果的进一步支持，这些结果与其他绝缘性邻近量子自旋液体候选材料相似，从而强化了研究结论。

Abstract: We conducted a comprehensive and comparative muon-spin relaxation and rotation ($μ$SR) investigation on two fcc-lattice metallic compounds, HoCdCu$_4$ ($T_\mathrm{N}\approx 8$ K) and HoInCu$_4$ ($T_\mathrm{N}\approx 0.76$ K), to elucidate the nature of their magnetic ground states and the role of frustration in stabilizing them. Our $μ$SR results reveal that, in contrast to HoCdCu$_4$, strong magnetic frustration exists in HoInCu$_4$. Notably, in HoInCu$_{4}$, only 30% of the Ho-moments participate in the static magnetic ordering below $T_\mathrm{N}$, while the remaining 70% of the Ho-moments exhibit dynamic correlations and persistent spin dynamics down to 0.3 K, resembling a quantum spin-liquid (QSL) behavior. By contrast, in HoCdCu$_{4}$, all the Ho-moments contribute to the magnetic order below $T_\mathrm{N}$. Furthermore, in HoInCu$_{4}$, the temperature dependence of the relaxation rate indicates the presence of quantum critical fluctuations in the paramagnetic state near $T_\mathrm{N}$, suggesting the proximity to a quantum critical point (QCP). These observations suggest that the ground state of HoInCu$_{4}$ is a proximate quantum spin liquid (PQSL), a state that has not been reported before in frustrated metallic systems. Our $μ$SR findings are further corroborated by recent inelastic neutron results on HoInCu$_4$, which show similarities to other insulating PQSL candidates, thus reinforcing our conclusions.

</details>


### [26] [Between Mott and cluster Mott: spin-orbit entangled dimer singlets in Ba$_3$CeRu$_2$O$_9$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06886)
*L. Pätzold,A. Sandberg,H. Schilling,H. Gretarsson,E. Bergamasco,M. Magnaterra,P. Becker,P. H. M. van Loosdrecht,J. van den Brink,M. Hermanns,M. Grüninger*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过共振非弹性X射线散射发现Ba3CeRu2O9处于局域化莫特极限与准分子极限之间的复杂交叉区域，其自旋轨道纠缠的单重态基态表现出独特的混合特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 六方4d钌酸盐Ba3MRu2O9具有结构二聚体和竞争相互作用的微妙平衡，其中洪德耦合（Hund's coupling）、三角晶体场分裂以及$a_{1g}$和$e_g^π$轨道的跃迁能量均处于狭窄窗口内，导致从局域化莫特极限到团簇莫特极限的一系列可能基态。

Method: 采用共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic x-ray scattering）技术，研究具有每个二聚体四个空穴的Ba3CeRu2O9，分析其电子态特性。

Result: Ba3CeRu2O9处于局域化莫特情况与准分子极限之间的复杂交叉区域，其自旋轨道纠缠（spin-orbit entangled）的单重态基态主要表现出莫特型电荷分布（每个Ru位点两个空穴），但自旋和轨道占据与基于交换的莫特方案矛盾，而与团簇莫特方法一致，准分子试探波函数可描述超过70%的基态。

Conclusion: 在交叉区域，晶体场等参数的微小变化可能强烈影响电子态特性，Ba3CeRu2O9的基态特性由局域化莫特极限和准分子极限的混合特征共同决定。

Abstract: The hexagonal 4d ruthenates Ba3MRu2O9 host structural dimers and exhibit a delicate balance of competing interactions. Hund's coupling, trigonal crystal-field splitting, and hopping for $a_{1g}$ and $e_g^π$ orbitals all fall within a narrow energy window. This yields a series of possible ground states, ranging from the localized Mott limit with (anti-) ferromagnetic exchange coupling via orbital-selective behavior to the cluster Mott limit with quasimolecular orbitals that are delocalized over the two dimer sites. Using resonant inelastic x-ray scattering, we show that Ba3CeRu2O9 with four holes per dimer resides in the intricate crossover regime between the localized Mott case and the quasimolecular limit. The spin-orbit entangled singlet ground state predominantly shows a Mott-like charge distribution with two holes per Ru site. At the same time, spin and orbital occupation contradict an exchange-based Mott scenario but agree with a cluster Mott approach. A quasimolecular trial wave function describes more than 70% of the ground state. In this crossover regime, small changes of, e.g., the crystal field may strongly affect the character of electronic states.

</details>

Method: 基于 TensorKit.jl 构建对称性感知框架，通过 TRG、HOTRG 和 LoopTNR 等方法构造配分函数的张量网络表示并进行粗粒化（coarse-graining）。软件包设计注重可用性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: TNRKit.jl 为张量网络重整化方法提供了全面的实现框架，同时该论文也作为张量网络重整化框架的自包含介绍。软件包的开源特性促进了算法的应用、比较和发展。

Abstract: We present TNRKit.jl, an open-source Julia package for Tensor Network Renormalization (TNR) of two- and three-dimensional classical statistical models and Euclidean lattice field theories. Built on top of TensorKit.jl\cite{tensorkit}, it provides a symmetry-aware framework for constructing tensor-network representations of partition functions and coarse-graining them using methods such as TRG, HOTRG, and LoopTNR. Beyond thermodynamic quantities, the package enables the extraction of universal conformal data -- including scaling dimensions and the central charge -- directly from fixed-point tensors. TNRKit.jl is designed with both usability and extensibility in mind, offering a practical platform for applying, benchmarking, and developing modern tensor renormalization algorithms. This paper also serves as a self-contained introduction to the TNR framework.

### [30] [Reconstruction of F-cohomological field theories on moduli of compact type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07270)

Result: 主要结果包括：1) 证明了紧致型模空间上F-上同调场论的Givental-Teleman重构定理类似结果；2) 重构了扩展$r$-自旋类在扩展方向上的限制；3) 推导出了紧致型上$κ$-类之间的具体关系。

Conclusion: 结论表明Givental-Teleman重构框架可以扩展到紧致型模空间，为F-上同调场论提供了新的重构工具，并成功应用于$r$-自旋理论和$κ$-类关系的研究。

Abstract: We prove an analogue of Givental-Teleman reconstruction for F-cohomological field theories on the moduli space of compact type. We apply it to reconstruct the restriction of the extended $r$-spin classes to the extended direction and deduce relations between $κ$-classes (both in compact type).

</details>

### [31] [Dark Matter on a Slide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06315)
*Hsin-Chia Cheng,Xu-Hui Jiang,Lingfeng Li,Ennio Salvioni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种GeV能级热暗物质（thermal dark matter）模型，其暗物质由暗强相互作用（confining strong interaction）产生的暗π介子（dark pions）组成，通过暗π介子上散射至较重暗介子（dark mesons）再衰变至标准模型粒子的机制获得正确遗迹密度（relic density）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索一种只能通过加速器实验测试的GeV能级热暗物质场景。传统直接和间接暗物质探测对此类暗物质大多无效，因此需要寻找新的探测途径。

Method: 采用基于SU(3)/SO(3)陪集（coset）的最小模型，暗物质通过U(1)味对称性（flavor symmetry）稳定。遗迹密度机制涉及暗π介子上散射至较重暗介子（暗K介子和暗η介子的对应物），以及不稳定暗η介子衰变至标准模型粒子。

Result: 正确遗迹密度要求暗介子质量劈裂（mass splittings）为10%至50%，暗η介子寿命短于10³ m/c。最显著信号出现在LHC，表现为包含长寿命暗η介子的暗簇射（dark showers）衰变至可见末态。

Conclusion: 该暗物质模型主要通过加速器实验探测，多个已知门户相互作用（portal interactions）可在弱能标以上完成该场景，不同门户对应不同的预期信号特征。

Abstract: We present a scenario for GeV-scale thermal dark matter that can only be tested with accelerator experiments. Dark matter is composed of dark pions arising from a confining strong interaction in the dark sector. The thermal relic density is obtained through the interplay of up-scatterings of dark pions to heavier dark mesons (the dark counterparts of the kaons and $η$), and decays of the unstable dark $η$ to Standard Model particles. This mechanism is analogous to a playground slide, where one climbs up first and then slides down with a release of energy. We illustrate the scenario with a minimal model based on the SU(3)/SO(3) coset, where dark matter is stabilized by a U(1) flavor symmetry. The correct relic density is obtained with dark meson mass splittings of 10% to 50% and a dark-$η$ lifetime shorter than $10^3\,\mathrm{m}/c$. Direct and indirect dark matter searches are mostly ineffective, as a consequence of the charge conjugation symmetry of the stabilizing U(1). The most striking signals arise at the LHC, from the production of dark showers containing long-lived dark $η$'s that decay to visible final states. These signatures crucially depend on the portal interaction connecting the dark sector to the Standard Model. We show that several well-known portals can complete the scenario above the weak scale, and outline the expected signals in each case.

</details>


### [32] [Diffusion-Based Point-Cloud Generation of Heavy-Ion Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06458)
*Rita Sadek,Vinicius Mikuni,Mateusz Ploskon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分数驱动扩散过程（score-driven diffusion process）和点边Transformer架构（Point-Edge Transformer）的快速高保真生成模型，用于模拟重离子碰撞事件。该模型采用两阶段训练策略，在低多重数O-O碰撞上预训练后，在高多重数Pb-Pb碰撞上微调，能够生成逼真的高多重数重离子事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞产生包含数千至数万粒子的末态，其模拟是高能核物理中计算最密集的任务之一。需要开发快速、高保真的生成模型来替代传统计算密集型模拟方法。

Method: 基于分数驱动扩散过程（score-driven diffusion process）和点边Transformer架构（Point-Edge Transformer），在OmniLearn框架内构建生成模型。采用两阶段训练策略：第一阶段在低多重数O-O碰撞上训练，学习稳定的事件和粒子表示；第二阶段在高多重数Pb-Pb碰撞上进行微调。

Result: 通过广泛的闭包检验进行基准测试，包括一维和二维事件级与粒子级可观测量的一致性、从生成粒子重建的流一致性、使用FastJet的端到端喷注发现（包括关键喷注和子结构可观测量），以及基于分类器的样本保真度量化。结果表明紧凑生成模型能够产生逼真的高多重数重离子事件。

Conclusion: 结果令人鼓舞，表明紧凑生成模型能够产生逼真的高多重数重离子事件，使得高能重离子碰撞的局部尺度生成成为可实现的实际目标。

Abstract: Heavy-ion collisions produce final states with thousands to tens of thousands of particles, making their simulation among the most computationally intensive tasks in high-energy nuclear physics. We present a fast, high-fidelity generative model for heavy-ion events based on a score-driven diffusion process and the Point-Edge Transformer architecture within the OmniLearn framework. A two-stage training strategy is performed: Stage-1 training on lower-multiplicity O-O collisions allowing the model to learn a stable event and particles representation, followed by fine-tuning on challenging high-multiplicity Pb-Pb collisions. We benchmark the generator with a broad set of closure checks, including agreement of event- and particle-level observables in one and two dimensions, flow consistency reconstructed from the generated particles, end-to-end jet finding with FastJet including key jet and substructure observables, and a classifier-based application to quantify the sample fidelity. The results are promising, showing that a compact generative model can produce realistic, high-multiplicity heavy-ion events, at a level that makes local-scale generation for heavy-ion collisions at high energies a practical goal.

</details>


### [33] [Distribution amplitudes and functions of ground-state scalar and pseudoscalar charmonia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06510)
*X. -Y. Zeng,Y. -Y. Xiao,Z. -N. Xu,C. D. Roberts,J. Rodríguez-Quintero*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用连续施温格函数方法分析粲偶素（charmonia）的基态标量和赝标量态，发现这些态的结构比简单的氢原子类比更复杂，揭示了轨道角动量成分的非平凡性和分布振幅/分布函数的非正定性特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粲偶素常被视为类似氢原子的简单系统，可用于理解重夸克量子色动力学（QCD）。本研究旨在检验这一假设，分析粲偶素基态标量和赝标量态的结构复杂性。

Method: 采用连续施温格函数方法（continuum Schwinger function methods）分析粲偶素基态标量态（χ_{c0}）和赝标量态（η_c）的结构特性。

Result: 研究发现粲偶素结构比简单氢原子类比更复杂：χ_{c0}并非简单P波系统，η_c波函数也包含S波以外的贡献。分布振幅（DAs）和分布函数（DFs）具有非平凡特性，特别是χ_{c0}的分布振幅非正定，包含正负支撑域。两种态的胶子动量分数相同，比π介子中胶子动量分数低10%。

Conclusion: 粲偶素的结构比传统氢原子类比更复杂，需要更精细的理论描述。虽然实验验证困难，但这些结果为理解重夸克强子的局域和全局结构特征提供了重要的理论基准。

Abstract: Charmonia are often supposed to provide simple hydrogen-like ``atomic'' systems that can be used to obtain insights into heavier-quark QCD. We use continuum Schwinger function methods to analyse this hypothesis in connection with ground-state scalar and pseudoscalar charmonia and find that a more complex picture of these states may be necessary. For instance, considering orbital angular momentum, the $χ_{c0}$ is not a simple $P$-wave system; similarly, the $η_c$ wave function contains more than merely $S$-wave contributions. The distribution amplitudes (DAs) and distribution functions (DFs) of these mesons are also nontrivial. For instance, the $χ_{c0}$ DA is not positive definite: owing to QCD symmetries, it possesses domains of balanced negative and positive support. This feature is also expressed in the $χ_{c0}$ DF, but differences between $χ_{c0}$ and $η_c$ DFs diminish under scale evolution. Notably, the light-front momentum fraction carried by glue is the same in both states: it is 10\% less than the in-pion glue momentum fraction. Whilst experimental confirmation of the predictions herein is unlikely, our results should serve as benchmarks for complementary theory attempts to understand local and global structural features of heavier-quark hadrons.

</details>


### [34] [The chromomagnetic moment of a heavy quark with hyperasymptotic precision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.05044)
*Cesar Ayala,Antonio Pineda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究确定了重夸克色磁矩（chromomagnetic moment）的主要红外重整化子（infrared renormalon）归一化，并利用超渐近精度（hyperasymptotic precision）计算了B和D介子基态的超精细劈裂（hyperfine splitting），通过拟合实验数据获得了重夸克有效理论（HQET）中的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决重夸克有效理论中微扰级数（perturbative series）的高阶系数估计问题，特别是与红外重整化子相关的发散行为，这对于精确计算重介子的超精细劈裂至关重要。

Method: 方法包括确定重夸克色磁矩的主要红外重整化子归一化，估计微扰级数的高阶系数，并采用超渐近精度计算B和D介子基态的超精细劈裂，其中包含了与第一红外重整化子相关的主导项（leading terminant）。

Result: 通过将实验数据拟合到算子乘积展开（operator product expansion）的理论预测中，以$\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}$为自由参数，获得了$\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}=0.507(7)$ GeV$^2$的基态结果，该参数在重夸克有效理论中具有重要意义。

Conclusion: 研究成功确定了重夸克色磁矩的主要红外重整化子归一化，并通过超渐近精度方法实现了对B和D介子超精细劈裂的精确计算，为理解重夸克系统的非微扰效应提供了重要理论工具。

Abstract: We determine the normalization of the leading infrared renormalon of the chromomagnetic moment of a heavy quark. Estimates of higher order coefficients of the perturbative series are given. We compute the hyperfine splitting of the $B$ and $D$ mesons for the ground state with hyperasymptotic precision by including the leading terminant, associated with the first infrared renormalon. We fit the experimental data to the operator product expansion theoretical prediction with $\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}$ as the free parameter. We obtain $\hat μ^2_{G,\rm PV}=0.507(7)$ GeV$^2$ for the ground state.

</details>


### [35] [Hamiltonian Constraints on Spontaneous Lorentz Symmetry Breaking in the Bumblebee Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06271)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li,Zhi Xiao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明通过拉格朗日势能最小值确定自发洛伦兹破缺的标准做法通常是错误的，指出哈密顿密度才是推导真实真空的正确方法，并证明标准二次势能无法一致地产生真空期望值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在纠正确定自发洛伦兹破缺（spontaneous Lorentz violation）的标准做法，指出通过拉格朗日势能最小值确定真空态的方法存在根本性缺陷，需要建立更严格的推导框架。

Method: 通过分析矢量场的哈密顿结构（Hamiltonian structure）和约束条件，从哈密顿密度（Hamiltonian density）推导真实真空态，并系统研究不同类型势能函数的一致性条件。

Result: 证明标准二次势能无法一致地产生真空期望值（vacuum expectation value, VEV），确定三次势能为最简单可行的替代方案，并证明光滑势能仅支持稳定的类时或类光真空期望值。

Conclusion: 研究结论可推广到高阶张量场，并对高阶张量场和洛伦兹破缺有效场论（Lorentz-violating effective field theories）施加严格的一致性约束，为相关理论研究提供了重要修正。

Abstract: This study demonstrates that the common practice of determining spontaneous Lorentz violation via the minimum of a Lagrangian potential is generally incorrect. By analyzing the Hamiltonian structure and constraints of vector fields, we show that the true vacuum must be derived from the Hamiltonian density. We prove that the standard quadratic potential cannot consistently generate a vacuum expectation value (VEV), identifying a cubic potential as the simplest viable alternative. Furthermore, we prove that smooth potentials only support stable timelike or lightlike VEVs. These conclusions extend to higher-rank tensor fields and impose rigorous consistency constraints on higher-rank tensor fields and Lorentz-violating effective field theories.

</details>


### [36] [QED radiative corrections in inverse beta decay from virtual pions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07113)
*Oleksandr Tomalak*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文评估了反中微子能量大于10 MeV时，逆β衰变（IBD）过程中由虚π介子贡献的辐射修正，发现这些修正对运动学依赖性的影响小于核子形状因子的不确定性，从而实现了千分之一级别的理论精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆β衰变（inverse beta decay, IBD）是反应堆和超新星反中微子的主要探测通道。为了在反中微子能量大于10 MeV时提供精确的IBD截面，需要评估辐射修正对理论精度的影响。

Method: 在重子手征微扰理论（heavy baryon chiral perturbation theory）框架下，评估了虚π介子贡献的辐射修正。分析了领头阶（leading order）和次领头阶（next-to-leading order）的贡献，特别关注了π介子同位旋分裂贡献和Wilson系数c₄的作用。

Result: 研究发现，π介子诱导的QED辐射修正对运动学依赖性的影响处于核子形状因子动量依赖性的不确定度水平甚至更低。所有次领头阶辐射修正都相对较小，使得在相对低能时IBD的理论精度不受Wilson系数c₄精确值的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究实现了反中微子能量大于10 MeV时，带电流弹性（反）中微子-核子散射（charged-current elastic (anti)neutrino-nucleon scattering）的千分之一级别理论精度，为精确测量反应堆和超新星反中微子提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: Inverse beta decay (IBD), $\overlineν_e p \to e^+ n \left( γ\right)$, is the main detection channel for reactor and supernova antineutrinos. To provide precise IBD cross sections at antineutrino energies $E_{\overlineν_e} \gtrsim 10~\mathrm{MeV}$, we evaluate radiative corrections from virtual pions within the framework of heavy baryon chiral perturbation theory. At leading order, only the pion isospin-splitting contributions are not suppressed by the electron mass. At next-to-leading order, besides recoil effects, only the Wilson coefficient $c_4$ contributes to the kinematic dependence. However, its precise value is not relevant for IBD at relatively low energies since all next-to-leading order radiative corrections are relatively small. We find the kinematic dependence of the pion-induced QED radiative corrections at the level and below the uncertainty from the momentum dependence of the nucleon form factors. Our results enable sub-permille theoretical precision of charged-current elastic (anti)neutrino-nucleon scattering at antineutrino energies $E_{\overlineν_e} \gtrsim 10~\mathrm{MeV}$.

</details>

Conclusion: 该非局域夸克模型通过修正拉普拉斯变换的方法，有效实现了夸克禁闭机制，并能够同步描述禁闭相和退禁闭相。研究为理解有限温度下介子质谱行为提供了理论框架，特别是在相变区域的质量演化规律。

Abstract: The mass spectrum of pseudoscalar and scalar meson modes at finite temperature is studied in the framework of a nonlocal quark model. The model implements quark confinement via the modification of the Laplace transform of the quark propagator. In order to synchronize the confining and deconfining phases, a modification of the transform is proposed. The behavior of the screening masses of mesons is studied in a wide region of temperatures, while the pole masses are described up to the deconfining phase transition.

### [38] [Constraining magnetic monopoles and multiply charged particles with diphoton events at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07300)

Method: 研究聚焦于这类虚拟粒子在有效场论和Born-Infeld情景下对光-光散射过程的贡献。利用CMS-TOTEM精密质子谱仪（Precision Proton Spectrometer）测量的质子标记光子对中心独占产生（central exclusive production of photon pairs）数据，结合重求和（resummation）技术处理大HECO-光子耦合。

Abstract: The LHC is achieving energies never reached before, opening up possibilities for the discovery of exotic particles in the TeV mass range. Such states include magnetic monopoles, which can explain the electric charge quantisation and restore the symmetry in Maxwell's equations with respect to the magnetic and electric fields. Scenarios proposed to shed light to dark matter and neutrino masses introduce high-electric-charge objects (HECOs). The existence of both classes of particles can be probed in precision measurements in a manner complementary to direct searches. We focus on the contributions of such virtual particles to light-by-light scattering in the context of effective field theories and a Born-Infeld scenario. Specifically, measurements of central exclusive production of photon pairs with proton tagging carried out by the CMS-TOTEM Precision Proton Spectrometer with LHC Run 2 proton-proton collision data are used to constrain magnetic monopole and HECOs. Resummation techniques have been employed to deal with the large HECO-photon coupling. Masses of up to a few tens of TeV have been excluded for monopoles and HECOs of various spins and magnetic and electric charges, respectively.
