### [39] [Uncool soft-wall transitions and gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06306)
*Ameen Ismail,Lian-Tao Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了软壁（soft-wall）曲率奇点截断的翘曲额外维度理论中的相变动力学，发现与传统的Randall-Sundrum模型不同，软壁结构导致相变快速完成且过冷度较小，产生的引力波信号可被未来空间干涉仪探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Randall-Sundrum模型中的一级相变通常具有强过冷特性，但软壁曲率奇点截断的翘曲额外维度理论可能改变这一标准图像，需要深入理解其相变动力学。

Method: 采用简单的翘曲几何ansatz以获得解析结果，同时保持软壁的基本行为；计算黑洞膜视界位置的有效四维作用量，并利用该有效作用量分析相变动力学。

Result: 软壁结构中热黑洞膜相仅存在于最小温度以上，该温度与临界温度相差不大；相变快速完成（典型β/H值为10³⁻⁴）且过冷度较小；TeV能标相变产生的引力波信号可被未来空间干涉仪探测。

Conclusion: 软壁截断的翘曲额外维度理论中的全息相变（holographic phase transition）动力学与传统硬膜模型显著不同，表现为快速、轻微过冷的相变过程，其引力波信号具有可观测前景。

Abstract: Theories with warped extra dimensions, like the Randall-Sundrum (RS) model, exhibit a holographic phase transition from a hot, deconfined black brane phase to a cool, confined phase. The standard picture of a first-order, strongly supercooled phase transition is expected to change in variations where the extra dimension is smoothly cut off by a soft-wall curvature singularity, as opposed to a hard brane. To understand this situation, we consider a simple ansatz for the warped geometry which allows us to obtain analytical results while maintaining the essential behavior of a soft wall. Unlike RS with the usual Goldberger-Wise stabilization, the hot, black brane phase only exists above a minimum temperature, which is not much smaller than the critical temperature. We explore the dynamics of the phase transition across the range of possibilities for the asymptotic geometry of a soft wall. This involves calculating an effective 4D action for the location of the black brane horizon. Using the effective action, we show that the phase transition completes rapidly ($β/H$ of $10^{3\text{-}4}$ is typical) and with only slight supercooling. We compute the resulting gravitational wave signal for a TeV-scale transition, finding that it is accessible to future space-based interferometers.

</details>


### [40] [The non-topological $Z^\prime$ string in the 331 model and its classical stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06530)
*Zhengyang Bian,Ning Chen,Mian Guo,Zhanpeng Hou,Haoyang Ji,Junyi Wei,Zhuo Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了最小331模型中非拓扑$Z^\prime$弦的经典稳定性，发现仅在$\vartheta_S \approx \frac{\pi}{2}$的半局域极限附近稳定，表明基于${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(N>5)$李代数的统一理论中不太可能存在此类非拓扑弦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探索最小331模型中非拓扑$Z^\prime$弦的经典稳定性，该模型源自${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(6)$玩具模型的最大对称性破缺模式。通过分析此类弦的稳定性，可以评估其在基于${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(N>5)$李代数的统一理论中的存在可能性。

Method: 研究方法包括引入两个希格斯三重态（Higgs triplets）以实现${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_c\oplus {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_W \oplus {\mathfrak u}(1)_X\to {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_c\oplus {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(2)_W \oplus {\mathfrak u}(1)_Y$的序贯对称性破缺。通过分析弦背景附近的小扰动并数值求解耦合的亥姆霍兹方程（Helmholtz equations）来评估稳定性。

Result: 研究结果显示，即使在调整希格斯自耦合以最小化不稳定性时，该弦也仅在$\vartheta_S \approx \frac{\pi}{2}$的半局域极限（semilocal limit）附近保持稳定。这一发现表明此类非拓扑弦在更广泛的参数空间中普遍不稳定。

Conclusion: 结论指出，基于${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(N>5)$李代数的统一理论中不太可能存在此类非拓扑弦，因为其稳定性仅限于非常狭窄的参数区域。这一发现对构建包含稳定拓扑缺陷的统一模型具有重要启示意义。

Abstract: We study the classical stability of a non-topological $Z^\prime$ string in the minimal 331 model, which arises from the maximal symmetry breaking pattern of an ${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(6)$ toy model. Two Higgs triplets are introduced according to the emergent global symmetries in the fermionic sector of the ${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(6)$ toy model, which will achieve the sequential symmetry breaking of ${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_c\oplus {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_W \oplus {\mathfrak u}(1)_X\to {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(3)_c\oplus {{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(2)_W \oplus {\mathfrak u}(1)_Y$. By analyzing small perturbations around the string background and solving the coupled Helmholtz equations numerically, we find that the string is stable only near the semilocal limit of $\vartheta_S \approx \fracπ{2}$, even when Higgs self-couplings are tuned to minimize instabilities. This suggests that such non-topological strings are unlikely to exist in unified theories based on ${{\mathfrak s}{\mathfrak u}}(N>5)$ Lie algebras.

</details>


### [41] [Experimental predictions of the $E_8 \times ωE_8$ octonionic unification program : A falsification-oriented catalogue for quantum foundations, particle physics, gravitation, and cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06288)
*Tejinder P. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文旨在系统整理$E_8 \times ωE_8$八元数理论中可实验验证的预测，并将其按逻辑强度分类，为该理论的实验检验提供清晰框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该理论框架具有高度综合性，但广度既是其吸引力也是主要弱点。论文旨在将理论中可实验验证的预测集中整理并分类，以展示其不同领域预测的内在一致性，避免被误解为互不关联的猜想集合。

Method: 采用"冷启动"教学式方法，从理论核心要素到可观测量的映射开始，系统整理理论在量子基础、粒子物理和引力领域的预测，并按逻辑强度进行分类。

Result: 论文系统整理了理论在量子基础方面（如客观自发坍缩、算子时间、时间自发坍缩等）和粒子物理方面（如右手前引力规范区、扩展希格斯区、暗电磁学等）的详细预测，并建立了这些预测之间的逻辑关联。

Conclusion: 通过将理论的可实验验证预测系统化整理和分类，为检验$E_8 \times ωE_8$八元数理论的实验脆弱性提供了清晰框架，有助于评估该统一理论框架的有效性。

Abstract: The $E_8 \times ωE_8$ octonionic program aims at a deliberately ambitious synthesis: quantum theory without external classical time, objective collapse, emergent classical space-time, exceptional Jordan-algebra flavor structure, and an exceptional-group unification of visible matter with a right-handed pre-gravitational sector. The purpose of the present paper is not to review the whole formalism, but to assemble in one place the claims that are experimentally vulnerable and to classify them by logical strength. We begin with a cold-start pedagogical map from the core ingredients of the program to the observables it claims to generate. This map matters because the program's breadth is both its attraction and its principal vulnerability: if the particle-physics, gravitation, and quantum-foundational claims are not visibly derived from the same structure, the framework reduces to a collection of disconnected conjectures.
  On the quantum-foundational side the program predicts objective spontaneous collapse, operator time, spontaneous collapse in time, loss of temporal interference above an attosecond-scale separation, a six-dimensional explanation of apparent nonlocality, possible Bell correlations beyond the Tsirelson bound, a fermion-only collapse sector, and holographic or Karolyhazy-type space-time uncertainty. In particle physics it predicts a right-handed pre-gravitational gauge sector, an extended Higgs sector, dark electromagnetism and its dark photon, three inert right-handed Majorana neutrinos, Majorana light neutrinos, a maximal leptonic Dirac phase, CKM root-sum rules, charged-fermion mass relations including the first-generation $1{:}4{:}9$ pattern and the relation $m_τ/m_μ= m_s/m_d$, a low-energy fine-structure constant, a weak-mixing-angle derivation, and the mixed-regime relation $α_s(M_Z)/α_{em}(0)=16$.

### [42] [Tunable Valley Polarization in Diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06351)
*Nattakarn Suntornwipat,Jan Isberg,Saman Majdi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了一种基于金刚石的双栅极、双漏极谷晶体管架构，通过栅极电压调控实现可调谐的谷极化输运，并证明金刚石中的谷极化输运在宏观距离上对热变化具有显著鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信息技术需要器件稳定性，其中电子态的可控性至关重要。金刚石谷电子学（diamond valleytronics）通过利用谷自由度（valley degree of freedom）存储和操纵信息，提供了一个有前景的平台。

Method: 采用双栅极、双漏极架构（dual-gate, two-drain architecture）的金刚石谷晶体管，通过栅极电压调制（gate voltage modulation）实现可调谐的谷极化输运。该方法利用了金刚石导带谷（conduction band valleys）的显著有效质量各向异性（effective-mass anisotropy）来控制空间分布和渡越时间。

Result: 实验证明金刚石中的谷极化输运在宏观距离上对热变化具有显著鲁棒性（remarkably robust against thermal variations）。该架构实现了对空间分布和渡越时间的控制，展示了谷态（valley states）的稳定性。

Conclusion: 这些结果证明了谷态的弹性（resilience of valley states），并突显了金刚石在下一代量子和高功率电子学中用于节能谷电子器件（energy-efficient valleytronic devices）的潜力。

Abstract: Device stability is essential for quantum information technologies, where reliable control of electronic states is crucial. Diamond valleytronics offers a promising platform by exploiting the valley degree of freedom to store and manipulate information. In this work, we demonstrate a diamond-based valley transistor with a dual-gate, two-drain architecture that enables tunable valley-polarized transport via gate voltage modulation. By leveraging the significant effective-mass anisotropy of diamond's conduction band valleys, this architecture provides control over spatial distribution and transit times. We further demonstrate that valley-polarized transport in diamond is remarkably robust against thermal variations over macroscopic distances. These results demonstrate the resilience of valley states and highlight diamond's potential for energy-efficient valleytronic devices in next-generation quantum and high-power electronics.

### [43] [Ballistic atomic transport in narrow carbon nanotubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06490)
*Alberto Ambrosetti,Pier Luigi Silvestrelli,John F. Dobson,Luca Salasnich*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究采用量子力学方法描述氦-4在窄碳纳米管中的流动，发现即使在有界面相互作用、有限温度和缺陷的现实条件下，仍能实现无摩擦的弹道波状传输，揭示了纳米尺度界面的量子本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半经典摩擦理论将能量耗散与牛顿运动关联，但观察到水在窄碳纳米管中几乎无阻碍流动的现象挑战了这一理论。研究旨在超越标准牛顿视角，探索纳米尺度界面的量子特性。

Method: 采用量子力学描述氦-4在窄碳纳米管中的流动，基于布洛赫波动力学方法，考虑非零界面相互作用、有限温度和碳纳米管缺陷等现实流动条件。

Result: 在0 K温度下，氦-4波能在理想周期性界面势垒中无摩擦传播；低于由界面起伏调节的临界速度时，等离子体和声子量子发射的能量损失被禁止。引入缺陷后仍观察到微米尺度的平均自由程，热声子和等离子体导致更低的散射率。

Conclusion: 研究确立了在现实纳米尺度器件中窄碳纳米管内弹道波状传输的意外出现，并证明了纳米尺度界面的内在量子性，超越了传统半经典摩擦模型。

Abstract: Friction forces are conventionally modeled via semiclassical theories that associate energy dissipation with newtonian motion on corrugated interface potentials. This consolidated approach is challenged at the nanoscale by observation of nearly unimpeded water flow in narrow carbon nanotubes (CNTs), in spite of nonvanishing energy corrugations. Here we go beyond the standard newtonian perspective, adopting a quantum mechanical description of 4 He flow through narrow CNTs. Building upon our Bloch-wave dynamics [Phys. Rev. Lett. 131, 206301 (2023)] we explore realistic flow conditions, including non-negligible interface interactions, finite temperatures, and imperfect CNTs. At T = 0 K we found that 4 He waves can propagate through ideally periodic, corrugated interface potentials with no friction: below a critical velocity regulated by interface corrugations, energy loss by emission of plasmon and phonon quanta is forbidden. Introducing realistic impurities/defects one still finds very large mean free paths that can exceed the micrometer scale, while thermal phonons and plasmons yield even lower scattering rates. This establishes the unexpected emergence of ballistic wavelike transport in narrow CNTs within realistic nanoscale devices, and demonstrates the intrinsic quantumness of nanoscale interfaces.

</details>


### [44] [Exact Solution for Current-Driven Domain-Wall Dynamics Beyond Lorentz Contraction in Antiferromagnets with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06730)
*Mu-Kun Lee,Rubén M. Otxoa,Masahito Mochizuki*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究反铁磁体（AFMs）中具有Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）的电流驱动畴壁（DW）动力学，旨在提供精确的理论描述并识别DMI修饰的畴壁动力学在实验上可观测的特征。

Method: 通过理论分析获得了螺旋畴壁动力学的精确解析解，该方法适用于体DMI下的头对头畴壁和界面DMI下的上下畴壁（当磁易轴与DMI矢量对齐时）。

Result: 解析解预测：非绝热自旋转移矩驱动恒定畴壁速度，阻尼类自旋轨道矩诱导畴壁倾斜角稳定旋转。畴壁宽度表现出非传统的电流依赖性，呈现纯伸长或先收缩后伸长模式，这与无DMI反铁磁畴壁的洛伦兹型收缩形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了电流驱动反铁磁畴壁动力学的精确描述，并指出了在合成反铁磁体中DMI修饰的畴壁动力学具有实验上可观测的特征，为相关实验验证提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study current-driven domain-wall (DW) dynamics in antiferromagnets (AFMs) with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI). We obtain an exact analytical solution for spiral DW dynamics, applicable to both head-to-head DWs under bulk DMI and up-down DWs under interfacial DMI when the magnetic easy axis is aligned with the DMI vector. For the latter case experimentally relevant to synthetic AFMs with in-plane anisotropy, the solution predicts a constant DW velocity driven by nonadiabatic spin-transfer torque together with a steady rotation of the DW tilt angle induced by damping-like spin-orbit torque. Remarkably, the DW width shows unconventional current dependence, either pure elongation or contraction followed by elongation depending on damping and torque parameters, in sharp contrast to the Lorentz-type contraction known for antiferromagnetic (AF) DWs without DMI. These results provide an exact description of current-driven AF-DW dynamics and suggest experimentally accessible signatures of DMI-modified DW dynamics in synthetic AFMs.

### [45] [Resolving Single-Peptide Phosphorylation Dynamics in Plasmonic Nanopores using Physics-Informed Bi-Path Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06743)
*Mulusew W. Yaltaye,Yingqi Zhao,Kuo Zhan,Vahid Farrahi,Jian-An Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种结合物理信息深度学习与纳米等离子体孔技术的框架，用于从复杂的单分子表面增强拉曼光谱（SM-SERS）信号中可靠识别单个肽段的磷酸化修饰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质磷酸化（protein phosphorylation）作为细胞信号传导的动态指标，在低丰度和低化学计量比条件下难以检测。虽然单分子表面增强拉曼光谱（SM-SERS）技术提供了无标记分子检测能力，但随机信号波动、肽段残基的部分激发以及背景干扰阻碍了细微翻译后修饰（PTMs）的可靠识别。

Method: 研究提出了一种物理信息深度学习框架，整合多实例学习（multiple-instance learning）与结合时间卷积网络和双向门控循环单元的时间编码器，以捕捉局部光谱变异性和长程闪烁动态。针对扩散驱动的光谱异质性，采用皮尔逊相关系数（Pearson-correlation）分割长光谱轨迹，实现标签模糊下的弱监督训练。

Result: 该框架能够在强背景干扰和随机信号波动条件下，稳健地区分单个肽段的磷酸化修饰。通过将纳米等离子体限制与时空深度学习相结合，实现了单分子磷酸化事件的高保真检测。

Conclusion: 该方法推动了超灵敏磷酸化蛋白质组学（phosphoproteomic）分析的发展，为低丰度翻译后修饰的单分子检测提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Protein phosphorylation provides a dynamic readout of cellular signaling yet remains difficult to detect at low abundance and stoichiometry. Single-molecule surface-enhanced Raman spectroscopy (SM-SERS) using particle-in-pore plasmonic nanopores offers label-free molecular detection with submolecular sensitivity. However, reliable identification of subtle post-translational modifications (PTMs) is hindered by the stochastic nature of SM-SERS signals, partial excitation of peptide residues within the plasmonic hotspot, and background interference. Here, we introduce a physics-informed deep learning framework to decode complex SM-SERS dynamics and identify single-peptide PTMs. The model integrates multiple-instance learning with a temporal encoder combining temporal convolutional networks and bidirectional gated recurrent units to capture both local spectral variability and long-range blinking dynamics. To address diffusion-driven spectral heterogeneity, long spectral trajectories are segmented using Pearson-correlation, enabling weakly supervised training under label ambiguity. This framework robustly distinguishes single peptide phosphorylation despite strong background interference and stochastic signal fluctuations. By coupling nanoplasmonic confinement with spatiotemporal deep learning, our approach enables high-fidelity detection of single-molecule phosphorylation events and advances ultrasensitive phosphoproteomic analysis.

</details>


### [46] [Self-Assembled Telecom Color Centers in Silicon and Their Growth Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06766)
*Jacqueline Marböck,Enrique Prado Navarrete,Merve Karaman,Oliver E. Lang,Thomas Fromherz,Maciej O. Liedke,Andreas Wagner,Moritz Brehm,Johannes Aberl*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了超低温分子束外延（MBE）生长条件下真空环境对硅色心（SiCCs）自组装和光学性质的影响，重点关注生长压力和基底温度对W、G、G'、T等关键色心形成的作用，并探讨了生长压力对抑制发光背景的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅色心（SiCCs）作为光子量子技术的关键组件具有重要应用前景，但传统离子注入制备方法存在垂直离子散射和晶格损伤等限制。超低温分子束外延（MBE）作为一种新型全外延制备技术，需要极纯净的生长环境，然而目前缺乏关于外延过程中真空条件如何具体影响SiCC形成、光学性质及周围晶体质量的研究。

Method: 采用超低温（ULT）分子束外延（MBE）技术，在低于约350°C的温度下通过动力学限制生长（碳掺杂）硅（Si:C）实现SiCCs的自组装。研究生长压力和基底温度对W、G、G'、T等重要色心自组装和光致发光（PL）性质的影响，并利用PL和多普勒展宽变能正电子湮没谱（Doppler broadening variable energy positron annihilation spectroscopy）分析生长压力对抑制发光背景的作用。

Result: 研究发现生长压力和基底温度对硅色心（SiCCs）的自组装和光致发光（PL）性质具有显著影响。特别强调了生长压力在抑制发光背景方面的关键作用，这对于推进量子光子学应用至关重要。

Conclusion: 超低温分子束外延（MBE）制备硅色心（SiCCs）过程中，真空生长条件（特别是生长压力和基底温度）对色心的形成、光学性质及周围晶体质量具有决定性影响，优化这些参数对于实现高质量量子光子器件至关重要。

Abstract: Artificial atoms based on color centers in silicon (SiCCs) have recently emerged as promising candidates for highly integrable and scalable key components in photonic quantum technology, including telecom single-photon sources and spin memory devices. A novel all-epitaxial fabrication technique for SiCCs, based on ultra-low-temperature (ULT) molecular beam epitaxy (MBE), addresses limitations of conventional fabrication via ion implantation, such as vertical ion straggle and collateral crystal lattice damage. This method solely relies on self-assembly of SiCCs during kinetically-limited growth of (carbon-doped) Si(:C) at ULTs <~350°C. The latter requires an extraordinary pristine growth environment to prevent unintended defect formation caused by the incorporation of impurities from the background vapor; however, so far, no study has specifically addressed how exactly the vacuum conditions during epitaxy influence SiCC formation, their optical properties, and the quality of the surrounding crystal matrix. Here, we investigate the impact of the growth pressure and the substrate temperature on the self-assembly and photoluminescence (PL) properties of important SiCCs, such as W, G, G', and T centers. Further, we use PL and Doppler broadening variable energy positron annihilation spectroscopy to emphasize the role of the growth pressure in suppressing the luminescence background, which is crucial for advancing quantum photonics applications.

</details>


### [47] [Telecom C-band single-photon sources with a semiconductor-dielectric microresonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06869)
*Yuriy Serov,Aidar Galimov,Sergey Sorokin,Nikolai Maleev,Marina Kulagina,Yuriy Zadiranov,Grigorii Klimko,Maxim Rakhlin,Alexey Veretennikov,Gleb Veyshtort,Olga Lakuntsova,Yuliya Salii,Daria Berezina,Sergey Troshkov,Demid Kirilenko,Alexey Blokhin,Alexei Vasil'ev,Alexander Kuzmenkov,Mikhail Bobrov,Irina Sedova,Tatiana V. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前量子密钥分发（quantum key distribution）中广泛使用的单光子源是高度衰减的激光脉冲，其单光子产生概率较低。需要开发更高效的确定性单光子源来提升量子通信性能。

Method: 采用InAs/GaAs量子点置于微柱形微腔（micropillar-shaped microcavity）中，创新性地使用不同半导体和介电材料分别构成下布拉格反射镜（GaAs/AlGaAs）和上布拉格反射镜（Si/SiO₂）。通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长相干异质结构，并在不完全微柱上沉积少量Si/SiO₂对来实现材料兼容性。

Result: 该设计实现了π脉冲（π-pulses）共振激发，能够产生偏振光子，并达到了创纪录的11%端到端效率（end-to-end efficiency）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种高效的确定性单光子源，通过创新的异质材料集成方案显著提升了单光子产生效率，为量子密钥分发等应用提供了性能更优的光子源。

Abstract: Secure communications with quantum key distribution over fiber-optic links is one of the few recognized applications of quantum physics at the level of individual quanta -- single C-band photons. Currently, the widely used sources of such photons are highly attenuated laser pulses, featured by a low probability of single photon occurrence. Here, we present an efficient source with an InAs/GaAs quantum dot on a metamorphic buffer layer inside a micropillar-shaped microcavity. The key innovation is the use of different semiconductor and dielectric materials to form the lower (GaAs/AlGaAs) and upper (Si/SiO$_2$) Bragg reflectors. Compatibility of these materials in a monolithic source is achieved by depositing a small amount of Si/SiO$_2$ pairs on an incomplete micropillar made from a coherent heterostructure grown by molecular beam epitaxy. This design enables resonant excitation with $π$-pulses and generation of polarized photons with a record-breaking end-to-end efficiency of 11%.

### [48] [Millisecond spin relaxation times of distinct electron and hole subensembles in MA$_x$FA$_{1-x}$PbI$_3$ perovskite crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06887)
*Rongrong Hu,Sergey R. Meliakov,Dmitri R. Yakovlev,Bekir Turedi,Maksym V. Kovalenko,Manfred Bayer,Vasilii V. Belykh*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 混合A位钙钛矿单晶展现出长寿命自旋态，其自旋弛豫机制由核超精细场主导，载流子在浅局域化位点间的跳跃决定了超精细场的相关时间。这些特性使其成为量子信息应用的有前景固态平台。

Abstract: The unique combination of outstanding optical quality and attractive spin properties opens new avenues for optical spin control in hybrid organic-inorganic perovskite semiconductors. Using the optically detected magnetic resonance technique, we study the spins of electrons and holes in mixed-cation MA$_x$FA$_{1-x}$PbI$_3$ single crystals with $x = 0.4$ and 0.8. Multiple distinct spin subensembles with $g$-factors spanning from 2.9 to 3.6 for electrons and from 0.5 to 1.2 for holes are resolved, revealing diverse localization environments. We measure the longitudinal spin relaxation times, $T_1$, reaching 2 ms and remaining in the $μ$s range even for weakly localized carriers at the cryogenic temperature of 1.6 K. The magnetic-field dependence of $T_1$ is dominated by the random nuclear (Overhauser) fields with strengths of $\sim 0.4-0.8$ mT for electrons and $\sim 4-12$ mT for holes, corresponding to $μ$s-long correlation times of the hyperfine field determined by carrier hopping between shallow localization sites. The temperature dependence of $T_1$ reveals a weak localization potential of the charge carriers and shows a correlation between $T_1$ and the inhomogeneity of the spin ensemble. These results establish mixed-A-site perovskite single crystals as a promising solid-state platform with long-lived spin states for quantum information applications.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子莫特转变（exciton Mott transition, EMT）通常与粒子数反转和光学增益的出现相关联，但本研究旨在探索在超快非平衡激发条件下这一传统范式是否可能失效。

Method: 采用飞秒泵浦-探测光学光谱（femtosecond pump-probe optical spectroscopy）驱动单层过渡金属硫族化合物进入高密度光激发态，并结合最先进的实时从头算模拟（real-time ab initio simulations）分析非平衡动力学过程。

Abstract: Exciton dissociation via the excitonic Mott transition (EMT) governs the high-density optical response of semiconductors and sets fundamental limits for optoelectronic devices. The EMT is conventionally linked to the onset of population inversion and the emergence of optical gain. Here, we demonstrate that this paradigm can break down under ultrafast non-equilibrium excitation. Using femtosecond pump-probe optical spectroscopy, we drive a monolayer transition metal dichalcogenide into a dense photoexcited state in which the excitonic resonance is completely quenched within ~100 fs, while the optical gain is entirely absent across the explored fluence range. State-of-the-art real-time ab initio simulations reveal that the EMT is governed by an interplay of strongly nonthermal carrier populations and nonequilibrium dynamical screening of the Coulomb interaction.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相关纳米尺度系统的输运是量子点和分子尺度器件的基础，但随着系统尺寸增大，大型开放量子系统的精确模拟面临计算挑战。张量网络方法通过高效压缩量子态，为解决这一尺度障碍提供了有前景的途径。

Method: 扩展了基于张量的求解器，引入跳跃计数估计器（jump-counting estimator），能够直接从引线诱导的隧穿事件计算稳态电子电流。该方法与最先进的QmeQ主方程求解器进行了基准测试，比较了引线-点和点间耦合参数。

Result: 在可处理范围内与QmeQ主方程求解器获得了定量一致的结果。相比经典方法，TJM将内存需求和计算时间降低了数量级，能够模拟远超出基于密度矩阵的输运求解器范围的相互作用量子点阵列。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了包含多达50个量子点的阵列中的量子输运建模，为更大阵列中尺寸依赖的非平衡输运系统研究提供了可能，突破了传统密度矩阵方法的计算限制。

Abstract: Transport through correlated nanoscale systems underpins the operation of quantum-dot and molecular-scale devices, yet accurate simulations of large open quantum systems remain computationally challenging as system size increases. Tensor-network methods offer a promising route past this scaling barrier by efficiently compressing quantum states. Here we extend a tensor-based solver with a jump-counting estimator that enables direct computation of steady-state electron currents from lead-induced tunneling events. We benchmark the resulting currents against the state-of-the-art master-equation solver QmeQ across a range of lead-dot and inter-dot coupling parameters and find quantitative agreement in the tractable regime. Compared with classical approaches, TJM reduces memory requirements and wall-clock time by orders of magnitude, enabling simulations of interacting quantum-dot arrays far beyond the range accessible to density-matrix-based transport solvers and systematic studies of size-dependent nonequilibrium transport in larger arrays. Our approach allow us to model quantum transport in an array of up to fifty (50) quantum dots.

Abstract: In type II multiferroics, noncollinear spin textures are expected to induce electric polarization directly, leading to strong magnetoelectric coupling. Here, using vectorial spin polarized scanning tunneling microscopy, we investigated the spin-driven multiferroicity in monolayer NiI2 at atomic scale. ### [52] [Revisiting quadratic band crossing: from interaction-driven instability to intrinsic topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07139)
*Yadong Jiang,Linghao Huang,Zhaochen Liu,Huan Wang,Jing Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在凝聚态物理中，实现高温鲁棒的量子反常霍尔（quantum anomalous Hall, QAH）相仍是一个核心挑战。虽然二次能带交叉点（quadratic band crossing points, QBCP）为实现QAH态提供了有前景的途径，但现有方案大多局限于理想化模型或受到相互作用驱动的竞争序的阻碍。

Method: 提出一种通用机制：通过对称性保护的轨道双重态（如dₓz、dyz）与孤立轨道（如dz²）之间的能带反转，生成具有相反曲率的QBCP。该交叉点在单粒子水平上被本征原子自旋轨道耦合直接打开能隙，而底层的能带反转自然地保护所得拓扑能隙免受其他相互作用驱动的不稳定性影响。

Result: 该机制表明现有QBCP方案的局限性并非其固有特性，而是源于具体实现方式。进一步建议MNX₂（M=Ni、Pd、Pt；N=Nb、Ta；X=S、Se、Te）单层化合物作为本征实现该机制的现实材料体系。

Conclusion: 这些发现为在关联材料中实现鲁棒的QAH相提供了一条具体途径，通过能带反转机制保护拓扑能隙免受竞争序影响，从而有望在高温下实现稳定的量子反常霍尔效应。

Abstract: The realization of robust quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) phases at elevated temperatures remains a central challenge in condensed matter physics. While quadratic band crossing points (QBCP) provide a promising route towards QAH states, existing proposals are largely confined to idealized models or hindered by interaction-driven competing orders. Here, we demonstrate that these limitations are not intrinsic to QBCP but arise from their specific implementation. We propose a general mechanism where band inversion between a symmetry-protected orbital doublet (e.g. $d_{xz},d_{yz}$) and an isolated orbital (e.g. $d_{z^2}$)-generically generates a QBCP with opposite curvature. This crossing is directly gapped at the single-particle level by intrinsic atomic spin-orbit coupling, while the underlying band inversion naturally shields the resulting topological gap against other interaction-driven instabilities. We further suggest monolayer compounds $MNX_2$ ($M$= Ni, Pd, Pt; $N$= Nb, Ta; $X$= S, Se, Te) as a realistic material class that intrinsically realizes this mechanism. These findings provide a concrete pathway toward robust QAH phases in correlated materials.

Abstract: The quest for quantum ground states beyond the conventional Fermi-liquid paradigm remains a central challenge in many-body physics. The ferromagnetic Kondo effect represents a particularly intriguing case: an exotic variant of the Kondo effect in which an asymptotically free spin gives rise to singular Fermi-liquid behavior. Despite its theoretical importance, this regime has long eluded experimental observation owing to its subtle spectroscopic signatures, vanishingly small energy scales, and strict symmetry constraints in conventional nanostructures. Here, we demonstrate the coexistence of the ferromagnetic and overscreened Kondo effects within a single molecular spin system$\unicode{x2014}$a triangulene dimer comprising spin-1 and spin-1/2 units adsorbed on a metal surface. Low-temperature scanning tunneling spectroscopy reveals characteristic signatures of singular Fermi-liquid behavior, which are fully supported by many-body calculations. The unique molecular design provides intrinsic control over spin configuration and coupling asymmetry, allowing distinct many-body regimes to be accessed within the same platform. Our results establish a robust strategy for realizing non-Fermi-liquid physics at the atomic scale and demonstrate that ferromagnetic Kondo behavior can not only be observed but also deliberately engineered in molecular systems.

TL;DR: 构建了一个由弱耦合Rashba纳米线阵列组成的三维螺旋二阶拓扑超导体模型，在特定参数区间内，体态和表面态均有能隙，但沿一维铰链闭合路径存在一对无能隙的螺旋$\mathbb{Z}_{2q}$ parafermionic模式（q为奇数）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维螺旋二阶拓扑超导体的构建及其拓扑边界态特性，特别关注在体态和表面态均有能隙的情况下，一维铰链上出现的特殊parafermionic模式。

Method: 通过构建由弱耦合Rashba纳米线阵列组成的模型，分析参数区间以确定体态和表面态能隙的存在条件，同时研究铰链模式的精确轨迹如何由线间耦合的层级结构和样品边界终止决定。

Result: 在特定参数区间内，系统体态和表面态均具有能隙，但沿一维铰链闭合路径存在一对无能隙的螺旋$\mathbb{Z}_{2q}$ parafermionic模式（q为奇数）。在非相互作用极限q=1时，系统具有无能隙的Majorana铰链模式。

Conclusion: 成功构建了三维螺旋二阶拓扑超导体模型，揭示了在体态和表面态均有能隙的情况下，一维铰链上可以存在特殊的parafermionic拓扑边界态，其具体轨迹由耦合层级和边界终止条件决定。

Abstract: We construct a model of a three-dimensional helical second-order topological superconductor formed by an array of weakly coupled Rashba nanowires. We identify the parameter regime in which there are energy gaps in both the bulk and surface energy spectra, while a pair of gapless helical $\mathbb{Z}_{2q}$ parafermionic modes (with $q$ being an odd integer) remains gapless along a closed path of one-dimensional hinges. The precise trajectory of these hinge modes is dictated by the hierarchy of interwire couplings and the boundary termination of the sample. In the noninteracting limit $q= 1$, the system hosts gapless Majorana hinge modes.

### [56] [Topological Magneto-Optical Switching in Even-Layered MnBi$_2$Te$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07315)
*Shahid Sattar,Roman Stepanov,C. M. Canali*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论计算揭示了MnBi₂Te₄薄膜中拓扑磁光开关的厚度依赖性机制，发现通过调控最外层七重层自旋排列可实现从轴子绝缘体到陈绝缘体的拓扑相变，并伴随磁光响应的量子化切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnBi₂Te₄薄膜为调控磁性、拓扑和磁光响应提供了独特平台，但层厚依赖的拓扑磁光开关机制尚需系统研究。本文旨在探索偶数层MnBi₂Te₄薄膜中拓扑磁光开关的物理机制及其厚度依赖性。

Method: 采用低能耦合狄拉克锥模型结合基于Wannier函数的紧束缚哈密顿量，该哈密顿量源自第一性原理计算，用于研究偶数层MnBi₂Te₄薄膜的拓扑磁光开关行为。

Result: 最外层七重层的相对自旋排列主要控制总陈数、光学电导率和磁光响应。6-SL薄膜中，最外层自旋排列从反平行变为平行时，系统从轴子绝缘体（C=0，法拉第旋转消失）切换到陈绝缘体（C=1，量子化磁光响应）。12-SL薄膜支持更高陈数相（C=2），低频法拉第旋转加倍。

Conclusion: 研究提供了厚度依赖的多级磁光开关路径，并确立了磁光谱学作为探测MnBi₂Te₄薄膜表面磁性和拓扑序的直接手段，为拓扑磁光器件的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ (MBT) thin films provide a unique material platform in which magnetism, topology, and magneto-optical (MO) response can be tuned through layer-thickness and relative spin alignments. In this work, using a low-energy coupled Dirac cone model together with Wannier-based tight-binding Hamiltonian derived from \textit{ab-initio} calculations, we investigate topological MO switching in even-layered MBT films. We argue that the relative spin alignment of the outermost septuple-layers (SL) mainly controls the total Chern number, optical conductibility, and consequently, the MO response. For a 6-SL MBT thin film, we found that reversing the outermost-SL alignments from antiparallel to parallel switches the system from axion insulating state with $C=0$ and vanishing Faraday rotation to a Chern insulating state with $C=1$ and a quantized MO response, irrespective of $PT$-symmetry and net magnetization. Increasing thickness reveals an additional regime: while 8-SL MBT hosts only $C=0$ and $1$ states, a 12-SL MBT film supports a higher Chern number phase with $C=2$ with a doubled low-frequency Faraday rotation. Our results provide a thickness-dependent route to multilevel MO switching and establish MO spectroscopy as a direct probe of surface magnetism and topological order in MBT thin films.

### [57] [Directional Andreev-Reflection Signatures of Inter-Orbital Pairing in Sr$_2$RuO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06706)
*G. Csire,Y. Fukaya,M. Cuoco,Y. Tanaka,R. K. Kremer,A. S. Gibbs,G. A. Ummarino,D. Daghero,R. S. Gonnelli*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究发现Sr₂RuO₄超导体表现出与传统二维系统相反的各向异性行为：垂直于面外方向的表面出现显著安德烈夫束缚态，而面内边缘的带隙内谱特征减弱，这可由超导配对的轨道间特性解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统准二维超导系统中，安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states, ABS）通常出现在面内边缘，而垂直于面外方向的表面保持完全带隙，这种方向各向异性长期作为约束配对对称性的关键范式。本研究旨在探索Sr₂RuO₄是否遵循这一传统行为模式。

Method: 采用边缘和表面敏感光谱学技术，观测不同方向表面的谱特征。结合从头计算（ab initio）和模型计算，包括Sr₂RuO₄/Ag界面重构分析，研究轨道间配对通道对谱响应的贡献。

Result: 观察到Sr₂RuO₄表现出与传统行为相反的异常各向异性：垂直于面外方向的表面出现显著的带隙内安德烈夫束缚态，而面内边缘的带隙内谱特征强度降低。研究表明这种异常各向异性可能源于超导配对的轨道间特性。

Conclusion: 轨道间配对通道（包括偶宇称和奇宇称）自然产生稳健的表面安德烈夫束缚态，同时抑制平面边缘模式，并能解释水平线节点的出现。研究结果强调了轨道间关联在塑造谱响应中的可能作用，并为Sr₂RuO₄中超导序参量的结构提供了约束条件。

Abstract: Unconventional superconductivity in quasi--two-dimensional systems is commonly identified through the emergence of Andreev bound states (ABS) at in-plane edges, while surfaces perpendicular to out-of-plane direction remain fully gapped due to weak interlayer coherence. This directional anisotropy has long served as a key paradigm for constraining pairing symmetries. Here, we show that Sr$_2$RuO$_4$ exhibits a striking reversal of this behavior. Using edge- and surface-sensitive spectroscopy, we observe pronounced in-gap ABS at surfaces perpendicular to the out-of-plane direction, whereas in-plane edges exhibit a reduced intensity of the in-gap spectral features. We show that this anomalous anisotropy can arise from the inter-orbital character of the superconducting pairing. Both even- and odd-parity inter-orbital pairing channels naturally generate robust surface ABS while suppressing planar edge modes and can also provide a mechanism for the appearance of a horizontal line node. Supported by \textit{ab initio} and model calculations, including Sr$_2$RuO$_4$/Ag interface reconstructions, our results highlight the possible role of inter-orbital correlations in shaping the spectroscopic response and provide constraints on the structure of the superconducting order parameter in Sr$_2$RuO$_4$.

</details>

Method: 研究基于第一性原理计算确定非谐晶格势，并在此势场上模拟光诱导声子动力学。通过选择性激发适当的红外活性声子模式（infrared-active phonon mode）来调控结构参数。

Result: 研究发现，当选择性激发适当的红外活性声子模式时，铁基超导体中的关键结构参数——阴离子高度h（anion height）会接近其理想值。这一结果表明通过非线性声子学概念调控晶体结构的可行性。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了基于非线性声子学概念调控铁基超导体晶体结构并增强超导性的可能性，为超导材料的光控调控提供了新思路。

Abstract: Nonlinear phononics provides a route to control crystal structures through light-induced phonon excitation. In this study, we apply nonlinear phononics to an iron-based superconductor, LaFeAsO, with the aim of tuning its crystal structure toward the ideal one to enhance superconductivity. We simulate light-induced phonon dynamics on the anharmonic lattice potential determined by first-principles calculations. We find that the anion height $h$, a key structural parameter in iron-based superconductors, approaches its ideal value when an appropriate infrared-active phonon mode is selectively excited. This result suggests the possibility of controlling crystal structures and enhancing superconductivity in iron-based superconductors based on the concept of nonlinear phononics.

### [59] [Influence of the Ortho-II superstructure in the YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ Orthorhombic phase after annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07060)
*Roberto F. Luccas,Lorenzo Gallo,Cesar E. Sobrero,Jorge A. Malarría*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验探讨了YBa₂Cu₃O₇₋δ（YBCO）材料中氧原子有序性对正交相最终结构的影响，揭示了Ortho-II超结构在低温氧合过程中的关键作用及其对最终衍射图谱的印记效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究YBCO材料中氧原子有序性对其正交相最终结构的影响，特别是Ortho-II超结构在相变过程中的作用机制。通过分析不同氧合条件下材料的结构演变，揭示氧原子有序化对最终材料性能的影响。

Method: 采用等温氧合（isothermal oxygenation）方法，从非氧合状态（δ=1）开始，在300-800°C温度范围内对YBCO粉末进行氧合处理。使用热重分析天平监测质量变化，并进行差热分析（differential thermal analysis, DTA）。通过X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）研究不同条件下获得的材料结构差异。

Result: 实验观察到YBCO材料中的四方-正交（Tetragonal-Orthorhombic, T-O）相变，并在两种不同条件下获得氧合材料：直接转变为Ortho-I超结构，以及通过Ortho-II超结构进行转变。X射线衍射显示两种条件下获得的衍射图谱存在差异。在低温氧合（T_O < 400°C）条件下，T-O相变通过Ortho-II超结构区域进行，导致氧原子在材料中逐步有序化。

Conclusion: 研究提出Ortho-II超结构在低温氧合过程中对氧原子有序化起关键作用，这种有序化在YBCO材料的最终结构中留下印记，即使材料已超出Ortho-II超结构的稳定区域。该机制解释了不同氧合条件下获得的衍射图谱差异。

Abstract: Based on experimental results, this work proposes the influence of the Oxygen order present in the Ortho-II superstructure of YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ (YBCO), on the final ordering of Oxygens in its Orthorhombic phase for $δ$ $\approx$ 0. Isothermal oxygenation (oxyg) of YBCO powder material is performed, starting from non-oxygenated material ($δ$ $=$ 1) and evolving until saturation in an oxygen atmosphere. The oxyg process is carried out within a temperature range from 300 $^o$C to 800 $^o$C (300 $^o$C $<$ T$_O$ $<$ 800 $^o$C). During the oxyg process, and using a thermogravimetric balance, the evolution of mass (m) and the differential thermal analysis (DTA) of the material are monitored with respect to an inert reference material subjected to the same conditions as the YBCO powder.
  These results allow observation of the Tetragonal-Orthorhombic (T-O) transition occurring in the YBCO material. From these results, oxygenated YBCO material is obtained by working at different temperatures and under two different conditions: through a direct T-O transition into the Ortho-I superstructure, and by passing through the Ortho-II superstructure along the transition. The material obtained under these two conditions is studied by X-Ray diffraction, revealing differences in the resulting diffractograms. Furthermore, we propose that, for low values of T$_O$ (T$_O$ $<$ 400 $^o$C), the T-O transition proceeds through the region of the phase diagram where the Ortho-II superstructure is present, leading to progressive ordering of the Oxygen atoms within the material. This ordering leaves a fingerprint in the final configuration reached by the YBCO material, even beyond the region where the Ortho-II superstructure is stable. Finally, we suggest that this mechanism is responsible for the differences observed between the diffractograms obtained under both conditions.

</details>


### [60] [Perpendicular electric field induced $s^\pm$-wave to $d$-wave superconducting transition in thin film La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07185)
*Yongping Wei,Xun Liu,Fan Yang,Mi Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过动力学团簇量子蒙特卡洛计算研究了电场调控下双层哈伯德模型的配对对称性演化，发现电场会抑制dz²轨道产生的s±波配对，并诱导向dx²-y²轨道d波配对的转变，后者随电场呈现穹顶状行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Ruddlesden-Popper双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中垂直电场可能改变超导性质的启发，研究电场对双层哈伯德模型中配对对称性的调控作用。旨在理解电场强度变化对未掺杂、空穴掺杂和电子掺杂区域配对对称性的影响。

Method: 采用动力学团簇量子蒙特卡洛（dynamical cluster quantum Monte Carlo）方法研究不平衡的双轨道双层哈伯德模型（two-orbital bilayer Hubbard model）。通过大规模多体计算分析电场诱导的配对对称性及其随电场强度的演化。

Result: 研究发现dz²轨道产生的s±波配对（s±-wave pairing）被电场抑制，同时发生从s±波到d波配对（d-wave pairing）的对称性转变。这一转变由层间dz²轨道失配和电子向dx²-y²轨道转移驱动。dx²-y²轨道产生的d波配对随电场呈现穹顶状行为（dome-like behavior）。

Conclusion: 大规模多体计算证实了先前弱耦合方法的预期，为Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐的超导机制提供了深入见解。电场通过调控轨道占据和层间耦合，能够显著改变体系的配对对称性。

Abstract: Inspired by the possibility that superconducting properties may be altered by applying a perpendicular electric field in the Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, we investigated the imbalanced two-orbital bilayer Hubbard model using dynamical cluster quantum Monte Carlo calculations. Focusing on the pairing symmetries induced by the electric field and their evolution with field strength in the undoped, hole-doped, and electron-doped regimes, we found that the $s^\pm$-wave pairing originating from the $d_{z^2}$ orbital is suppressed; while a pairing symmetry transition from $s^\pm$-wave to $d$-wave pairing occurs, driven by the interlayer $d_{z^2}$ orbital mismatch and the transfer of electrons into the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital under the applied electric field. Intriguingly, the $d$-wave pairing arising from the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital exhibits dome-like behavior with the electric field. Our large-scale many-body calculations align with the previous expectation from weak-coupling methods and provide further insight into the superconducting mechanism in RP nickelates.

### [61] [Identifying Topological Invariants of Non-Hermitian Systems via Domain-Adaptive Multimodal Model for Mathematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06998)
*Jiuchun Meng,Lichao Sun,Xiumei Wang,Dandan Zhu,Xingping Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.other

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一个由领域自适应多模态数学模型组成的框架，用于识别拓扑不变量（topological invariants）。该模型将哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）在动量空间的本征值（eigenvalues）和本征向量（eigenvectors）作为两种输入模态。模型以Qwen Math作为多模态模型的主干，显著增强了其数学理解能力和计算精度。

Result: 研究结果展示了该框架在识别拓扑不变量方面的有效性。该方法为未来通过大型语言模型（LLM）研究拓扑不变量识别提供了一个范式。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的基于领域自适应多模态数学模型的框架，为利用大型语言模型（LLM）解决高维非厄米趋肤效应中的拓扑不变量识别问题提供了新的解决方案。该框架整合了Qwen Math作为主干，有效提升了数学理解和计算能力。

Abstract: The emergence of the non-Hermitian skin effect, distinguished by the exponential localization of bulk states onto boundaries in open systems, has redefined the conventional band theory. It can be established through the generalized Brillouin zone framework, the amoeba formulation or generalized Fermi surface in the different dimensions. However, its algorithmic implementation is still challenging in the high-dimensional cases. The large language models (LLM), functioning as the new paradigm in machine learning, can help to tack scientific problems. Here, we propose a framework composed by domain-adaptive Multimodal model for mathematics to identify topological invariants. We feed the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the Hamiltonian in momentum space into our model as two input modalities. The Qwen Math is integrated as the backbone of the multimodal model, significantly enhancing its mathematical understanding capability and computational precision. Our results provide a paradigm for future studies on topological invariants identification via LLMs.

### [62] [Spin-Valley Relaxation of Rydberg Excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07280)
*V. Jindal,K. Mourzidis,M. Semina,D. Lagarde,A. Balocchi,P. Renucci,T. Boulier,T. Taniguchi,K. Watanabe,M. Glazov,X. Marie*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究直接测量了WSe2单层中里德伯激子（Rydberg excitons）的自旋弛豫，发现高激发态激子具有接近90%的光致发光圆偏振度，且自旋弛豫时间随主量子数增加而显著延长，从1s激子的~2ps增至3s激子的~75ps。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 里德伯激子（Rydberg excitons）具有大空间扩展性和减小的电子-空穴重叠，其自旋-谷动力学应与基态激子不同。研究旨在直接测量高质量WSe2单层中里德伯激子的自旋弛豫特性。

Method: 采用连续波和时间分辨的光学取向实验（optical orientation experiments）测量里德伯激子的自旋弛豫。通过基于电子-空穴交换驱动自旋弛豫的微观模型进行定量分析。

Result: 激发态激子表现出异常大的光致发光圆偏振度（photoluminescence circular polarization），3s态接近90%。时间分辨测量显示自旋弛豫时间随主量子数（principal quantum number）增加而显著延长，从1s激子的~2ps到3s激子的~75ps。

Conclusion: 微观模型定量再现了观测趋势，证明里德伯激子能够在二维半导体中实现可调谐的自旋-谷动力学（spin-valley dynamics）。

Abstract: Rydberg excitons, characterized by large spatial extension and reduced electron-hole overlap, must have a spin-valley dynamics different from that of ground state excitons. Here we report a direct measurement of spin relaxation of Rydberg excitons in high-quality WSe2 monolayer using continuous-wave and time-resolved optical orientation experiments. Excited excitonic states exhibit exceptionally large photoluminescence circular polarization, approaching 90% for the 3s state. Time-resolved measurements reveal a strong increase of the spin relaxation time with the principal quantum number, from ~2 ps for the 1s exciton to ~75 ps for the 3s exciton. A microscopic model based on electron-hole exchange-driven spin relaxation quantitatively reproduces the observed trend, demonstrating that Rydberg excitons enable tunable spin-valley dynamics in two-dimensional semiconductors.

### [63] [SMT-AD: a scalable quantum-inspired anomaly detection approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06265)
*Apimuk Sornsaeng,Si Min Chan,Wenxuan Zhang,Swee Liang Wong,Joshua Lim,Dario Poletti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SMT-AD的量子启发张量网络异常检测方法，该方法基于多分辨率张量叠加，具有高度并行性，在标准数据集上实现了与现有基线方法竞争的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子启发的张量网络算法已被证明是机器学习任务（包括异常检测）的有效且高效模型。本文旨在开发一种高度并行化的量子启发方法，以改进异常检测性能。

Method: 提出SMT-AD（Superposition of Multiresolution Tensors for Anomaly Detection）方法，基于键维数为1的矩阵乘积算子（matrix product operators）叠加，通过傅里叶辅助特征嵌入（Fourier-assisted feature embedding）转换输入数据。可学习参数数量随特征大小、嵌入分辨率和矩阵乘积算子结构中的附加组件数量线性增长。

Result: 在包括信用卡交易在内的标准数据集上成功实现了异常检测。即使采用最小配置，该方法也能在与已建立的异常检测基线方法的比较中达到竞争性性能。此外，通过突出最相关的输入特征，该方法提供了一种直接的方式来减少模型权重甚至提升性能。

Conclusion: SMT-AD是一种有效的量子启发张量网络异常检测方法，具有高度并行性、线性参数增长和竞争性性能，同时提供了模型权重优化和特征重要性分析的直接途径。

Abstract: Quantum-inspired tensor networks algorithms have shown to be effective and efficient models for machine learning tasks, including anomaly detection. Here, we propose a highly parallelizable quantum-inspired approach which we call SMT-AD from Superposition of Multiresolution Tensors for Anomaly Detection. It is based upon the superposition of bond-dimension-1 matrix product operators to transform the input data with Fourier-assisted feature embedding, where the number of learnable parameters grows linearly with feature size, embedding resolutions, and the number of additional components in the matrix product operators structure. We demonstrate successful anomaly detection when applied to standard datasets, including credit card transactions, and find that, even with minimal configurations, it achieves competitive performance against established anomaly detection baselines. Furthermore, it provides a straightforward way to reduce the weight of the model and even improve the performance by highlighting the most relevant input features.

</details>

### [64] [Optoelectronic and Thermoelectric Properties of High-Performance AlSb Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06294)
*Dilshod Nematov,Amondulloi Burkhonzoda,Iskandar Raufov,Sherali Murodzoda,Saidjafar Murodzoda,Sakhidod Sattorzoda,Anushervon Ashurov,Makhsud Barot Islomzoda,Kholmirzo Kholmurodov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算系统研究了立方相(F-43m)和六方相(P63mc)铝锑化物(AlSb)的光电与热电性质。两种相均为准直接带隙半导体，六方相因对称性降低和带隙变窄而表现出增强的低能光吸收，立方相则因载流子迁移率更高而具有更高的功率因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在全面探究铝锑化物(AlSb)在不同晶体结构下的光电与热电性质，特别关注锑(Sb)半核d态电子对能带边缘电子结构的贡献，这一效应在传统泛函中难以准确描述，而杂化方法可能高估其影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算方法，结构优化使用SCAN泛函，电子与光学性质评估采用改进的Becke-Johnson势结合Hubbard修正(mBJ+U)，该方法能最佳描述带边电子结构并准确处理Sb半核d态的贡献。

Result: 立方相和六方相AlSb均为准直接带隙半导体，计算带隙分别为1.71 eV和1.50 eV，与实验数据吻合良好。光学响应显示在可见光和紫外区域有强吸收，六方相因对称性降低和带隙变窄而表现出增强的低能光吸收。热电分析显示两相均具有大的负塞贝克系数，功率因子随载流子浓度单调增加，立方相因载流子迁移率更高而功率因子更大，六方相则因热导率降低而在高温下具有更好的热电性能。

Conclusion: AlSb是一种多功能半导体，其光电和热电性质可通过晶体结构调控。研究结果强调了准确处理Sb d电子效应对于可靠预测材料性质的重要性，为AlSb在光电器件和热电转换领域的应用提供了理论指导。

Abstract: This study presents a comprehensive first-principles investigation of the optoelectronic and thermoelectric properties of aluminum antimonide (AlSb) in its cubic (F-43m) and hexagonal (P63mc) phases. Structural optimization was performed using the SCAN functional, and all electronic and optical properties were evaluated using the modified Becke-Johnson potential combined with the Hubbard correction (mBJ+U), which best describes the band-edge electronic structure, explicitly accounting for the contribution of the d-states of the Sb half-core, which cannot be adequately accounted for by conventional functionals and may be overestimated by hybrid approaches. Both AlSb phases are found to be quasi-direct bandgap semiconductors, with calculated band gaps of 1.71 eV for the cubic phase and 1.50 eV for the hexagonal phase, in good agreement with available experimental data. The optical response reveals strong absorption in the visible and ultraviolet regions, moderate reflectivity, and high refractive indices, indicating pronounced light-matter interaction characteristic of III-V semiconductors. The hexagonal phase exhibits enhanced low-energy optical absorption due to its reduced symmetry and narrower band gap. Thermoelectric analysis demonstrates large negative Seebeck coefficients, thermally activated carrier generation, and a monotonic increase of the power factor with carrier concentration for both phases. The cubic phase shows higher power factor values due to enhanced carrier mobility, whereas the hexagonal phase benefits from reduced thermal conductivity, which is favorable for thermoelectric performance at elevated temperatures. These results establish AlSb as a multifunctional semiconductor with tunable optoelectronic and thermoelectric properties and highlight the importance of an accurate treatment of Sb d-electron effects for reliable property prediction.

</details>


### [65] [Grafted Low-Leakage Si/AlN p-n Diodes Enabled by Fluorinated AlN Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06359)
*Yi Lu,Tsung-Han Tsai,Qingxiao Wang,Haicheng Cao,Jie Zhou,You Jin Koo,Chenyu Wang,Yang Liu,Yueyue Hao,Michael Eller,Connor Bailey,Stephanie Liu,Nicholas J. Tanen,Zhiyuan Liu,Mingtao Nong,Robert M. Jacobberger,Tien Khee Ng,Katherine Fountaine,Vincent Gambin,Boon S. Ooi,Xiaohang Li,Zhenqiang Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于氟化诱导AlFx形成与SiNx钝化相结合的界面工程方法，用于抑制通过半导体接枝技术制备的p-Si/n-AlN异质结二极管中的缺陷辅助泄漏电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超宽带隙（ultrawide-bandgap）AlN是下一代功率电子器件的有前途材料，但其实际应用受到不稳定表面化学性质和高p型掺杂剂激活能的阻碍。特别是用于在n型AlN上形成低电阻接触所需的高温快速热退火（rapid thermal annealing, RTA）会导致形成厚且有缺陷的表面氧化物，从而降低异质结性能。

Method: 采用低损伤伪原子层刻蚀（pseudo-atomic layer etching）工艺去除RTA诱导的氧化物并恢复接近化学计量比的AlN表面。随后进行XeF2处理形成超薄AlFx层，该层在p-Si纳米膜集成前通过原子层沉积（atomic-layer-deposited）SiNx覆盖层进行稳定化。

Result: 电学测量显示，与未处理或氧化物去除的AlN表面相比，工程化的AlFx/SiNx界面将反向泄漏电流降低了数个数量级，同时保持了正向传导特性。温度依赖性分析表明普尔-弗兰克尔发射（Poole-Frenkel emission）被强烈抑制，泄漏起始点向更高反向偏压移动，最终受限于AlN体晶体质量。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了AlFx/SiNx钝化作为稳定AlN界面和实现低泄漏超宽带隙异质结器件的有效策略。X射线光电子能谱（X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy）和透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy）证实了Al-F键的形成、Al-O含量的减少以及薄界面SiOx/SiON层的存在。

Abstract: Ultrawide-bandgap AlN is a promising material for next-generation power electronics; however, its practical implementation is hindered by unstable surface chemistry and the high activation energy of p-type dopants. In particular, high-temperature rapid thermal annealing (RTA), required for forming low-resistance contacts on n-type AlN, leads to the formation of thick and defective surface oxides that degrade heterojunction performance.
  In this work, we present an interface engineering approach based on fluorination-induced AlFx formation combined with SiNx passivation to suppress defect-assisted leakage in p-Si/n-AlN heterojunction diodes fabricated via semiconductor grafting. A low-damage pseudo-atomic layer etching process is employed to remove RTA-induced oxides and restore a near-stoichiometric AlN surface. Subsequent XeF2 treatment forms an ultrathin AlFx layer, which is stabilized by an atomic-layer-deposited SiNx capping layer prior to p-Si nanomembrane integration.
  Electrical measurements show that the engineered AlFx/SiNx interface reduces reverse leakage current by several orders of magnitude compared to untreated or oxide-removed AlN surfaces, while preserving forward conduction characteristics. Temperature-dependent analysis indicates strong suppression of Poole-Frenkel emission and a shift of leakage onset to higher reverse bias, ultimately limited by bulk AlN crystal quality. X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy and transmission electron microscopy confirm the formation of Al-F bonds, reduced Al-O content, and the presence of a thin interfacial SiOx/SiON layer.
  These results establish AlFx/SiNx passivation as an effective strategy for stabilizing AlN interfaces and enabling low-leakage ultrawide-bandgap heterojunction devices.

</details>


### [66] [Influence of Manganese Content on Plastic Deformation Mechanisms in Polycrystalline α-Ti-Mn Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06360)
*G. Marković,M. Fedorov,M. Sokića,K. Frydrych,F. J. Dominguez-Gutierrez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究采用分子动力学模拟探究锰含量对α-Ti-Mn合金塑性变形机制的影响，发现增加锰含量会提高应力水平并增强抗塑性变形能力，同时改变位错活动和缺陷演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钛合金因其高比强度、耐腐蚀性和生物相容性在航空航天、生物医学和能源领域广泛应用。具有六方密堆积晶体结构的α-钛合金表现出由晶体滑移和缺陷演化控制的特征变形机制，需要研究合金元素（如锰）含量对其塑性变形机制的影响。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟研究多晶α-Ti-2Mn和α-Ti-4Mn（原子百分比）合金。原子模型在室温下以10^9 s^-1的应变速率进行单轴加载，通过应力-应变行为、结构演化、位错成核与相互作用以及局部变形场分析来评估力学响应。

Result: α-Ti-Mn合金的塑性变形主要由六方密堆积晶格内的位错成核及其后续演化主导。增加锰含量导致更高的应力水平和增强的抗塑性变形能力，同时伴随位错活动和缺陷演化的变化。

Conclusion: 锰含量显著影响α-Ti-Mn合金的塑性变形机制，更高的锰含量通过改变位错动力学和缺陷演化过程来增强材料的力学性能。

Abstract: Titanium alloys are widely used in aerospace, biomedical, and energy applications owing to their high specific strength, corrosion resistance, and biocompatibility. Among them, $α$-titanium alloys with a hexagonal close-packed (hcp) crystal structure exhibit characteristic deformation mechanisms governed by crystallographic slip and defect evolution. In this study, the influence of manganese content on the plastic deformation mechanisms of polycrystalline $α$-Ti-2Mn and $α$-Ti-4Mn (at.%) alloys is investigated using molecular dynamics simulations. Atomistic models were subjected to uniaxial loading at room temperature at a strain rate of 10$^9$ s$^{-1}$. The mechanical response was evaluated through stress-strain behavior, structural evolution, dislocation nucleation and interaction, and analysis of the local deformation field. Plastic deformation in these $α$-Ti-Mn alloys is dominated by dislocation nucleation and their subsequent evolution within the hcp lattice. Increasing Mn content leads to higher stress levels and enhanced resistance to plastic deformation, accompanied by changes in dislocation activity and defect evolution.

</details>


### [67] [Study of the Nonlinear Dependence of Anomalous Hall Conductivity on Magnetization in Weak Itinerant Ferromagnet ZrZn2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06441)
*Surasree Sadhukhan,Stepan S. Tsirkin,Yaroslav Zhumagulov,Igor. I. Mazin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过直接计算检验了在单域巡游铁磁体ZrZn₂中反常霍尔效应（AHE）与磁化强度的线性关系，发现在零磁化极限下线性关系成立，但在约0.4 μB/Zr的小磁矩下完全失效甚至符号反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect, AHE）与净磁化强度的线性关系长期存在误解，特别是在传统铁磁体中这种关系被理解为畴布居效应。本研究旨在检验在单域（single-domain）巡游铁磁体（itinerant ferromagnet）中，这种线性关系能在多大程度上成立，这是最接近Karplus和Luttinger原始分析的情况。

Method: 采用直接计算方法，使用Karplus-Luttinger公式对原型巡游铁磁体ZrZn₂中的反常霍尔效应进行计算，特别关注零磁化极限和不同磁矩条件下的行为。

Result: 计算显示在零磁化极限（M→0）时线性关系成立，但在约0.4 μB/Zr的小磁矩下，该线性关系完全失效，甚至出现符号反转（flips the sign）。

Conclusion: 反常霍尔效应与磁化强度的线性关系仅在特定极限条件下成立，在更现实的磁矩条件下会完全失效，这澄清了对AHE与磁化线性关系的误解，并验证了Karplus-Luttinger理论在单域巡游铁磁体中的适用性。

Abstract: As opposed to the ordinary Hall effect, the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) remained unexplained for decades, and, amazingly, some misconceptions have survived even now, in particular, the claim that AHE is linearly related to the net magnetization. Karplus and Luttinger provided a quantum-mechanical explanation of AHE by explicitly including the SOC and the Berry curvature of electronic bands. They did address the question of linearity, but only in the relatively uncommon limit of the exchange coupling smaller than SOC. Now the linear relation in traditional ferromagnets is understood as a domain population effect: both AHE and magnetization are independently proportional to the domain disbalance. In this connection, it is interesting to check to what extent this relation will hold in {\em single-domain} itinerant ferromagnet, the closest case to that analyzed by Karplus and Luttinger? We answer this question by direct calculations, using the Karplus-Luttinger formula, of AHE in a prototypical itinerant ferromagnet, ZrZn$_2$. We show that in the zero-magnetization limit, $M\rightarrow 0$, the linear relation hold, but at rather small moments of $\sim 0.4\ μ_B$/Zr breaks down completely and even flips the sign.

</details>


### [68] [Volume Collapse Without a Structural Transition in Shock-Compressed FeO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06768)
*C. Crépisson,T. Stevens,M. Fitzgerald,C. Camarda,P. G. Heighway,D. Peake,D. McGonegle,A. Descamps,A. Amouretti,D. A. Chin,K. K. Alaa El-Din,S. Azadi,E. Brambrink,K. Buakor,L. Pennacchioni,M. Sieber,A. Coutinho Dutra,J. Hernandez Gordillo,K. Yamamoto,J. -A. Hernandez,R. Torchio,T. Tschentscher,Y. Wang,H. Taylor,J. Pintor,O. S. Humphries,M. Andrzejewski,C. Baehtz,E. Barraud,A. B. Belonoshko,D. S. Bespalov,E. Boulard,R. Briggs,D. Cabaret,O. Castelnau,A. Chakraborti,J. Chantel,D. M. Cheshire,G. Collins,T. E. Cowan,Y. J. Deng,S. Di Dio Cafiso,L. Dresselhaus-Marais,X. Fang,A. Forte,S. Galitskiy,E. Galtier,T. Gawne,H. Ginestet,F. Hanby,A. Hari,N. J. Hartley,H. Höppner,N. Jaisle,J. Kim,Z. Konôpková,A. Krygier,J. Kuhlke,C. M. Lonsdale,S-N. Luo,J. Lütgert,M. Masruri,E. E. McBride,J. D. McHardy,M. I. McMahon,R. S. McWilliams,S. Merkel,T. Michelat,J-P. Naedler,B. Nagler,M. Nakatsutsumi,A-M. Norton,I. K. Ocampo,I. I. Oleynik,C. Otzen,N. Ozaki,C. A. J. Palmer,S. E. Parsons,A. Pelka,A. Phelipeau,C. Prescher,N. Pulver,C. Prestwood,C. Qu,D. Ranjan,R. Redmer,C. Sahle,A. A. Sanjuan Mora,S. Schumacher,J-P. Schwinkendorf,N. Sévelin-Radiguet,G. Shoulga,R. F. Smith,S. Singh,C. N. Somarathna,M. Stevenson,C. V. Storm,C. Strohm,T-A. Suer,M. X. Tang,A. Tipeev,M. Toncian,T. Toncian,U. Trdan,J. D. Tunacao,J. D. Umpleby-Thorp,L. Wang,M. Wilke,U. Zastrau,G. Gregori,D. Polsin,C. Sternemann,J. S. Wark,T. M. Hutchinson,C. McGuire,S. Pandolfi,A. Sollier,A. Higginbotham,T. R. Preston,D. Kraus,J. H. Eggert,K. Appel,M. Harmand,S. M. Vinko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: FeO在31-199 GPa激光冲击压缩下保持B1（岩盐）结构至191 GPa熔化边界，但在约60 GPa处观察到静态实验中未见的7-10%异常体积塌缩，被识别为FeO中的等结构高自旋到低自旋金属转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究FeO在激光驱动冲击压缩下的结构相变和电子态变化，特别是探索高压下可能存在的自旋转变现象，以补充静态压缩实验的发现。

Method: 采用X射线衍射（x-ray diffraction）和X射线发射光谱（x-ray emission spectroscopy）技术，在31-199 GPa压力范围内对FeO进行激光驱动冲击压缩（laser-driven shock compression）研究。

Result: FeO沿Hugoniot线保持B1（岩盐）结构至191 GPa熔化边界；在约60 GPa处观察到7-10%的异常体积塌缩（volume collapse），该现象在静态实验中未出现；X射线发射光谱在180 GPa直接证实了低自旋态（low-spin state）的存在。

Conclusion: FeO在约60 GPa处发生的异常体积塌缩被识别为等结构高自旋到低自旋金属转变（isostructural high-spin to low-spin metallic transition），这一动态压缩特有的现象揭示了FeO在高压下的电子结构演化。

Abstract: We report x-ray diffraction and emission spectroscopy of FeO under laser-driven shock compression between 31-199 GPa. FeO retains the B1 (rocksalt) structure along the Hugoniot to the melt boundary at 191 GPa. While the phase and volume are broadly consistent with results from static compression, we observe an anomalous 7-10% volume collapse around 60 GPa absent in static experiments. We identify this as an isostructural high-spin to low-spin metallic transition in FeO. The low-spin state is directly evidenced by x-ray emission spectroscopy at 180 GPa.

</details>


### [69] [Quantitative 3D Analysis of Porosity and Fractal Geometry in Electrochemically Etched Macroporous Silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06517)
*A. Ramírez-Porras,I. Prado,N. R. Schwarz,U. Steiner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过聚焦镓离子束扫描电子显微镜断层扫描技术，重构了电化学蚀刻大孔硅层的三维孔网络结构，发现基于二维图像的表面积孔隙率会系统性低估真实的三维体积孔隙率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大孔硅（macroporous silicon）因其巨大的内表面积和可调的孔结构而广泛应用于传感和光电子领域，但形态与功能之间的定量关联需要准确表征三维孔网络结构。

Method: 采用聚焦镓离子束扫描电子显微镜断层扫描（focused Ga+ ion beam scanning electron microscopy tomography）技术，重构电化学蚀刻大孔硅层的代表性体积，提取真实的三维孔隙率和表面积-体积比，并与二维SEM图像估计值进行比较。

Result: 研究结果表明，基于表面积的孔隙率（surface-based porosity）会系统性低估真实的体积孔隙率（volumetric porosity），这种差异源于孔隙的各向异性、分支和尺寸变异性。分形分析（fractal analysis）显示孔网络具有适度的几何复杂性，与电化学大孔形成机制一致。

Conclusion: 结果强调了直接三维表征对于可靠形态量化（morphological quantification）的重要性，并为解释大孔硅的结构趋势提供了稳健的分析框架。

Abstract: Macroporous silicon is widely employed in sensing and optoelectronic applications due to its large internal surface area and adjustable pore structure. However, quantitative correlations between morphology and functionality require accurately characterizing the three dimensional pore network. In this study, we used focused Ga+ ion beam scanning electron microscopy tomography to reconstruct representative volumes of electrochemically etched macroporous silicon layers. We extracted true three dimensional porosity and surface-to-volume ratios and compared them with two-dimensional estimates obtained from SEM images. Our results demonstrate that surface-based porosity systematically underestimates true volumetric porosity. These discrepancies arise from anisotropy, branching, and variability in pore size. Fractal analysis reveals that the pore network has moderate geometric complexity, consistent with electrochemical macropore formation mechanisms. The results highlight the importance of direct 3D characterization for reliable morphological quantification and provide a robust framework for interpreting structural trends in macroporous silicon.

</details>


### [70] [The effects of dispersion damping and three-body interactions for accurate layered-material exfoliation energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06539)
*Adrian F. Rumson,Kyle R. Bryenton,Erin R. Johnson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究评估了XDM(Z)阻尼函数在LM26层状材料基准测试中的性能，并展示了通过加入Axilrod-Teller-Muto三体相互作用项可进一步提升剥离能和晶格常数的计算精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状材料的剥离能和晶格常数精确预测依赖于对伦敦色散物理的正确描述。现代后验色散校正方法如XDM模型虽能捕捉长程渐进行为，但需要阻尼函数防止短程发散，因此需要评估新型Z阻尼函数的性能。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）中的交换空穴偶极矩（XDM）模型，对比评估了Beck-Johnson（BJ）阻尼函数和新型Z阻尼函数在LM26基准测试中的表现。该基准包含石墨、六方氮化硼、氧化铅和过渡金属二硫化物等材料，并进一步引入了Axilrod-Teller-Muto（ATM）三体相互作用项。

Result: XDM(Z)在LM26基准测试中首次得到评估，结果显示包含ATM三体相互作用项可同时提升XDM(BJ)和XDM(Z)计算的剥离能精度。该方法在半局域泛函中实现了迄今为止LM26基准的最佳性能。

Conclusion: XDM(Z)阻尼函数在层状材料建模中表现出色，结合ATM三体相互作用项可显著提升剥离能计算精度，为层状材料的精确模拟提供了更优的色散校正方案。

Abstract: Accurate predictions of exfoliation energies and lattice constants of layered materials hinge on a correct description of London dispersion physics. Modern a posteriori dispersion corrections in density-functional theory (DFT), such as the exchange-hole dipole moment (XDM) model, capture the proper asymptotic behaviour at long range while making use of damping functions to prevent unphysical divergence at short range. In the united-atom limit, the dispersion energy is damped to a finite, non-zero value by both the canonical Becke--Johnson (BJ) damping function and the new Z-damping function. XDM(BJ) has previously demonstrated exceptional accuracy for modelling layered materials, such as in the LM26 benchmark, which includes graphite, hexagonal boron nitride, lead(II) oxide, and transition-metal dichalcogenides. This work presents the first assessment of XDM(Z) on the same benchmark. We also show that inclusion of three-body interactions via the Axilrod--Teller--Muto (ATM) term further improves the computed exfoliation energies for both XDM(BJ) and XDM(Z), yielding the best performance achieved on LM26 using semi-local functionals to date.

### [71] [On the possibility of hybrid chalcogenide perovskite photovoltaics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06555)

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对A位点的一系列单价和二价有机阳离子进行筛选，评估其电子、光学和热力学性质。

This contrasts with the halide perovskites, for which hybrid organic-inorganic systems exhibit record performance. In this work, we assess the viability of hybrid chalcogenide perovskite absorbers using first-principles calculations. We screen a wide range of monovalent and divalent organic cations within the A-site to evaluate their electronic, optical, and thermodynamic properties. Our analysis reveals that the majority of candidates are structurally unstable; however, we identify the hydrazinium cation (\ce{N2H6^{2+}}) as a unique candidate that maintains a stable perovskite structure. Specifically, we identify \ce{N2H6ZrSe3} as the most promising candidate, exhibiting a quasi-direct band gap of \SI{1.31}{eV} and a theoretical maximum efficiency of \SI{24.5}{\percent} for a \SI{200}{\nm} thin film.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）和键价模型（bond-valence model），将化学键分解为共价和离子贡献，分别用量化指标：积分晶体轨道哈密顿布居总和（integrated crystal orbital Hamilton population, $S_c$）和马德隆能（Madelung energy, $S_i$）表示。

Abstract: We carry out bond-strength based analysis for the migration barrier ($E_{\rm B}$) of oxygen vacancies in rutile-type 3$d$ transition-metal dioxides by combining density-functional theory (DFT) and the bond-valence model. The covalent and ionic contributions to chemical bonding are explicitly decomposed and quantified by the sum of the integrated crystal orbital Hamilton population ($S_c$) and the Madelung energy ($S_i$), respectively. Both $S_c$ and $S_i$ exhibit strong correlations with the $E_{\rm B}$ from DFT ($E_{\rm B}^{\rm DFT}$), and their average $\bar{S}$ provides a reasonable estimate of $E_{\rm B}^{\rm DFT}$ across the oxide series. Inspired by the bond-valence model, two parameters are extracted by fitting to a large dataset of 3$d$ transition-metal dioxides. Our results show that using these parameters, $E_{\rm B}$ of oxygen vacancies can be efficiently estimated.

Abstract: We investigate the nanoscale friction behaviour of MX2 monolayers (M = Mo, W; X = S, Se) on Au(111) and Ag(111) substrates with a silicon tip using classical molecular dynamics simulations with machine-learning-based force fields. This approach enables an accurate description of tip-surface interactions and friction mechanisms at the atomic scale. We observe a pronounced non-monotonic dependence of the friction force on the applied normal load, indicating a breakdown of Amontons's law at the nanoscale. Analysis of lateral force' signals and their spatial Fourier transforms reveals the coexistence of multiple sliding modes, including longitudinal sliding, lateral slip, and zig-zag motions. We show that the overall friction response is governed by the relative contributions of these motions. While the qualitative features of friction are largely substrate-independent, both the magnitude of friction and the balance between sliding modes depend sensitively on the substrate-monolayer combination. In particular, Au/MoSe2/Si exhibits significantly reduced friction due to suppression of lateral slip motion. Our results indicate that the method is broadly applicable for probing nanoscale friction in related heterostructures.

Recent studies have demonstrated that certain observables commonly associated with TDs can also be identified in disordered solids indicating that topological concepts may be as crucial in amorphous solids as in crystals. This hints that TDs may offer a first-principles framework for understanding their mechanical response and complex spatiotemporal dynamics. In this Perspective, we review recent theoretical, numerical, and experimental studies that have exploited topological concepts to rationalize mechanical properties of amorphous solids. We also highlight pressing open questions and some promising directions for future research in the field.

Abstract: The solid electrolyte interphase SEI critically dictates the cyclability and Coulombic efficiency of sodium-metal batteries, yet its dynamic formation mechanisms and atomic-scale evolution during electrochemical cycling remain elusive due to the spatiotemporal limitations of existing techniques. Here, an "Interface Reactor" sampling strategy is proposed to construct a charge-aware neuroevolution potential (qNEP). These findings establish a comprehensive atomic-scale framework linking solvation structure, interfacial reaction networks, and electrochemical performance, providing mechanistic guidelines for rational SEI engineering in next-generation alkali-metal batteries. ### [77] [Towards viable H$_2$ storage in Ca decorated low-dimensional materials with insights from reference quantum Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07110)
*Yasmine S. Al-Hamdani,Dario Alfè,Andrea Zen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究采用先进的固定节点扩散蒙特卡洛（fixed-node diffusion Monte Carlo）方法，评估了两种锚定钙原子的策略：硼掺杂石墨烯和碳纳米管。研究发现，钙原子在碳纳米管内部锚定能有效提升氢分子吸附能，使其达到适合储氢的能量窗口（-0.2至-0.4 eV），为氢存储材料设计提供了可靠的基准数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢技术是减少污染和降低CO₂排放的关键能源替代方案。然而，当前碳纤维罐中的氢分子存储机制在移动应用中降低了燃料经济性，需要开发替代存储机制。在质子交换膜典型操作条件下吸附分子态氢（H₂）可能满足存储需求，但H₂是最小的分子，在适合存储的结合能窗口（-0.2至-0.4 eV）内物理吸附倾向有限。

Method: 本研究采用最先进的固定节点扩散蒙特卡洛（fixed-node diffusion Monte Carlo）方法，结合选择的密度泛函近似（density functional approximations），评估两种锚定钙（Ca）的策略：钙在硼掺杂石墨烯（boron doped graphene）上，以及钙在碳纳米管（carbon nanotubes）内部。该方法旨在准确预测钙和氢分子的结合能。

Result: 研究预测了可靠的钙和氢分子结合能，确认钙在碳纳米管内部和硼掺杂石墨烯上都能被有效锚定，同时提升氢分子吸附能。特别重要的是，锚定策略改善了氢分子吸附能，其中钙修饰碳纳米管内部的吸附能达到可行的存储窗口。扩散蒙特卡洛结合能为开发数据驱动方法和指导氢存储材料系统设计提供了急需的基准。

Conclusion: 钙锚定策略，特别是在碳纳米管内部锚定，能有效提升氢分子吸附能达到适合存储的能量窗口。本研究提供的基准数据对于开发数据驱动方法和指导氢存储材料系统设计具有重要意义，为解决氢存储技术瓶颈提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Hydrogen technology is set to be a key energy alternative for mitigating pollution and reducing CO$_2$ emissions. However, the current storage mechanism of hydrogen molecules in carbon fibre tanks detracts from the fuel economy of hydrogen in mobile applications, necessitating the development of alternative storage mechanisms. Adsorbing hydrogen in its molecular form (H$_2$) at typical operating conditions of proton exchange membranes can potentially meet storage requirements. However, H$_2$ is the smallest molecule with only two electrons and therefore it has very limited propensity to physisorb in a material within the binding energy window of $-0.2$ to $-0.4$ eV that is suitable for storage. Calcium atom decorators on graphene have previously shown promise for tunable H$_2$ binding, but the system is thermodynamically unstable toward the formation of calcium hydride. Moreover, the absolute adsorption of H$_2$ is challenging to predict accurately and is typically overestimated with van der Waals inclusive density functional approximations. In this work, we perform state-of-the-art fixed-node diffusion Monte Carlo alongside a selection of density functional approximations for two strategies of anchoring Ca: (i) Ca on boron doped graphene and (ii) Ca inside carbon nanotubes. We predict reliable Ca and H$_2$ binding energies, and establish that Ca is anchored inside carbon nanotubes and on boron doped graphene, while boosting the H$_2$ adsorption energy. Importantly, the H$_2$ adsorption energy is found to be improved by the anchoring strategies, with the energy inside a Ca decorated carbon nanotube reaching the viable storage window. The reference DMC binding energies provide much-needed benchmarks for developing data-driven methods and guiding experiment in the systematic design of hydrogen storage materials.

Abstract: We propose alterelectricity, an electrical analogue of altermagnetism, in which two switchable states possess alternating band structures. Such alterelectric states arise when a switchable sublattice-selective structural change connects two configurations related by a non-inversion symmetry. Using an anisotropic Lieb-lattice model, we establish a general symmetry framework for identifying alterelectricity. We further identify two material realizations of alterelectricity: (i) interlayer sliding in bilayers, as exemplified by tetragonal Ag2N and hexagonal FeHfI6; and (ii) ferroelectrically switchable Ti-adsorbed SnP2S6. This work establishes the foundational concept of alterelectricity and expands the material landscape of ferroic electronics.

MLIPs trained only on defect configurations in small supercells exhibit systematic energy errors in larger supercells, demonstrating limited transferability. Here, we present a machine learning Hamiltonian (MLH) model-based method for calculating total energies and atomic forces in defect supercells with linear-scaling computational cost, enabling efficient structural relaxation and accurate formation energy predictions. In this work we question the common interpretation of the experimental dynamics in terms of a massive bound electron-hole exciton that scatters with phonons and behaves as a quasi-particle. By using a combined theoretical and experimental investigation, we demonstrate that the observed dynamics can be interpreted as the photo-induced transition from direct to indirect excitonic-insulating order. *Liu Yang,Ming Li,Shui-Sen Zhang,Hang Zhou,Yi-Dong Liu,Xiao-Yan Guo,Wen-Jian Lu,Yu-Ping Sun,Evgeny Y. Tsymbal,Kaiyou Wang,Ding-Fu Shao*

Abstract: Nonvolatile magnetotransport responses in a single magnetic material have generally not been expected to exhibit a large ON/OFF ratio, because they are usually tied to spin-orbit coupling and therefore remain relatively weak. Here we show, contrary to this expectation, that giant nonvolatile magnetotransport can arise in a single magnetic material through magnetoelastic reconstruction of nonrelativistic real-space transport paths. Using the two-dimensional antiferromagnet FePS$_{3}$ as a representative system, first-principles quantum transport calculations reveal that charge transport is strongly tied to its quasi-one-dimensional zigzag sublattice chains and, under suitable doping, can even become confined to them. Moreover, strain lifts the degeneracy among symmetry-related zigzag variants and thus reorients these transport paths through magnetoelastic coupling. As a result, both the longitudinal and transverse conductivities change dramatically, yielding a giant magnetoelastic magnetoresistance of up to $10^{4}$% and an energy-independent Hall ratio that far exceeds the spontaneous Hall ratios found in conventional magnets. These results establish a route to exploiting symmetry-related magnetic variants and their associated transport paths for reconfigurable, high-performance spintronic devices with large nonvolatile readout contrast.

### [85] [Programmable Photocatalysis via Symmetry-Defined Periodic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07260)
*Qun Yang,Di Luo,Prineha Narang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出利用对称性定义的周期性势场（symmetry-defined periodic potentials）作为光催化策略，通过工程化长波长静电势场实现光生载流子的空间分离。以单层InSe为例，利用扭曲hBN产生的莫尔图案（moiré pattern）实现微带形成、带隙重整化（band-gap renormalization）和稳健的载流子分离。

Result: 实验可实现的莫尔图案产生微带形成、带隙重整化和稳健的载流子分离。通过匹配的BN/InSe局部配准，莫尔控制层向InSe传递可测量的静电调制，建立了连续势场工程与局部表面环境之间的微观联系。周期性势场强烈重组载流子分布，同时仅微弱扰动吸附趋势。

Conclusion: 周期性势场可作为光催化和二维材料中其他光驱动界面现象的广泛适用设计原则。该策略识别了一个实际有用的区域，其中电荷分离可被工程化，而不需要对基础表面化学进行重大改变。

Abstract: Photocatalysis in atomically thin semiconductors is often limited by rapid electron-hole recombination, making it difficult to translate favorable band structures into efficient chemical function. Here we propose symmetry-defined periodic potentials as a strategy for photocatalysis: instead of modifying the chemistry of the active layer, one engineers a long-wavelength electrostatic landscape that spatially separates photoexcited electrons and holes. Applied to monolayer InSe, we show that experimentally accessible moiré patterns, such as those generated by twisted hBN, produce miniband formation, band-gap renormalization, and robust carrier separation. Using commensurate BN/InSe local registries, we further show that the moiré control layer transfers a measurable electrostatic modulation to InSe, providing the microscopic link between continuum potential engineering and the local surface environment. The key result is that the periodic potential strongly reorganizes carrier distribution while only weakly perturbing adsorption trends, thereby identifying a practically useful regime in which charge separation can be engineered without demanding major changes to the underlying surface chemistry. These results position periodic potentials as a broadly applicable design principle for photocatalysis and other light-driven interfacial phenomena in two-dimensional materials.

</details>


### [86] [Determining the Free-Carrier Fraction in 2D Perovskites using Power Dependent Photoluminescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07262)
*Antonella Cutrupi,Marc Melendez Schofield,Raquel Utrera-Melero,Michel Frising,Enrique Arevalo Rodriguez,Upasana Das,Ferry Prins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于功率依赖光致发光（power-dependent photoluminescence）和萨哈方程（Saha-equation）的定量分析方法，用于直接测量半导体中自由载流子分数（free-carrier fraction），特别适用于具有中间激子结合能（intermediate exciton binding energies）的材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确确定纳米结构材料中光学激发态（optical excited state）的性质（激子或自由载流子）对器件设计至关重要，因为光电子和光伏技术需要针对优化的激发态动力学进行不同考量。传统的幂律分析（power-law analysis）在指数介于线性（纯激子）和二次方（纯自由载流子）之间时过于简化了基础物理机制。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于功率依赖峰值光致发光（power-dependent peak photoluminescence）和萨哈方程（Saha-equation）的完整分析方法，能够直接定量分析自由载流子分数。以不同厚度的Ruddlesden-Popper钙钛矿（Ruddlesden-Popper perovskites）作为模型系统进行研究，这些材料覆盖了广泛的激子结合能（exciton binding energies）和完整的自由载流子分数范围。

Result: 研究结果与先前报道的这些材料中激子结合能数值一致，证实了该方法的可靠性。该方法能够以微米空间分辨率探测晶界（grain boundaries）或边缘附近自由电荷分数的空间变化。研究还强调了在实际操作条件下进行光学表征的重要性，因为更高的激发密度（higher fluences）可能人为增强激子形成并扭曲太阳通量条件下的激发态解释。

Conclusion: 该方法为探测具有中间激子结合能的半导体中光学激发态性质提供了一个简单有效的工具，能够直接定量分析自由载流子分数，并在实际器件操作条件下提供更准确的激发态表征。

Abstract: Determining the nature of the optical excited state (excitons or free carriers) in nanostructured materials is crucial for device design, as optoelectronic and photovoltaic technologies require different considerations regarding the optimized excited state dynamics. Power-dependent photoluminescence is widely used to distinguish between excitons and free carriers, but the classical power-law analysis oversimplifies the underlying physics when the exponent lies between the linear (pure excitons) and quadratic (pure free carriers) limits. In this work, we present a complete study enabling a direct and quantitative analysis of the free-carrier fraction based on power-dependent peak photoluminescence and placing its analysis in the context of the Saha-equation. We study Ruddlesden-Popper perovskites with varying thickness as a model system, as they cover a wide range of exciton binding energies and the full range of free carrier fractions. Our results agree with previously reported values for the exciton binding energies in these materials, confirming the reliability of this approach and providing a simple and effective tool for probing the nature of optically excited states in semiconductors with intermediate exciton binding energies. We demonstrate that our method allows probing spatial variations in the fraction of free charges near grain boundaries or edges at micrometer spatial resolution. Finally, our results highlight the importance of performing optical characterization under excitation densities relevant to realistic operating conditions, as higher fluences can artificially enhance exciton formation and distort excited-state interpretation under solar-fluence conditions.

### [87] [Physics-Informed 3D Atomic Reconstruction and Dynamics of Free-Standing Graphene from Single Low-Dose TEM Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07271)
*Xiaojun Zhang,Shih-Wei Hung,Yawei Wu,Jyh-Pin Chou,Angus I. Kirkland,Roar Kilaas,Fu-Rong Chen*

Method: 该框架结合了模拟退火优化（simulated annealing optimisation）与分子动力学正则化（molecular dynamics regularisation），并采用基于Kullback-Leibler散度的校准方法使前向模型与实验图像统计特性对齐，以减少系统偏差。

Abstract: Resolving the three-dimensional (3D) atomic geometry of free-standing graphene in real time is essential for understanding how intrinsic rippling governs its electronic properties. However, the low electron doses required to mitigate radiation damage impose severe signal-to-noise constraints that limit conventional reconstruction methods. Here, we present a physics-informed computational framework that reconstructs 3D atomic coordinates of single-layer graphene from individual low-dose transmission electron microscopy (TEM) frames (8x10^3 e-/Ang^2, 1 ms temporal resolution). The approach combines simulated annealing optimisation with molecular dynamics regularisation, achieving sub-angstrom out-of-plane accuracy (sigma_z < 0.45 Ang), validated against ground-truth simulations. A Kullback-Leibler divergence-based calibration aligns the forward model with experimental image statistics, reducing systematic bias. Applied to high-speed time-series data, the framework enables simultaneous extraction of real-time ripple dynamics, strain tensors, surface curvature, bond-length distributions, and density functional theory (DFT)-derived electron localisation functions (ELF). We establish quantitative relationships linking local geometry, strain, and bond-length variations to electron localisation, demonstrating that sub-angstrom structural fluctuations drive spatially localised, millisecond-scale electronic modulation. A critical dose threshold is identified below which structural information becomes irrecoverable, providing practical guidance for experimental design. The framework is broadly applicable to beam-sensitive two-dimensional materials.

### [88] [Symmetry-protected four double-Weyl fermions and their topological phase transitions in nonmagnetic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07301)
*Yun-Yun Bai,Ke-Xin Pang,Yan Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Method: 建立了严格的晶体对称性约束，将仅含四个对称性保护的双外尔点（DWPs）的存在限制在28个空间群中，涵盖非磁性无自旋和自旋系统。基于此分类，识别出一种sp2-sp3杂化的手性碳同素异形体THRLN-C32作为理想候选材料。
