Conclusion: 该工作为非磁性自旋系统中最小双外尔半金属（double-WSMs）提供了确定性的理论框架，并引入了一个研究应变可调拓扑量子现象的最佳材料平台。

Abstract: Realizing Weyl semimetals (WSMs) with the minimal number of Weyl points (WPs) fundamentally simplifies extracting intrinsic topological responses. While a minimum of four conventional ($|C|=1$) WPs in nonmagnetic crystals is well-established, the exact symmetry requirements and material realization for the unique configuration of four unconventional double-Weyl points (DWPs, $|C|=2$) remain unresolved. Here, we establish rigorous crystalline symmetry constraints restricting the existence of exactly four symmetry-protected DWPs to merely 28 space groups in both nonmagnetic spinless and spinful systems. Guided by this classification, we identify an $sp$$^2$--$sp$$^3$ hybridized chiral carbon allotrope, THRLN-C$_{32}$, as an ideal candidate hosting precisely this four-DWP configuration near the Fermi level. These $C_4$-protected DWPs project extended or closed-loop Fermi arcs onto the surface Brillouin zone, providing unambiguous spectroscopic signatures. Furthermore, external strain drives profound topological phase transitions encapsulated in a unified evolution landscape: the pristine four-DWP state dissociates into two exotic three-terminal Weyl complexes, degenerates into eight conventional $|C|=1$ WPs, or collapses into a trivial insulator. This work provides a definitive theoretical framework for minimal double-WSMs in nonmagnetic spinful systems and introduces an optimal material platform for investigating strain-tunable topological quantum phenomena.

### [89] [$c=1$ strings as a matrix integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06301)
*Scott Collier,Lorenz Eberhardt,Victor A. Rodriguez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文建立了c=1弦理论S矩阵的三重对偶性：世界面描述、矩阵量子力学和基于特定谱曲线的(0+0)维矩阵积分。通过从复Liouville弦的交数表达式出发，推导出闭形式Feynman规则，并证明振幅满足微扰时空幺正性和Mirzakhani型递推关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究c=1弦理论的微扰S矩阵，旨在建立其三种不同表述之间的对偶关系：世界面描述、矩阵量子力学和矩阵积分。这一三重对偶性（triality）的建立有助于深化对弦理论不同表述之间联系的理解。

Method: 从复Liouville弦（complex Liouville string）的交数（intersection numbers）表达式出发，推导出c=1振幅作为黎曼曲面模空间（moduli space of Riemann surfaces）上交数的闭形式Feynman规则表达式。通过限制在第一布里渊区（first Brillouin zone）和解析延拓到洛伦兹运动学（Lorentzian kinematics）来恢复物理S矩阵元。

Result: 证明了c=1弦理论的S矩阵可以用基于谱曲线$\mathsf{x}(z) = 2\sqrt{2}\cos(z)$, $\mathsf{y}(z)=\sin(z)$的双重标度(0+0)维矩阵积分描述。从交数理论表达式直接证明了振幅满足微扰时空幺正性（perturbative spacetime unitarity），并显示它们满足Mirzakhani型递推关系（Mirzakhani-type recursion relation）。与已知的矩阵量子力学结果详细吻合，为三重对偶性提供了有力证据。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了c=1弦理论的三重对偶性：世界面描述、矩阵量子力学和矩阵积分。通过交数理论方法，不仅推导了振幅的闭形式表达式，还证明了其幺正性和递推关系，为弦理论不同表述之间的深刻联系提供了新的理解框架。

Abstract: We study the perturbative $S$-matrix of the $c=1$ string and show that it admits a description in terms of a double-scaled (0+0)-dimensional matrix integral based on the spectral curve $\mathsf{x}(z) = 2\sqrt{2}\cos(z)$, $\mathsf{y}(z)=\sin(z)$. Combined with the famous duality to matrix quantum mechanics, this establishes a triality between three formulations of the theory: the worldsheet description, matrix quantum mechanics, and a matrix integral.
  Starting from the intersection number expressions for the complex Liouville string, we derive closed-form Feynman rule expressions for the $c=1$ amplitudes as intersection numbers on the moduli space of Riemann surfaces. The intersection theory naturally computes amplitudes corresponding to a discretized target space where momentum is conserved only modulo an integer. The physical $S$-matrix elements are recovered by restriction to the first `Brillouin zone' and analytic continuation to Lorentzian kinematics. We prove that these amplitudes satisfy perturbative spacetime unitarity directly from the intersection theory expressions, and show that they satisfy a Mirzakhani-type recursion relation. We show detailed agreement with the known matrix quantum mechanics results, providing strong evidence for the triality.

</details>


### [90] [Lattice chiral symmetry from bosons in 3+1d](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06307)
*Zhiyao Lu,Sahand Seifnashri,Shu-Heng Shao*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可解的哈密顿量，在格点上精确实现了手征$U(1)_V \times U(1)_A$对称性，通过使用格点玻色子而非费米子规避了Nielsen-Ninomiya型不可行定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于构建格点模型以精确实现手征对称性，同时规避Nielsen-Ninomiya不可行定理（no-go theorem）。传统格点费米子理论面临手征对称性保持的困难，本文探索使用玻色子替代方案。

Method: 采用格点玻色子而非费米子构建可解哈密顿量，实现精确的$U(1)_V \times U(1)_A$手征对称性。通过格点θ角（lattice theta angle）的变化展示手征反常（chiral anomaly），并对$U(1)_V$或$U(1)_A$进行规范化（gauging）操作。

Result: 连续极限（continuum limit）对应具有类轴子耦合（axion-like coupling）的紧致玻色子场论（compact boson field theory）。$U(1)_A$对称性在连续极限中转变为高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetry）。规范化操作分别导致格点非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry）和2群对称性（2-group symmetry），与连续理论图像一致。

Conclusion: 该工作成功构建了精确实现手征对称性的格点玻色子模型，为研究手征反常、非可逆对称性和2群对称性提供了格点实现框架，并建立了格点与连续理论之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We present a solvable Hamiltonian that realizes an exact lattice chiral $U(1)_V \times U(1)_A$ symmetry. Nielsen-Ninomiya-type no-go theorems are evaded by using lattice bosons rather than fermions. The continuum limit is a compact boson field theory with an axion-like coupling. The $U(1)_V$ symmetry shifts the scalar, while $U(1)_A$ acts on local operators associated with short axion strings and is transmuted into a higher-form symmetry in the continuum limit. We demonstrate the chiral anomaly by showing that the lattice theta angle is shifted by an axial rotation when $U(1)_V$ is gauged. Gauging either $U(1)_V$ or $U(1)_A$ leads to lattice non-invertible and 2-group symmetries, respectively, matching the continuum picture.

### [92] [Massive modes on magnetized blow-up manifold of $T^2/\mathbb{Z}_N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06635)
*Tatsuo Kobayashi,Hajime Otsuka,Hikaru Uchida*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将 $T^2/\mathbb{Z}_N$ 轨道（orbifold）的奇点用 $S^2$ 的一部分适当替换来构造爆破流形。分析中要求爆破过程保持总磁通量、总曲率以及连接线上的有效磁通量不变，以确保磁化轨道和磁化球面上大质量模的平滑连接。

Conclusion: 成功建立了磁化爆破流形上大质量模的分析框架，明确了爆破过程需满足的物理量守恒条件，并揭示了局域模数量与质量能级之间的定量关系：每个奇点处的局域模数量随质量能级每增加一单位而增加一个。

Abstract: We study massive modes on a magnetized blow-up manifold of $T^2/\mathbb{Z}_N$. The blow-up manifold can be constructed by appropriately replacing orbifold singular points with a part of $S^2$. To ensure a smooth connection between the massive modes on magnetized $T^2/\mathbb{Z}_N$ orbifold and those on magnetized $S^2$, it is required that not only the total magnetic flux as well as the total curvature but also the effective magnetic flux on the connected line remain invariant under the blow-up procedure. Furthermore, we find that the number of the localized modes at each orbifold singular point increases by one for each unit increment of the mass level.

### [93] [Can Locality, Unitarity, and Hidden Zeros Completely Determine Tree-Level Amplitudes?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07195)
*Kang Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文从软极限（soft limit）视角探讨了局域性（locality）、幺正性（unitarity）和新发现的隐藏零点（hidden zeros）是否能完全确定树图振幅（tree-level amplitudes）。作者通过重构杨-米尔斯理论（YM）的单软定理（single-soft theorems）和非线性西格玛模型（NLSM）的双软定理（double-soft theorems），证明这三者足以完全确定树图YM和NLSM振幅。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究局域性、幺正性和新发现的隐藏零点是否足以完全确定树图振幅。这一研究动机源于从软极限视角理解振幅基本约束条件的需要，特别是对于杨-米尔斯理论和非线性西格玛模型这两类重要理论。

Method: 研究方法基于软极限视角，从局域性、幺正性和隐藏零点出发重构了树图YM振幅的单软定理和树图NLSM振幅的双软定理。该方法依赖于先前研究建立的框架，即完整振幅可以从这些软定理中构造出来。

Result: 研究结果表明，通过局域性、幺正性和隐藏零点可以成功重构YM振幅的单软定理和NLSM振幅的双软定理。由于已有研究证明完整振幅可以从这些软定理构造，因此作者得出结论：这三者完全确定了树图YM和NLSM振幅。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论：局域性、幺正性和隐藏零点共同完全确定了树图杨-米尔斯理论和非线性西格玛模型的振幅。这一发现为理解振幅的基本约束条件提供了新的视角，并确认了软极限方法在振幅理论中的重要性。

Abstract: In this note, we address the question of whether locality, unitarity, and newly discovered hidden zeros can completely determine tree-level amplitudes, from the perspective of soft limit. We reconstruct the single-soft theorems of tree YM amplitudes and the double-soft theorems of tree NLSM amplitudes from locality, unitarity, and hidden zeros. A series of studies have shown that the full YM and NLSM amplitudes can be constructed from these soft theorems; therefore, we conclude that locality, unitarity, and hidden zeros completely determine the tree-level YM and NLSM amplitudes.

</details>


### [94] [Loop Blow-up Inflation: An Overview](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07288)
*Sukŗti Bansal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文更新了Loop Blow-up Inflation的观测预测，发现弦环修正（string loop corrections）不仅普遍存在，而且改变了原始的非微扰图像，在较大场值处产生新的慢滚（slow-roll）机制，导致修正的暴胀动力学和独特的宇宙学预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于重新评估弦环修正对Kähler势的影响，这些修正长期以来被视为大体积情景（Large Volume Scenario）中blow-up inflation的潜在威胁。本文认为这些修正普遍存在，而非可避免的，并会从根本上改变原始的非微扰图像。

Method: 方法基于arXiv:2403.04831的工作，聚焦于弦环修正对Kähler势的影响。通过分析这些修正如何改变标量势（scalar potential）从指数形式向幂律平台（power-law plateau）的转变，研究修正的暴胀动力学。

Result: 结果显示弦环修正使最小场值附近的慢滚失效，而在较大场值处产生新的慢滚机制。这导致修正的暴胀动力学和独特的宇宙学预测，包括增加的张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）。所有三种SM-location情景均与最新的$n_s$、$r$和$ΔN_{\rm eff}$约束一致。

Conclusion: 结论表明弦环效应在弦紧致化（string compactifications）中实现可行暴胀方面发挥着建设性作用，而非仅仅是有害的。更新的Giudice-Masiero系数使Scenario III与更严格的额外暗辐射约束一致，所有情景均与近期观测数据相容。

Abstract: This proceedings contribution provides an overview of Loop Blow-up Inflation and updates its observational predictions and their comparison with the latest CMB and BAO data from combined analyses of SPT, Planck, ACT, and BICEP/Keck, as well as ACT DR6 constraints on extra dark radiation. It is based on work originally published in arXiv:2403.04831, carried out in collaboration with L. Brunelli, M. Cicoli, A. Hebecker, and R. Kuespert, and presented at the 2025 Workshop on Quantum Gravity and Strings. We focus on string loop corrections to the Kähler potential, long regarded as a potential threat to blow-up inflation in the Large Volume Scenario. We argue that these corrections, previously assumed avoidable, are in fact generically present and qualitatively alter the original non-perturbative picture: they invalidate slow-roll near the minimum and instead generate a new slow-roll regime at larger field values, where the scalar potential transitions from an exponential to a power-law plateau.
  This leads to modified inflationary dynamics and distinct cosmological predictions, including an increased tensor-to-scalar ratio. We confront all three SM-location scenarios with the latest constraints on $n_s$, $r$, and $ΔN_{\rm eff}$. The tighter bound on extra dark radiation requires an updated Giudice-Masiero coefficient in Scenario III, yielding revised predictions presented here for the first time. All scenarios remain consistent with recent observations, with the ACT+DESI combination yielding near-perfect agreement in $n_s$ for vanishing extra dark radiation at $0.03σ$ deviation. We also comment on subleading loop corrections, which improve robustness by reducing the field value required for slow roll. These results highlight that string loop effects, rather than being merely detrimental, can play a constructive role in realising viable inflation in string compactifications.

### [95] [Groenewold-Moyal twists, integrable spin-chains and AdS/CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07291)
*Riccardo Borsato,Miguel García Fernández*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究首次通过可积性方法处理Groenewold-Moyal扭转变形下的AdS/CFT对偶谱问题，构建了耦合两个$\mathfrak{sl}(2)$不变自旋链的扭曲自旋链模型，并在弦理论侧匹配了基态能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是首次通过可积性方法处理Groenewold-Moyal扭转变形（Groenewold-Moyal twist deformation）下的AdS/CFT对偶谱问题。该工作旨在理解这类变形如何影响AdS/CFT对应关系中的谱结构。

Method: 方法包括构建耦合两个$\mathfrak{sl}(2)$不变自旋链的扭曲自旋链模型，该模型可视为$AdS_3/CFT_2$自旋链子扇区的变形。研究采用Baxter方程方法计算基态和激发态能量，并在弦理论侧构造Maldacena-Russo-Hashimoto-Itzhaki型AdS变形。

Result: 结果显示在特定基下自旋链哈密顿量呈现Jordan块形式，而在构造Groenewold-Moyal扭转变形的生成元本征态基中则表现为可对角化且具有变形谱。在弦理论侧，成功匹配了自旋链基态能量的$\mathcal O(J^{-3})$项与弦经典解的守恒荷。

Conclusion: 结论表明该变形体系具有可积性特征，弦sigma模型的守恒荷具有非局域性且不对应标准等距对称性，但可通过单值矩阵计算，是可积性提供的守恒荷塔的一部分。

Abstract: We take the first steps to address via integrability the spectral problem of AdS/CFT dual pairs deformed by Groenewold-Moyal twists. In particular, we start by considering a twisted spin-chain that couples, through a Groenewold-Moyal twist deformation, two $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$-invariant spin-chains. We interpret this deformed spin-chain as a deformation of a subsector of the $AdS_3/CFT_2$ spin-chain, but the construction shares qualitative features also with the corresponding deformation of the $AdS_5/CFT_4$ spin-chain, for example. As in similar types of deformations, we show that there exists a certain basis in which the spin-chain Hamiltonian takes a Jordan-block form. At the same time, by working in the basis of eigenstates of the generators used to construct the Groenewold-Moyal twist, the Hamiltonian appears to be diagonalisable and with a deformed spectrum. Employing the method of the Baxter equation, we write down the energy of the ground state and of excited states in a perturbation of the deformation parameter. We then consider the string-theory side of the duality, where the twist is realised as a deformation of AdS of the type of Maldacena-Russo-Hashimoto-Itzhaki. We construct a deformation of the usual BMN classical solution, and in the large-$J$ limit we match the leading $\mathcal O(J^{-3})$ term of the energy of the spin-chain groundstate with a conserved charge of the string classical solution. Differently from the undeformed setup as well as similar kinds of deformations, we find that the general expression of this charge of the string sigma-model is non-local, and that it does not correspond to a standard isometry. Nevertheless, it can be computed from the monodromy matrix and it is part of the tower of conserved charges provided by integrability.

</details>


### [96] [Exotic theta terms in 2+1d fractonic field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07293)
*Yuki Furukawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了2+1维φ理论中的奇异θ项，该理论为XY-plaquette模型提供了连续描述。这些θ项包括体θ项和叶状θ项，两者均导致广义Witten效应，使携带缠绕子系统电荷的涡旋算符获得动量子系统电荷。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于φ理论框架，该理论展现动量和缠绕子系统对称性。通过分析两种θ项：体θ项和叶状θ项，其中叶状θ项通过耦合叶状结构相邻叶片上的缠绕流构造。使用基于改进Villain公式的晶格实现来验证理论特征。

Result: 研究发现两种θ项均导致广义Witten效应，使携带缠绕子系统电荷的涡旋算符获得动量子系统电荷。特别地，叶状θ角可在空间上变化而不影响经典运动方程，其对应的Witten效应呈现更复杂结构：涡旋算符获得四极动量电荷。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在2+1维φ理论中，不连续场构型诱导的非平凡反作用产生新的拓扑项，包括体θ项和叶状θ项。这些θ项导致广义Witten效应，揭示了分形系统中拓扑项的丰富物理内涵，特别是叶状θ角的空间变化特性及其四极动量电荷效应。

Abstract: In this work, we study exotic theta terms in the 2+1d $φ$-theory, which provides a continuum description of the XY-plaquette model. The $φ$-theory can be viewed as a fractonic analogue of the 1+1d compact boson and exhibits momentum and winding subsystem symmetries. In this theory, discontinuous field configurations play a crucial role. Although such configurations spoil the naive topology of the field, they induce nontrivial backreactions that give rise to new topological terms. We study two types of theta terms, which we call the bulk theta term and the foliated theta term. The foliated theta term is constructed by coupling winding currents on neighboring leaves of a foliation. Remarkably, the corresponding theta angle can vary spatially without affecting the classical equations of motion. Both theta terms lead to generalized Witten effects, in which vortex operators carrying winding subsystem charge acquire momentum subsystem charge. In the case of the foliated theta angle, the Witten effect exhibits a more intricate structure: vortex operators acquire a quadrupolar momentum charge. We demonstrate these features using lattice realizations based on the modified Villain formulation.

### [97] [Theoretical and Observational Bounds on Dynamical Chern-Simons Gravity as an Effective Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07332)
*Alexander Cassem,Mark P. Hertzberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文对动态陈-西蒙斯（dCS）引力理论进行了因果性和幺正性约束分析，发现dCS耦合常数受到显著限制，表明其对宏观观测系统（如黑洞合并）的修正应非常小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力有效理论（gravitational effective theories）对于描述偏离广义相对论（General Relativity）的空间至关重要。通过因果性（causality）和幺正性（unitarity）等基本原理检验这些理论，可以对相应参数施加约束。动态陈-西蒙斯（dynamical Chern-Simons, dCS）引力作为一种宇称破缺的广义相对论修正，引起了广泛关注，包括可能产生新的引力波形和宇宙暴胀现象。

Method: 首先在dCS引力背景下推导色散关系（dispersion relation）和波包速度，计算相应的夏皮罗时间延迟（Shapiro time delay）至二阶，分析超光速可能性。然后通过一组具有（赝）汤川耦合的N个费米子构建紫外完备（UV completion），施加微扰性和引力物种界限（gravitational species bound）约束。

Result: 因果性要求对dCS耦合常数施加界限，该界限比标准估计略尖锐但兼容。通过紫外完备分析发现，dCS耦合常数受到显著更强的约束，具体取决于物种界限尺度的选择。研究还识别了紫外完备产生的高阶算符。

Conclusion: 总体而言，dCS对引力动力学的任何修正，在宏观观测系统（如晚期合并黑洞）中可能都非常小。这表明该理论在可观测尺度上的效应受到严格限制。

Abstract: Gravitational effective theories are essential for characterizing the space of deviations from General Relativity (GR). Testing these theories against fundamental principles, such as causality and unitarity, can yield constraints on the corresponding parameters. In this paper, we perform such an analysis on the very interesting dynamical Chern-Simons (dCS) gravity. This is a parity violating correction to GR wherein a new scalar field couples to the Pontryagin density $^*R\,R$. It has generated significant interest, including possible new gravitational wave shapes for LIGO/Virgo and new phenomena from cosmic inflation. In this work, we begin by deriving the dispersion relation and wave packet speed on top of a gravitational wave background in dCS gravity. This alters the corresponding Shapiro time delay (which we compute to second order), potentially giving superluminality. Causality then demands a bound on the dCS coupling constant, which we find to be moderately sharper, but compatible with, standard estimates. We then examine a UV completion in the form of a set of $N$ fermions with a (pseudo) Yukawa coupling. By imposing perturbativity and a gravitational species bound, we find that the dCS coupling constant is constrained significantly more, depending on the choice of scale of the species bound. We also identify higher order operators generated from the UV completion. Overall, we find that any dCS corrections to gravitational dynamics should likely be very small on macroscopic systems of observational interest, such as in late-time merging black holes.

</details>

*Mohd Ali,Georg Stettinger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明BEF辛结构可直接从L∞-拉格朗日量推导，建立了BEF辛结构与Barnich-Brandt辛形式之间的精确关系，并展示了BEF方法如何自然地编码角项信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bernardes、Erler和Firat在2025年提出了适用于非局域理论的相空间辛形式新表达式。本文旨在从L∞-拉格朗日量直接推导该BEF辛结构，并建立其与Barnich-Brandt辛形式之间的精确关系。

Method: 采用协变相空间方法（covariant phase space approach），从L∞-拉格朗日量（L∞-Lagrangian）直接推导BEF辛结构。通过理论分析建立BEF辛结构与Barnich-Brandt辛形式之间的精确关系，并针对二阶运动方程理论进行具体证明。

Result: 证明了对于具有二阶运动方程的理论，BEF辛结构与Barnich-Brandt构造完全一致，从而解释了广义相对论中典型角项在BEF方法中的出现。此外，BEF辛结构自然地编码了通用角项信息和部分边界条件信息。

Conclusion: BEF辛结构可直接从L∞-拉格朗日量推导，并与Barnich-Brandt辛形式在二阶运动方程理论中一致。该方法为处理辛结构和哈密顿量提供了系统框架，并通过具体示例验证了构造的有效性。

Abstract: In 2025, Bernardes, Erler and Firat proposed a novel, elegant expression for the symplectic form on phase space applicable to non-local theories. We show that this BEF symplectic structure can be derived directly from an $L_\infty$-Lagrangian by following the covariant phase space approach. Moreover, we establish a precise relation between the BEF symplectic structure and the Barnich--Brandt symplectic form for general finite-derivative theories. In particular, we prove that for theories with second-order equations of motion, the BEF symplectic structure coincides with the Barnich--Brandt construction, thereby explaining the emergence of the canonical corner term in general relativity within the BEF approach.
  We further argue that the BEF symplectic structure naturally encodes information about generic corner terms and some information about boundary conditions. In addition, we develop a general expression for the Hamiltonian in theories in $L_\infty$-form and present several explicit examples illustrating the construction.

### [99] [High Breakdown Field Multi-kV UWBG AlGaN Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06372)

Method: 采用AlGaN极化场效应晶体管（PolFETs）结构，利用栅极连接场板（gate-connected field plate）结构设计，在不同栅漏间距（LGD：3.9和6.8μm）下进行性能评估。

Abstract: We demonstrate high-performance UWBG AlGaN PolFETs exhibiting a state-of-the-art combination of nearly 1 A/mm on-state current (~ 960 mA/mm) and large breakdown field (> 4.8 MV/cm) in high carrier density (1.15 x 1013 cm-2). Multi-kV robustness is successfully demonstrated exhibiting 1.28 and 2.17 kV by utilizing a gate-connected field plate structures in 3.9 and 6.8 μm LGD, corresponding to the extremely low specific on-resistance of 1.25 and 2.86 mΩcm2, respectively. High RF performance is also achieved, providing fT and fMAX, of 8.5 and 15 GHz, respectively, for 3.9 μm LGD. These results highlight UWBG AlGaN as a platform for both high-voltage RF and power applications.

### [100] [Emitter-Host Interactions of High-Efficiency Deep Blue Single-Gaussian Europium (II) Emitters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06470)
*Mahmoud Soleimani,Paulius Imbrasas,Jan-Michael Mewes,Felix Kaden,Stephanie Anna Buchholtz,Karl Leo,Sebastian Schellhammer,Carsten Rothe,Sebastian Reineke*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种新型Eu(II)配合物分子设计策略，通过冠醚配体与碳硼酸盐阴离子组合实现深蓝色窄带发射，量子产率接近90%，并成功应用于真空沉积OLED器件，外量子效率超过12%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种新的分子设计概念，将冠醚配体（crown-ether ligand）与碳硼酸盐阴离子（carborate anions）结合，以定义配位环境并改善铕中心的立体屏蔽。基于密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）和时间分辨实验研究了Eu(II)配合物与主体环境之间的相互作用。

Result: 开发出两种发射体，结合了窄带深蓝色光致发光（photoluminescence）、量子产率接近90%以及适合真空沉积的热稳定性。OLED器件在456-458 nm处表现出电致发光（electroluminescence），光谱宽度低至36 nm，CIE坐标深至(0.15, 0.06)，最大外量子效率（external quantum efficiency）超过12%。

Conclusion: 确定了分子设计、Eu(II)核心的立体屏蔽以及激发态5d电子的能量限制是控制高效发光的关键因素，为Eu(II)发射体的理性设计提供了路线图。这些见解为开发更高效率和更深蓝色的Eu(II)基OLEDs奠定了基础。

Abstract: Eu(II) complexes are attractive emitters for deep-blue organic light-emitting diodes (OLEDs) due to their narrow, parity-allowed 4f-5d emission; however, their implementation in vacuum-processed OLEDs has remained limited. Here, we introduce a new molecular design concept for Eu(II) emitters, in which a crown-ether ligand is combined with carborate anions to define the coordination environment and improve steric shielding of the europium center. Based on this design, we present two emitters that combine narrow deep-blue photoluminescence with quantum yields approaching 90% and sufficient thermal stability for vacuum deposition. OLEDs incorporating these emitters exhibit electroluminescence at 456-458 nm, with spectral widths down to 36 nm and CIE coordinates as deep as (0.15, 0.06) and achieve a maximum external quantum efficiency above 12%. In order to find the pathway to maximum electroluminescence efficiency based on this emitter class, we study interactions between Eu(II) complexes and the host environment, based on density-functional theory and time-resolved experiments. We identify molecular design, steric shielding of the Eu(II) core, and energetic confinement of the excited 5d electron as key factors governing efficient luminescence, providing a roadmap for rational design of Eu(II) emitters. Together, these insights establish a foundation for higher-efficiency and deeper-blue OLEDs incorporating Eu(II) emitters.

</details>

### [102] [Spin-adapted neural network backflow for strongly correlated electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06841)
*Yunzhi Li,Zibo Wu,Bohan Zhang,Wei-Hai Fang,Zhendong Li*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自旋适配的神经网络回流（SA-NNBF）变分波函数，解决了神经网络波函数中自旋对称性缺失的问题，并在强关联电子系统中实现了超越传统方法的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确描述过渡金属配合物等系统中的强关联电子需要严格遵守自旋对称性，而现代基于神经网络的变分波函数普遍缺乏这一特性，导致在模拟近简并自旋态系统时出现严重的自旋污染问题。

Method: 提出了自旋适配神经网络回流（spin-adapted neural network backflow, SA-NNBF）拟设，在二次量子化框架下构建完全反对称波函数，结合神经网络回流空间分量和以乘积和形式表达的自旋本征函数。针对自旋适配的计算复杂性，引入了自旋本征函数的张量压缩算法和基于二次量子化中粒子-空穴对偶的更紧凑波函数表示。

Result: SA-NNBF能够对包含超过一百个电子的挑战性分子系统（如固氮酶中的FeMo辅因子FeMoco）进行变分蒙特卡洛计算。在典型强关联分子应用中，SA-NNBF在参数数量相近的情况下始终优于标准NNBF，并且以显著减少的计算资源超越了最先进的自旋适配密度矩阵重整化群（SA-DMRG）算法在FeMoco上的精度。

Conclusion: 该工作为探索完全保持对称性的神经网络量子态用于相互作用费米子问题建立了基础框架，解决了神经网络波函数中自旋对称性缺失的关键限制。

Abstract: Accurately describing strongly correlated electrons in systems such as transition metal complexes requires strict adherence to spin symmetry, a feature largely absent in modern neural-network-based variational wavefunctions. This deficiency can lead to severe spin contamination in simulating systems with near-degenerate spin states. To resolve this limitation, we present a spin-adapted neural network backflow (SA-NNBF) ansatz, formulated in second quantization for fermionic lattice models and ab initio quantum chemistry. Our approach constructs a fully antisymmetric wavefunction by combining a neural-network backflow spatial component with a spin eigenfunction expressed in a sum-of-products form. To address the computational complexity of spin adaptation, we introduce a tensor compression algorithm for spin eigenfunctions, and a more compact wavefunction representation based on the particle-hole duality in second quantization. These advancements enable variational Monte Carlo calculations using SA-NNBF for challenging molecular systems with more than one hundred electrons, including the FeMo-cofactor (FeMoco) in nitrogenase. Applications to prototypical strongly correlated molecules demonstrate that SA-NNBF consistently outperforms standard NNBF with a similar number of parameters. Furthermore, it surpasses the accuracy of the state-of-the-art spin-adapted density matrix renormalization group (SA-DMRG) algorithm for FeMoco with a significantly reduced computational resource. Our work establishes a foundational framework for exploring fully symmetry-preserving neural-network quantum states for interacting fermion problems.

### [103] [Self-consistent Hessian-level meta-generalized gradient approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07046)
*Pooria Dabbaghi,Juan Maria García Lastra,Piotr de Silva*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将$\vartheta$-MGGA类泛函重新表述为海森矩阵级元广义梯度近似（HL-MGGAs），引入简化的非经验泛函$\vartheta$-PBE，并设计其在投影缀加波（projector augmented-wave, PAW）方法中的自洽实现路线图。

Result: 利用完整的空间二阶密度导数集合，该泛函的描述符成功区分了标准等轨道指标（iso-orbital indicators）常混淆的不同单电子密度极限，如单中心原子密度和双中心键。分子和固态数据集的基准测试显示$\vartheta$-PBE能准确预测化学吸附能和分子性质，但在预测体相晶格常数方面仍面临挑战。

Conclusion: 这项工作证明了设计轨道无关、基于海森矩阵的交换相关泛函（orbital-independent, Hessian-based exchange-correlation functionals）的物理效用和可行性，为密度泛函理论的发展提供了新方向。

Abstract: The $\vartheta$-MGGA class of density functionals is formally reformulated as Hessian-level meta-generalized gradient approximations (HL-MGGAs). In contrast to standard meta-GGAs that rely on the orbital-dependent kinetic-energy density or the density Laplacian, HL-MGGAs utilize the full density Hessian. We introduce a simplified, non-empirical functional, $\vartheta$-PBE, and present a roadmap for its self-consistent implementation within the projector augmented-wave (PAW) method. By utilizing the complete set of spatial second-order density derivatives, the functional's underlying descriptor successfully distinguishes between distinct one-electron density limits, such as single-center atomic densities and two-center bonds, that standard iso-orbital indicators often conflate. Benchmarks across molecular and solid-state datasets reveal that while $\vartheta$-PBE delivers accurate chemisorption energies and molecular properties, challenges remain in predicting bulk lattice constants. Ultimately, this work demonstrates the physical utility and feasibility of designing orbital-independent, Hessian-based exchange-correlation functionals.

### [104] [Explicit Electric Potential-Embedded Machine Learning Framework: A Unified Description from Atomic to Electronic Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07322)
*Jingwen Zhou,Yawen Yu,Xuwei Liu,Chungen Liu*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的显式电势框架，用于同时预测原子力和电子密度分布，以推进电化学界面的精确大规模模拟。该框架包含数据生成、模型训练和应用三个组件，在Pt(111)/水界面模型中表现出高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了进一步发展电化学界面的精确大规模模拟，需要建立能够同时预测原子力和电子密度分布的框架。当前方法在描述原子力方面存在局限性，需要克服这一挑战以实现更全面的界面研究。

Method: 框架包含三个组件：数据生成、模型训练和应用。数据生成在Hy-DFT中实现，通过调节恒定电势从头算分子动力学（CP-AIMD）中的电势来提高收敛效率。模型训练包括两个模块：电势嵌入MACE（PE-MACE）和电势嵌入电子密度预测（PE-EDP）。PE-MACE基于MACE架构实现显式电势机器学习力场（EEP-MLFF），而PE-EDP基于等变图神经网络预测任意电势下的电子密度分布。

Result: 在Pt(111)/水界面模型系统中，PE-MACE和PE-EDP在训练和测试集上均表现出高精度。CP-MLMD的径向分布函数与CP-AIMD结果吻合良好，长时间尺度模拟揭示了电势诱导的界面水重组。PE-EDP的平面积分电荷分布和Bader分析与DFT结果一致。

Conclusion: 该框架能够同时描述任意电势下的原子动力学和电子密度分布，为研究电化学界面提供了有用工具。通过结合显式电势的机器学习方法，实现了对界面结构和电子性质的综合预测。

Abstract: To further develop accurate and large-scale simulations of electrochemical interfaces, we propose a unified explicit electric potential framework to simultaneously predict atomic forces and electron density distributions. The framework consists of three components: data generation, model training, and application. The data generation component, implemented in Hy-DFT, efficiently regulates the potential during constant-potential ab initio molecular dynamics (CP-AIMD), reducing the number of single-point calculations required for convergence. The model training component includes two modules: Potential-Embedded MACE (PE-MACE) and Potential-Embedded Electron Density Prediction (PE-EDP). PE-MACE implements an explicit electric potential machine learning force field (EEP-MLFF) based on the MACE architecture. We develop PE-EDP to overcome the limitation of EEP-MLFF in describing atom forces. PE-EDP, also based on equivariant graph neural networks, predicts electron density distributions under arbitrary potentials. Using the Pt(111)/water interface as a model system, both PE-MACE and PE-EDP show high accuracy on training and test sets. Radial distribution functions from CP-MLMD agree well with CP-AIMD, and long-timescale simulations reveal potential-induced reorganization of interfacial water. Planar-integrated charge profiles and Bader analysis from PE-EDP are consistent with DFT results. These results demonstrate that the framework can simultaneously describe atomic dynamics and electron density distributions under arbitrary potentials, providing a useful tool for studying electrochemical interfaces.

### [105] [The Random Subsequence Model and Uniform Codes for the Deletion Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07234)
*Ryan Jeong,Francisco Pernice*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文引入随机子序列模型（Random Subsequence Model），这是一种定义在随机字符串对上的自旋玻璃模型。研究显示该模型在零温度下处于自旋玻璃相，并由此证明了均匀随机码在删除信道中对所有删除概率都能达到正速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立随机子序列模型与多个长期问题的联系，包括删除信道中均匀随机码的最佳速率、两个随机字符串的最长公共子序列问题，以及统计物理中的有向聚合物模型。

Method: 引入随机子序列模型的两个变体：零模型（null model）和植入模型（planted model）。在N,M→∞且固定密度参数α=M/N∈(0,1)的体系下，分析零模型的退火自由能（annealed free energy）与零模型、植入模型的淬火自由能（quenched free energy）之间的渐近分离。

Result: 研究发现零模型的退火自由能与零模型、植入模型的淬火自由能在所有密度参数α值下都存在严格的渐近分离，表明这些模型在整个稠密体系下都处于零温度的自旋玻璃相。由此证明了均匀随机码在删除信道中对所有删除概率p∈[0,1)都能达到正速率，特别是解决了p≥1/2体系的首次正速率结果。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅为随机子序列模型建立了严格的理论结果，还解决了删除信道中均匀随机码性能的关键问题。通过给出植入模型退火自由能的精确解析公式，为删除信道容量提供了新的上下界，这些界比现有已知的删除信道容量上下界更为接近。

Abstract: We introduce the Random Subsequence Model, a spin glass model on pairs of random strings $(X,Y) \in \{0,1\}^N \times \{0,1\}^M$ whose partition function counts subsequence embeddings of $Y$ into $X$. We study two variants: the null model, where $X$ and $Y$ are independent and uniform, and the planted model, where $X$ is uniform and $Y$ is a uniformly-random length-$M$ subsequence of $X$. We connect the Random Subsequence Model to longstanding problems in various fields, including the best rate achievable by uniformly-random codes in the deletion channel, the longest common subsequence problem between two random strings, and models of directed polymers in statistical physics.
  In the regime where $N,M\to\infty$ at a fixed ratio $α= M/N \in (0,1)$, we exhibit strict asymptotic separations between the null annealed free energy and the quenched free energies of the null and planted models at all values of the density parameter $α$. This suggests that these models are in a spin glass phase at zero temperature throughout the entire dense regime. As a consequence, we show that uniformly-random codes achieve a positive rate in the deletion channel for all deletion probabilities $p\in [0,1),$ settling multiple conjectures of the second author, Isik and Weissman (2024) and proving the first such positive rate result for the regime $p \geq 1/2$.
  We also give an exact analytic formula for the annealed free energy of the planted model for all values of the density parameter. This implies a corresponding analytic upper bound on the best rate achievable by uniformly-random codes in the deletion channel, complementing the lower bound from our first result. Our upper and lower bounds for the capacity of the deletion channel under uniform codes are far closer to each other than the best known upper and lower bounds for the capacity of the deletion channel.

### [106] [Quantum Relative-alpha-Entropies: A Structural and Geometric Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06908)
*Sayantan Roy,Atin Gayen,Aditi Kar Gangopadhyay,Sugata Gangopadhyay*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的量子相对α熵（quantum relative-alpha-entropy），它扩展了Umegaki相对熵但超越了f散度类，揭示了现有散度框架未能捕捉的量子几何效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子散度大多依赖于经典f散度或Renyi型构造，这种依赖性掩盖了若干量子几何效应。需要引入一种超越f散度类的新型量子散度来揭示量子态的相对几何特性。

Method: 引入量子相对α熵作为Umegaki相对熵的扩展，该散度具有非线性凸性性质。利用Nussbaum-Szkola型分布建立了该散度与经典相对α熵之间的精确对应关系。

Result: 提出的散度在张量积下具有可加性，在酉变换下具有不变性，且仅依赖于量子态的相对几何而非绝对大小。对于α>1的情况，该散度产生了Petz-Renyi散度的广义凸性结果，补充了α<1时的已知凸性。

Conclusion: 相对α熵代表了一种基本的几何量子可区分性概念，这一概念未被现有散度框架所捕捉，揭示了量子信息理论中新的几何结构。

Abstract: Most quantum divergences derive their structure from classical f-divergences or Renyi-type constructions, a dependence that obscures several quantum geometric effects. We introduce a quantum relative-alpha-entropy that extends Umegaki's relative entropy while falling outside the f-divergence class. The proposed divergence exhibits a nonlinear convexity property, which yields a generalized convexity result for the Petz-Renyi divergence for alpha greater than one, complementing the known convexity for alpha less than one. It is additive under tensor products, invariant under unitary transformations, and depends only on the relative geometry of quantum states rather than their absolute magnitudes. Using Nussbaum-Szkola-type distributions, we also establish an exact correspondence of this divergence with classical relative-alpha-entropy. This reveals relative-alpha-entropy as a fundamentally geometric notion of quantum distinguishability not captured by existing divergence frameworks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 量子虫洞效应会改变氢原子的超精细结构。如果量子虫洞是非穿越性的，还会导致氢原子获得非零的总有效电荷（non-zero total effective charge）。

Conclusion: 氢原子超精细结构和总电荷的高精度测量为ER = EPR效应的振幅提供了强约束条件。这些观测效应可作为检验量子引力理论中ER = EPR猜想的重要实验依据。

Abstract: According to the ER = EPR conjecture, entangled particles are connected by quantum wormholes. Under the assumption that some of the electric field surrounding an entangled charged particle leaks into the wormhole, we show that this effect will modify the hyperfine structure of the hydrogen atom. In addition, if the quantum wormholes are non-traversable, this will also lead to a non-zero total effective charge for the hydrogen atom. These effects provide strong constraints on the amplitude of this potential ER = EPR effect, given high-precision measurements of the hydrogen atom's hyperfine structure and total charge.

### [108] [Quantum Gibbs sampling through the detectability lemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07214)
*Di Fang,Jianfeng Lu,Yu Tong,Chu Zhao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用可检测性引理（detectability lemma）改进了量子计算中的吉布斯态（Gibbs state）制备方法，避免了模拟Lindbladian演化的开销，并在局部Lindbladian和谱隙（spectral gap）依赖方面实现了显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 吉布斯态制备是量子计算中的重要子程序，现有方法通常依赖于模拟Lindbladian演化，这会带来显著的计算开销。本文旨在通过新方法避免这种开销并提高制备效率。

Method: 采用可检测性引理（detectability lemma）设计新的吉布斯态制备方法，避免模拟Lindbladian演化。同时结合可检测性引理算子和量子奇异值变换（quantum singular value transformation）实现无阻挫哈密顿量（frustration-free Hamiltonians）的基态投影算子。

Result: 对于包含M项的局部Lindbladian，该方法将成本降低了O(M)倍。通过结合可检测性引理和量子奇异值变换，在谱隙依赖方面实现了二次加速（quadratic speedup）。对于局部对易哈密顿量（local commuting Hamiltonians）的吉布斯态Lindbladian，获得了对Lindbladian谱隙的二次更好依赖关系。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于可检测性引理的吉布斯态制备方法显著降低了计算成本，并在谱隙依赖方面实现了二次加速，为量子计算中的吉布斯态制备提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Gibbs state preparation is an important subroutine in quantum computing. In this work we use the detectability lemma to improve Gibbs state preparation. Specifically, we design new Gibbs state preparation methods that do not rely on simulating Lindbladian evolution, thus avoiding the overhead from it. For local Lindbladians consisting of $M$ terms, this approach reduces the cost by a factor of $O(M)$. We also combine the detectability lemma operator and quantum singular value transformation to implement ground state projection operators of frustration-free Hamiltonians, resulting in a quadratic speedup in the spectral gap dependence. Applying this method to Lindbladians for the Gibbs state of local commuting Hamiltonians, we achieve quadratically better dependence on the Lindbladian spectral gap.

### [109] [Optimization of entanglement harvesting with arbitrary temporal profiles: the limit of second order perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06303)
*Marcos Morote-Balboa,T. Rick Perche*

TL;DR: 该研究通过优化两个局域探测器与量子场真空耦合的时间轮廓，将纠缠收获（entanglement harvesting）效率提升了数个数量级，超越了二阶微扰理论的范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索当两个局域探测器以任意时间轮廓与实标量量子场真空耦合时的纠缠收获协议，旨在超越当前二阶微扰理论的限制。

Method: 采用厄米展开（Hermite expansion）高效计算闭合形式的涂抹场传播子，并将探测器间的负性（negativity）重新表述为矩阵乘积形式，在不同信号条件下优化协议。

Result: 通过优化协议，将纠缠收获效率提升了数个数量级，使当前实验提案能够超越二阶微扰理论的适用范围。

Conclusion: 该研究开发了一种有效方法，通过优化探测器耦合的时间轮廓，显著增强了纠缠收获效率，为超越微扰理论限制的实验实现提供了可能。

Abstract: We study the protocol of entanglement harvesting when two local probes couple to the vacuum of a real scalar quantum field with arbitrary temporal profiles. We use a Hermite expansion to efficiently compute smeared field propagators in closed-form, recasting the negativity between the probes as a matrix product. We then optimize the protocol under different signalling conditions, enhancing entanglement harvesting by several orders of magnitude. This optimization would take current experimental proposals beyond the regime of second order perturbation theory.

</details>


### [110] [Probing the Planck scale with quantum computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06322)
*Boaz Katz,Shlomi Kotler*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（general relativity）与量子力学（quantum mechanics）在普朗克尺度（Planck scale）上存在不相容性，需要通过超越经典极限的量子计算来检验这一根本矛盾。

Method: 通过量化逻辑量子比特（logical qubit）数量与挑战经典性程度的关系，并考虑从实验室到可观测宇宙（observable universe）所有尺度的计算和通信操作成本。

Result: 研究发现500个逻辑量子比特足以否定局限于实验室的理论，而1600个逻辑量子比特的计算机将全面挑战经典极限，当前商业量子计算机的发展计划预计将超越这一限制。

Abstract: General relativity and quantum mechanics are incompatible at the Planck scale. This contention can be examined if a quantum computer is set to operate at a rate that exceeds the classical limit of one operation per Planck volume-time, or equivalently $2^{491}$ m$^{-3}$ s$^{-1}$. Here we quantify the relation between the logical qubit count and the extent to which classicality is challenged. We argue that 500 logical qubits are sufficient to reject theories confined to a laboratory. We account for the operational cost of computation and communication at all scales up to and including the observable universe, ultimately constrained by a 1600-logical-qubit computer. Remarkably, current plans for commercial quantum computers are projected to surpass this limit, thereby putting the quantum-gravity standoff to the test.

### [111] [Emergence of Non-Markovian Classical-Quantum Dynamics from Decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06891)
*Shogo Tomizuka,Hiroki Takeda*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明经典-量子动力学（classical-quantum dynamics）可以作为完全量子系统在退相干下的有效描述，为完全量子与经典-量子动力学之间建立了桥梁。研究推导了非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的约化动力学，并提出了经典-量子解释有效的具体判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力的本质尚未得到实验验证，而经典-量子动力学作为引力的替代描述已被提出。本研究旨在探索经典-量子动力学是否可以作为完全量子系统在退相干下的有效描述，从而为理解量子与经典描述之间的关系提供理论桥梁。

Method: 通过一个显式隐藏模型，其中介子（mediator）耦合到未观测的环境自由度，推导出约化动力学。该方法识别了经典-量子解释有效的具体判据：与介子部分相关的半维格纳算子（semi-Wigner operator）必须保持半正定，这可以表示为控制演化的非局域核（nonlocal kernels）的正性条件。

Result: 研究证明经典-量子动力学普遍地作为完全量子系统在退相干下的有效描述出现。在短记忆极限下，约化演化再现了Oppenheim及其合作者的马尔可夫经典-量子动力学。结果还表明经典介子可以从退相干的量子动力学中有效产生。

Conclusion: 经典介子可以从退相干的量子动力学中有效产生，因此实验与经典-量子模型的一致性并不能唯一确定介子是否本质上是经典的。这一发现对解释引力介导纠缠（gravity-mediated entanglement）等桌面实验的结果具有重要意义。

Abstract: The quantum nature of gravity remains experimentally unverified, despite recent proposals to probe it using tabletop experiments such as gravity-mediated entanglement schemes. In parallel, consistent formulations of classical--quantum dynamics have been developed as alternative descriptions of gravity, in which quantum matter interacts with a classical mediator assumed to be fundamentally classical. In this work, we show that classical--quantum dynamics arise generically as an effective description of fully quantum systems under decoherence, providing a bridge between fully quantum and classical--quantum dynamics. We derive the reduced dynamics, which are generically non-Markovian, using an explicit hidden model in which the mediator is coupled to unobserved environmental degrees of freedom. We identify a concrete criterion for when a classical--quantum interpretation is valid: the semi-Wigner operator associated with the mediator sector must remain positive semidefinite, which can be expressed as a positivity condition on nonlocal kernels governing the evolution. In the short-memory limit, the reduced evolution reproduces Markovian classical--quantum dynamics of Oppenheim and collaborators. Our results imply that a classical mediator can arise effectively from decohered quantum dynamics, so that experimental agreement with classical-quantum models does not uniquely determine whether the mediator is fundamentally classical.

### [112] [Quantum Fragmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06461)
*Yiqiu Han,Oliver Hart,Alexey Khudorozhkov,Rahul Nandkishore*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种系统构建量子希尔伯特空间碎片化哈密顿量的协议，该协议能够将经典碎片化模型提升为量子碎片化模型，其Krylov扇区结构只能在纠缠基中完全解析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有经典碎片化模型的Krylov扇区结构可以在局域基中解析，但量子碎片化模型需要新的系统构建方法。本文旨在开发一种协议，能够从经典碎片化模型（甚至非碎片化模型如Ising模型）构造量子碎片化哈密顿量。

Method: 采用Rokhsar-Kivelson类型构造，将经典碎片化模型作为输入，通过系统协议提升为量子碎片化模型。在一维情况下详细解释了如何标记和计数Krylov扇区，并提出了实验可验证的方案，包括制备特定初态和对约化密度矩阵进行层析成像。

Result: 成功构建了量子碎片化哈密顿量，其Krylov扇区结构只能在纠缠基中完全解析。分析了量子碎片化底层纠缠基的纠缠结构，明确区分了经典碎片化和一般哈密顿量在其本征基中的平凡"碎片化"。还将构造扩展到高维，提供了二维的显式原理证明示例。

Conclusion: 该协议为系统探索量子碎片化开辟了新途径，能够从经典碎片化模型（包括非碎片化输入）构造量子碎片化哈密顿量，其纠缠基结构是量子碎片化的关键特征。

Abstract: We introduce a systematic protocol for constructing quantum Hilbert-space-fragmented Hamiltonians, whose Krylov-sector structure, unlike in classically fragmented models, can be fully resolved only in an entangled basis. The protocol takes as input a classically fragmented model and uses a Rokhsar-Kivelson type construction to promote it to a quantum fragmented model. Notably, the procedure also works with non-fragmented inputs (such as Ising models). We explain how the Krylov sectors of the resulting quantum fragmented model may be labeled and counted in one dimension, and outline experimentally accessible verification of quantum fragmentation, assuming the ability to prepare specific initial states and perform tomography on reduced density matrices. We further analyze the entanglement structure of the entangled basis underlying quantum fragmentation, which sharply distinguishes it from both classical fragmentation and the trivial "fragmentation" of generic Hamiltonians in their eigenbasis. We also extend the construction to higher dimensions, with an explicit proof of principle example in two dimensions. We expect these results to open a new route to the systematic exploration of quantum fragmentation.

### [113] [Complete coherent control of spin qubits in self-assembled InAs quantum dots under oblique magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07074)
*I. Samaras,K. Barr,C. Schneider,S. Höfling,K. G. Lagoudakis*

Main category: quant-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索传统Voigt几何结构之外的磁场配置对量子比特控制的影响。传统方法通常要求纯Voigt几何结构，这限制了器件设计和场对准的灵活性。

Method: 研究使用自组装InAs负电荷量子点（negatively charged quantum dot）中的单个自旋量子比特，在倾斜磁场下进行实验。通过调节外加磁场的方向来调控基态自旋本征态的组成，并观察拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）和拉姆齐条纹（Ramsey fringes）。

Result: 在倾斜磁场配置下，基态自旋本征态被发现是裸电子自旋的不等叠加，其组成可通过外加磁场方向调节。研究实现了任意单量子比特旋转，并直接与Voigt几何结构下的结果进行比较。

Conclusion: 自旋量子比特控制不一定需要纯Voigt几何结构，倾斜磁场下同样可以实现完全相干控制。这放宽了器件和场对准的限制，为半导体量子点中量子信息处理架构的设计和优化提供了更灵活的途径。

Abstract: We demonstrate complete coherent control of a single spin qubit confined in a self-assembled InAs negatively charged quantum dot subjected to an Oblique magnetic field, and directly compare this regime with the conventional Voigt geometry. In the Oblique-field configuration, the groundstate spin eigenstates are found to be unequal superpositions of the bare electron spin, with their composition tunable via the orientation of the applied field. This tunable spin mixing provides an additional degree of freedom to engineer the spin basis and associated optical couplings in the charged quantum dot system. Although this geometry has a distinct structure with important implications, it provides a regime in which we can fully and coherently control the tailored spin qubit. We observe Rabi oscillations and Ramsey fringes, and demonstrate arbitrary single-qubit rotations, enabling a direct comparison with the Voigt case. Our results establish that spin-qubit control does not necessarily require a pure Voigt geometry and can instead be achieved under Oblique magnetic fields. This relaxes constraints on device and field alignment and offers a versatile route to design and optimize quantum information processing architectures in semiconductor quantum dots.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高分辨率能量分辨光谱技术，结合第一性原理计算分析两种代表性缺陷类型。通过低温（6 K）实验对比，识别热激活晶格振动对偶极子重新定向的影响机制。

Result: 实验揭示了由声子耦合驱动的发射偶极子方向连续光谱旋转，旋转角度可达40°。低温条件下光谱梯度显著抑制，证实热激活晶格振动是偶极子重新定向的主要驱动因素。

Abstract: The design of polarization-encoded quantum interfaces relies on the assumption that solid-state emitters possess static transition dipoles defined by the host lattice symmetry. Here, we demonstrate the vibronic breakdown of this static dipole approximation in hexagonal boron nitride quantum emitters. Through high-resolution energy-resolved spectroscopy, we reveal a continuous, spectral rotation of the emission dipole orientation reaching up to 40$^{\circ}$, driven by coupling to the phonon bath. This spectral gradient is significantly suppressed at cryogenic temperatures (6 K), identifying thermally activated lattice vibrations as the primary driver of the dipole reorientation. First-principles calculations on two representative defect types indicate the microscopic origin of this phenomenon as a coordinate-dependent transition dipole, where phonon-induced atomic displacements fundamentally perturb the electronic wavefunctions. By comparing the distinct defect environments, we demonstrate that the magnitude of the polarization rotation scales with the strength of the vibronic coupling. Our results not only identify a fundamental limit for polarization fidelity in solid-state quantum networks but also suggest a new class of strain-tunable quantum photonic devices based on vibronic dipole reorientation.

### [115] [Interaction-Mediated Non-Reciprocal Dynamics in Open Quantum Systems: From an Exactly Solvable Model to Generic Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07346)
*Pietro Borchia,Johannes Knolle,Andreas Nunnenkamp*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究展示了密度-密度相互作用（density-density interactions）如何在开放量子多体系统中传递浴诱导的非互易性（non-reciprocity），通过精确可解的Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型揭示了相互作用重塑激发动力学的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 储层工程（reservoir engineering）已成为实现开放量子多体系统中非互易动力学（non-reciprocal dynamics）的有力范式。本研究旨在探索相互作用如何在不同自由度间传递浴诱导的非互易性。

Method: 研究采用具有全对全Hatsugai-Kohmoto相互作用的一维自旋-1/2费米子晶格（one-dimensional lattice of spin-1/2 fermions），在工程化储层（engineered reservoir）存在下分析其Lindbladian动力学。通过建立精确可解性（exact solvability），并分析驱动-耗散费米-哈伯德链（driven-dissipative Fermi-Hubbard chain）来验证局部相互作用下的机制持续性。

Result: 非互易性与相互作用的相互作用（interplay）定性重塑了激发的动力学（dynamics of excitations）。相互作用甚至在未直接耦合到储层的自旋扇区（spin sectors）中诱导出定向漂移（directional drift）。对于局部相互作用，相同的机制在驱动-耗散费米-哈伯德链中持续存在。

Conclusion: Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型成为相互作用介导的非互易多体动力学（interaction-mediated non-reciprocal many-body dynamics）的最小且精确可解平台。密度-密度相互作用能够有效传递浴诱导的非互易性，为开放量子系统中的非互易现象提供了新机制。

Abstract: Reservoir engineering has emerged as a powerful paradigm to realize non-reciprocal dynamics in open quantum many-body systems. Here, we show that density-density interactions can transfer bath-induced non-reciprocity between different degrees of freedom. Specifically, we investigate a one-dimensional lattice of spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ fermions with all-to-all Hatsugai-Kohmoto interactions in the presence of an engineered reservoir. We establish the exact solvability of the Lindbladian dynamics and show that the interplay between non-reciprocity and interactions qualitatively reshapes the dynamics of excitations. Remarkably, interactions induce directional drift even in spin sectors that are not directly coupled to the reservoir. By analyzing a driven-dissipative Fermi-Hubbard chain, we show that the same mechanism persists for local interactions. The Hatsugai-Kohmoto model thus emerges as a minimal, exactly solvable platform for interaction-mediated non-reciprocal many-body dynamics.

### [118] [Constraints on a fifth force from the stellar orbits around the central supermassive black hole of the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06364)
*Predrag Jovanović,Duško Borka,Vesna Borka Jovanović*

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟银河系中心S2恒星在汤川引力模型下的轨道，利用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛方法拟合观测数据，约束了第五种力的强度δ和范围λ参数，并探讨了第五种力对S2恒星史瓦西进动的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究银河系中心（Galactic Center）是否存在第五种力（fifth force），以及这种力对围绕中心超大质量黑洞运行的恒星轨道可能产生的影响。特别关注第五种力是否能够解释S2恒星轨道与广义相对论预测之间的微小偏差。

Method: 研究采用汤川引力模型（Yukawa gravity model）模拟恒星轨道，该模型预测了第五种力的出现。通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛方法（Markov chain Monte Carlo method）将模拟轨道与观测到的S2恒星围绕人马座A*（Sgr A*）的轨道进行拟合，从而约束描述第五种力强度δ和范围λ的汤川相互作用参数。

Result: 研究结果显示，随着第五种力范围λ的增加，其强度δ也相应增大，相对误差Δδ/δ则减小。在三种不同范围情况下（几百AU、约一千AU、几千AU），第五种力强度分别为δ∼0.005、0.02和0.15。这些结果与先前研究及其他作者的结果一致。此外，研究还发现所有三种情况下的估计值在误差区间内都与GRAVITY Collaboration测量的f_SP = 1.10±0.19值兼容。

Conclusion: 研究表明，第五种力可能存在于银河系中心，其参数可以通过S2恒星轨道观测数据进行约束。第五种力能够解释S2恒星史瓦西进动（Schwarzschild precession）与广义相对论预测之间的微小差异，所有三种范围情况下的估计都与测量值在误差范围内一致。

Abstract: Here we investigate a possible presence of a fifth force at the Galactic Center (GC), and its potential influence on the stellar orbits around the central supermassive black hole of our Galaxy. For this purpose we simulated the stellar orbits in a Yukawa gravity model that predicts the emergence of a fifth force, and fitted them into the observed orbit of S2 star around Sgr A* at the GC. The fitting was performed using Markov chain Monte Carlo method which enabled us to constrain the parameters of Yukawa interaction describing the strength $δ$ and the range $λ$ of a fifth force. We studied the following cases for a fifth force range $λ$, when it is: i) about a few hundred AU (i.e. deep inside the orbit of S2 star), ii) about a thousand AU (i.e. approximately the size of S2 star orbit), and iii) several thousand AU (i.e. much larger than the size of S2 star orbit). The obtained results showed that as the range $λ$ of a fifth force increases, its strength $δ$ also increases and relative error $Δδ/δ$ decreases. The resulting fifth-force strengths in all three cases are respectively: $δ\sim$ 0.005, 0.02 and 0.15. These results are consistent with the corresponding results of both our previous studies and those of other authors, regardless of the different Yukawa-like potentials used to model a fifth force. In addition, we also studied whether the possible small discrepancies from the prediction of General Relativity for the Schwarzschild precession of S2 star could be caused by a fifth force. For this purpose we used the $f_\mathrm{SP}$ parameter that was recently measured in the case of S2 star by GRAVITY Collaboration in 2020. We found that the obtained estimates in all three cases are compatible, within the error intervals, with the measured value of $f_\mathrm{SP} = 1.10\pm 0.19$.

</details>

### [119] [Cholesteric Fingers from a Magnetic Perspective: Topology, Energetics, and Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06660)
*Takayuki Shigenaga,Andrey O. Leonov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究建立了手性液晶与手性磁体中拓扑孤子的统一描述框架，揭示了胆甾相手指（cholesteric fingers）作为由meron构成的复合手性孤子本质，并系统分析了其拓扑结构、相互作用及集体态相行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性液晶（chiral liquid crystals）与手性磁体（chiral magnets）中的拓扑孤子（topological solitons）具有密切相关的连续介质理论描述（Frank-Oseen和Dzyaloshinskii模型），但缺乏统一的理论框架。研究旨在利用这种对应关系，发展对受限胆甾相手指及其磁性对应物的统一描述。

Method: 在包含体各向异性（bulk anisotropies）和表面各向异性（surface anisotropies）的连续介质框架内，分析两种主要手指类型（CF-1和CF-2）的拓扑结构、相互作用和集体态。采用同伦（homotopic）视角，将纹理对应到skyrmions和droplets。

Result: 胆甾相手指是由meron构成的复合手性孤子：CF-2对应具有单位拓扑电荷的bimeron，CF-1是两个具有相同涡旋度的meron构成的拓扑平凡复合体。强垂直锚定（homeotropic anchoring）引起限制效应，重塑meron结构并重新分布薄膜厚度上的拓扑电荷。孤立手指在均匀态下呈排斥相互作用，表现为类粒子行为；当孤立手指能量为负时，出现周期性相，伴随发散晶格周期的成核型转变。在锥形背景中，相互作用因畸变区域重叠而变为吸引性。薄膜厚度控制稳定性：小厚度时孤子坍缩，大厚度时bimeron在表面稳定态和体态间呈现双稳态。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了手性液晶与手性磁体中拓扑孤子的统一描述，揭示了胆甾相手指作为复合手性孤子的本质特征。通过系统分析拓扑结构、相互作用和相行为，为理解受限几何中手性材料的拓扑纹理提供了普适框架，并阐明了厚度调控对孤子稳定性和结构的关键作用。

Abstract: Chiral liquid crystals and chiral magnets host a wide variety of topological solitons described by closely related continuum theories, namely the Frank-Oseen and Dzyaloshinskii models. Exploiting this correspondence, we develop a unified description of cholesteric fingers in confined liquid crystals and their magnetic counterparts. Within a continuum framework including bulk and surface anisotropies, we analyze the topology, structure, interactions, and collective states of the two main finger types, CF-1 and CF-2.
  We show that cholesteric fingers are composite chiral solitons built from merons. CF-2 corresponds to a bimeron with unit topological charge, while CF-1 is a topologically trivial composite of two merons with identical vorticities. From a homotopic viewpoint these textures correspond to skyrmions and droplets. Strong homeotropic anchoring induces confinement effects that reshape the meron structure and redistribute topological charge across the film thickness.
  Isolated fingers in the homogeneous state interact repulsively and behave as particle-like objects. Periodic phases emerge when the energy of an isolated finger becomes negative, leading to nucleation-type transitions with a diverging lattice period. Degenerate finger types allow mixed periodic sequences, analogous to stacking polytypes. In a conical background, interactions become attractive due to overlap of distortion regions.
  Film thickness controls stability and structure: at small thickness solitons collapse, while at large thickness bimerons exhibit bistability between surface-stabilized and bulk-like states.

</details>


### [120] [Two-dimensional active polar semiflexible polymer under shear flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06428)
*A. Lamura,R. G. Winkler*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟探讨了半柔性活性极性聚合物在线性流动下的非平衡结构与动力学特性，揭示了剪切流对聚合物构象、取向、翻滚运动及流变性质的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解半柔性活性极性聚合物（semiflexible active polar polymers）在剪切流作用下的非平衡行为，特别是流动如何影响聚合物的构象变化、取向排列、翻滚动力学及流变特性。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，将聚合物限制在二维空间中，并浸没于采用布朗多粒子碰撞动力学（Brownian Multiparticle Collision Dynamics）方法描述的流体中，研究其在施加线性剪切流下的行为。

Result: 剪切流导致聚合物构象变化，使其沿流动方向取向排列，并在高流速下诱发翻滚运动；在中等、活性依赖的剪切速率区间，观察到沿梯度方向的均方端到端距离具有特征标度指数，该指数由聚合物半柔性决定；翻滚动力学呈现特征时间，对魏森贝格数（Weissenberg number）的依赖性比柔性活性或被动聚合物更强；活性显著影响半柔性聚合物的流变性质，甚至在弱流动下可能导致负粘度；在极高剪切速率下，剪切主导活性，聚合物表现出被动行为。

Conclusion: 半柔性活性极性聚合物在剪切流下的行为表现出复杂的活性与流动耦合效应，其构象、动力学和流变性质强烈依赖于剪切速率和活性强度，揭示了活性物质在流动环境中的独特非平衡物理特性。

Abstract: The nonequilibrium structural and dynamical properties of semiflexible active polar polymers subject to linear flow are studied by numerical simulations. Filaments are confined in two dimensions and immersed in a fluid described by the Brownian Multiparticle Collision Dynamics approach. The applied shear flow causes conformational changes of a polymer, aligns it along the flow direction, and induces a tumbling motion at large flow rates. In an intermediate, activity-dependent shear-rate regime, a characteristic scaling exponent for the mean-square end-to-end distance along the gradient direction is observed. This exponent appears to be determined by the semiflexibility of the polymer. The tumbling dynamics exhibits a characteristic time, with a stronger dependence on the Weissenberg number than that of flexible active or passive polymers. Activity strongly impacts the rheological properties of the semiflexible polymers, and even implies a negative viscosity for weak flows. At very large values of the shear rate, shear dominates over activity and passive-polymer behavior is assumed.

</details>


### [121] [Frictional sliding strength of knotted and capstan configurations along the axis of a cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06962)
*Javier Sabater,Ji-Sung Park,Jérôme Crassous,Sébastien Neukirch,Pedro M. Reis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验、数值模拟和理论分析，揭示了细丝与圆柱体在打结（丁香结）和非打结（绞盘）配置下滑动强度的超线性缩放行为，并建立了统一的力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究报道了弹塑性细丝外科结的超线性缩放行为，本研究旨在探究这种非线性行为的来源，并检验其是否普遍存在于不同材料和几何配置中。

Method: 采用多材料实验（弹性棒、金属线、编织绳）、三维有限元模拟（FEM）和降阶离散弹性杆模拟（DER），并建立基于平面弹性线理论的解析模型分析绞盘配置。

Result: 实验证实了丁香结的超线性缩放行为与材料无关；数值模拟重现了实验规律；绞盘配置在较大角度下也表现出类似行为，但在较小角度下过渡到线性；解析模型成功解释了超线性行为源于法向力与接触弧长的耦合演化。

Conclusion: 研究建立了适用于不同材料、几何和拓扑结构的统一力学框架，揭示了细丝-圆柱接触系统中超线性缩放行为的普遍机制，并预测了向线性行为过渡的条件。

Abstract: We investigate the sliding strength of thin filaments in frictional contact with a translating cylinder, perpendicular to the filaments' axes, in knotted (clove hitch) and unknotted (capstan) configurations. Recent work reported superlinear scaling for surgical knots with elasto-plastic filaments [1]. Testing the clove hitch with various materials (elastomeric rods, metallic wires, braided ropes) reveals similar nonlinear behavior, ruling out plasticity. To explore the source of the previously reported nonlinear behavior, we perform three-dimensional FEM simulations (resolving full 3D mechanics) and reduced-order DER simulations (isolating geometric effects by neglecting cross-sectional deformation). Both FEM and DER simulations reproduce the experimental scaling. Simplifying the knot topology by studying capstan angles from $π/4$ to $4π$ yields comparable superlinear behavior, transitioning to linearity at smaller angles. We rationalize the results by developing an analytical model based on planar elastica theory for the capstan configuration (which exhibits behavior similar to the clove hitch but with a simpler topology). The model reproduces the observed superlinear behavior and rationalizes it by coupling the evolution of normal forces and contact arclength during tightening. The analysis further predicts transition to linearity when full contact between the filament and the cylinder is established, providing a mechanical framework applicable across materials, geometries, and topologies.

</details>


### [122] [Using test particle sum rules to improve approximations in classical DFT : White-Bear and White-Bear mark II versions of the Lutsko Functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07050)
*Melih Gül,Roland Roth,Robert Evans*

TL;DR: 该研究将测试粒子求和规则（test-particle sum rules）应用于硬球（hard-sphere）流体密度泛函的构建，通过优化Lutsko形式的基本测度理论（fundamental measure theory）参数，开发了比现有White-Bear泛函更精确和一致的密度泛函。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是扩展先前工作中基于测试粒子求和规则（test-particle sum rules）的硬球（hard-sphere）流体密度泛函构建方法，将其应用于更先进的White-Bear（WB）和White-Bear mark II泛函框架，以提升密度泛函的精度和一致性。

Method: 研究方法采用测试粒子求和规则（test-particle sum rules）来确定Lutsko形式的基本测度理论（fundamental measure theory, FMT）中的两个自由参数，通过最小化不同热力学路径（routes）对过剩化学势（excess chemical potential）和等温压缩率（isothermal compressibility）的相对误差来实现参数优化。

Result: 研究结果表明，优化得到的Lutsko WB泛函，特别是Lutsko WB mark II，在精度和一致性方面普遍优于早期处理方法获得的泛函，实现了更准确的热力学性质预测。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将测试粒子求和规则（test-particle sum rules）方法扩展到先进的白熊（White-Bear）泛函框架，通过参数优化获得了更精确和一致的硬球（hard-sphere）流体密度泛函，为经典密度泛函理论的发展提供了改进方案。

Abstract: In a recent paper [M. Gül et al., Phys. Rev. E, 110 (6), 064115] we showed that test particle sum rules, which address the excess chemical potential and isothermal compressibility, could be used to develop new and accurate classical density functionals for hard-sphere (HS) fluids. Here we extend our approach to the construction of HS functionals building upon the state of art White-Bear (WB) and White-Bear mark II functionals. Employing the same test-particle sum rules we determine the two free parameters in the Lutsko [James F. Lutsko, Phys. Rev. E, 102, 062137] formulation of fundamental measure theory (FMT) by minimizing the relative errors between different routes to the two thermodynamic quantities. The resulting optimized Lutsko WB functionals, especially Lutsko WB mark II, are generally more accurate and consistent than those obtained in earlier treatments.

</details>


### [123] [Phase coherence and disorder-induced wave propagation in micromotor arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07080)
*Romane Braun,Alexis Poncet,Alexandre Morin,Denis Bartolo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探索了由数千个3D打印旋转马达组成的微观元机器（metamachines）的自组织行为，揭示了这些马达如何通过未指定方向的进动（precession）形成反铁磁相（antiferromagnetic phase）、相位相干性（phase coherence）以及淬火无序（quenched disorder）引发的相位波（phase waves）传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器通过预设程序将动力转换为预定动力学和功能，而生命系统（如细胞和动物群体）则通过自组织实现复杂功能。现有研究多关注平移自推进（translational self-propulsion），而主动旋转（active rotation）作为设计更广泛活性材料（animate materials）的途径尚未充分探索。

Method: 研究采用由数千个3D打印旋转马达组成的微观元机器系统，分析这些马达在未指定方向进动时的集体行为。通过实验观察和理论解释，探索了系统的自组织动力学。

Result: 研究首先展示了马达如何集体排列形成纯净的反铁磁相（antiferromagnetic phase）。其次阐明了转子进动中时空有序性的出现，表现为相位相干性（phase coherence）。最后揭示了淬火无序（quenched disorder）如何引发相位波（phase waves）在不匹配转速的自组织区域间自由传播。

Conclusion: 基于旋转子的元机器系统可以揭示生命系统中节律波（metachronal-wave）的形成机制，并为合成活性材料中的信号传播提供新见解。这表明主动旋转系统为理解生物自组织和设计新型功能材料提供了重要途径。

Abstract: Machines are designed, assembled, and programmed to convert power into predetermined dynamics and functions. In contrast, living systems such as interacting cells and animal groups self-organize, synchronize, and perform complex tasks without predefined patterns. Inspired by these decentralized architectures, experiments have shown that small assemblies of elastically coupled self-propelled robots can achieve two fundamental functionalities observed in nature: collective motion and oscillatory deformations. However, biological inspiration has steered research toward translational self-propulsion, while active rotation remains an underexplored route to designing broader animate materials. Here, we study the self-organization of microscopic metamachines composed of thousands of 3D-printed rotary motors. We first demonstrate and explain how motors precessing in unspecified directions collectively arrange their dynamics into a pristine antiferromagnetic phase. Next, we elucidate the emergence of spatiotemporal order in the form of phase coherence in the rotors' precession. Finally, we show how quenched disorder initiates the free propagation of phase waves across self-organized regions with mismatched rotation speeds. Our results suggest that spinner-based metamachines could illuminate metachronal-wave formation in living systems, and signal propagation in synthetic animate materials.

</details>

### [124] [Defect-free arrays at the thousand-atom scale in a 4-K cryogenic environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07205)

TL;DR: 该论文报道了一种在4K低温环境下结合高数值孔径光学系统的大规模光镊阵列平台，实现了约5000秒的原子囚禁寿命，并成功制备了包含1024个原子的无缺陷阵列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发一个兼容里德堡态（Rydberg-state）操控的低温平台，以显著延长大规模光镊阵列的实验准备时间，为模拟和数字量子计算提供新的可能性。

Method: 采用4K低温平台结合高数值孔径（high numerical aperture）光学系统，通过组合两种不同波长的囚禁激光，并在重排和成像过程中最小化原子损失，实现大规模光镊阵列的制备。

Result: 实现了约5000秒的原子囚禁寿命，显著延长了实验时间，并成功制备了包含1024个原子的无缺陷（defect-free）阵列。

Conclusion: 该低温设计为模拟和数字量子计算（analog and digital quantum computing）开辟了令人兴奋的前景，展示了在低温环境下实现大规模原子阵列的可行性。

Abstract: We report on a cryogenic platform at 4 K incorporating high numerical aperture optics for the generation of large-scale tweezers arrays, and compatible with Rydberg-state manipulation. We achieve trapping lifetimes of around 5000 s, significantly extending the available experimental time for the preparation of large-scale arrays. By combining two trapping lasers at different wavelengths and by minimizing other atom losses during the rearrangement and imaging processes, we demonstrate the preparation of defect-free arrays with up to 1024 atoms. Our cryogenic design opens exciting prospects for analog and digital quantum computing.

### [125] [Two-dimensional shelving spectroscopy of ultraviolet ground state transitions in dysprosium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07283)
*Kevin S. H. Ng,Paul Uerlings,Fiona Hellstern,Jens Hertkorn,Luis Weiß,Stephan Welte,Tilman Pfau,Ralf Klemt*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该研究系统探索了镝（dysprosium）原子中多个紫外（UV）基态跃迁的光谱特性，这些跃迁在偶极原子实验中很少被利用，但具有与常用最强跃迁相当的衰变强度，可用于光学钟、量子气体显微镜和超越标准模型物理探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 镧系元素（lanthanides）具有开放的壳层电子结构和大的磁矩，为激光冷却、囚禁和相干控制提供了丰富的跃迁谱。然而，低于400纳米的众多紫外跃迁在偶极原子实验中很少被利用，这些跃迁对于光学布居激发态和多种应用具有重要意义。

Method: 采用二维存储光谱（two-dimensional shelving spectroscopy）技术，该技术提高了检测灵敏度，并提供了一种直接确定超精细同位素结构和激发态总角动量J的方法。通过测量同位素位移（isotope shifts）、超精细系数（hyperfine coefficients），并创建金图（King plots）来确定这些跃迁的电子性质。

Result: 研究发现镝原子的多个紫外激发态具有最大的衰变强度，这些强度与偶极原子中最常用的最强跃迁相当。通过光谱测量获得了同位素位移、超精细系数等关键参数，并利用金图分析了这些跃迁的电子特性。

Conclusion: 这些紫外跃迁的知识对于光学布居第一激发态至关重要，可用于构建光学钟（optical clock）、实现量子气体显微镜（quantum gas microscopy）中的高分辨率成像，以及通过增强的希夫矩（Schiff moments）探测镧系原子核以寻找超越标准模型的物理现象。

Abstract: The open inner-shell electronic structure of lanthanides with large magnetic moments gives rise to a rich spectrum of transitions available for laser cooling, trapping, and coherent control. Despite this, the large number of ultraviolet (UV) transitions below 400nm have so far been rarely utilized in dipolar atom experiments. Here, we investigate multiple UV ground state transitions in dysprosium. Several of these UV excited states have the largest decay strengths to the ultralong-lived, low-lying first excited state which are comparable to the most commonly used strongest transitions found in dipolar atoms. Using two-dimensional shelving spectroscopy which improves detection sensitivity and provides a straightforward way to determine the hyperfine-isotope structure and excited state total angular momentum $J$, we measure isotope shifts, hyperfine coefficients, and create King plots to determine their electronic nature. Such knowledge of these UV transitions which analogously exist in other magnetic atoms is important for optically populating the first excited state and can be used towards creating an optical clock, high resolution imaging in quantum gas microscopy, and probing lanthanide nuclei with enhanced Schiff moments in search of physics beyond the standard model.

</details>

### [126] [Ontology-based knowledge graph infrastructure for interoperable atomistic simulation data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06230)
*Abril Azocar Guzman,Sarath Menon,Tilmann Hickel,Stefan Sandfeld*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于本体论（ontology）的基础设施，将原子尺度模拟数据表示为知识图谱（knowledge graph），旨在解决数据格式异构、元数据不完整和工作流表示缺乏标准化等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子尺度模拟数据的重用常受限于异构格式、不完整元数据以及工作流和溯源信息缺乏标准化表示。这些限制阻碍了数据的可发现性、互操作性和重用性。

Method: 该方法结合领域本体论与软件框架，支持从现有数据集和模拟工作流生成点捕获数据。异构数据被归一化为统一的本体对齐表示，工作流则以机器可读形式表示，支持前向溯源追踪和计算过程的部分重建。

Conclusion: 这项工作为提升原子尺度模拟数据的可发现性（findability）、互操作性（interoperability）和重用性（reuse）提供了一个实用框架，实现了跨数据集的一致查询和分析。

Abstract: The reuse of atomistic simulation data is often limited by heterogeneous formats, incomplete metadata, and a lack of standardized representations of workflows and provenance. Here we present an ontology-based infrastructure for representing and integrating atomistic simulation data as a knowledge graph. The approach combines domain ontologies with a software framework that enables data capture both from existing datasets and directly from simulation workflows at the point of generation. Heterogeneous data from multiple sources are normalized into a common, ontology-aligned representation, enabling consistent querying and analysis across datasets. We demonstrate these capabilities through the integration of grain boundary data, cross-dataset analysis of material properties, and extraction of derived thermodynamic quantities from existing simulations. In addition, workflows are represented in a machine-readable form, enabling both forward provenance tracking and partial reconstruction of computational procedures. The resulting knowledge graph contains over 750,000 triples describing nearly 8,000 computational samples. This work provides a practical framework for improving the findability, interoperability, and reuse of atomistic simulation data.

### [127] [Observation of roton emission from a quantized vortex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06498)
*A. Lester,N. Morrison,F. Novotny,D. Schmoranzer,S. Ó Peatáin,V. Zavjalov,V. Tsepelin,S. Kafanov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 在零温极限下，无粘性量子流体中的湍流能量级联终止机制是量子流体动力学的核心挑战。本研究通过纳米机械谐振器直接观测到单个量子化涡旋的旋子发射，揭示了强关联量子液体中的主要耗散通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零温极限下，无粘性量子流体中湍流能量级联的终止机制是量子流体动力学的基础性挑战。现有理论强调声子发射，但未能解释超流氦-4中由强原子间关联产生的旋子极小值（roton minimum）。

Method: 使用10 mK温度下的高品质因子纳米机械谐振器，直接观测单个量子化涡旋（quantized vortex）的旋子发射。通过测量临界速度下的耗散起始和每周期能量损失，定量分析旋子能隙能量。

Result: 在临界速度下观察到尖锐的耗散起始，测量的每周期能量损失定量对应于旋子能隙能量（roton gap energy）。这证实了旋子发射是强关联量子液体中的主要耗散通道。

Conclusion: 研究通过建立旋子发射作为强关联量子液体的主要耗散通道，解决了零温能量弛豫的长期谜题。这一发现为理解无粘性量子流体中的湍流能量级联终止机制提供了关键实验证据。

Abstract: Turbulence in inviscid quantum fluids offers unparalleled access to the universal principles of non-equilibrium dynamics, spanning a vast range of length scales from macroscopic flow down to the individual vortex core. In the zero-temperature limit, the microscopic mechanism by which the turbulent energy cascade terminates in the absence of viscosity remains a foundational challenge in quantum hydrodynamics. While prevailing theoretical descriptions prioritize phonon emission, they fail to account for the strong interatomic correlations that give rise to the roton minimum in superfluid $^4\mathrm{He}$. Here, we report the direct observation of roton emission from a single quantized vortex using a high-quality-factor nanomechanical resonator at 10 mK. We identify a sharp onset of dissipation at a critical velocity, and measure the energy loss per cycle, which corresponds quantitatively to the roton gap energy. Our findings address the long-standing mystery of zero-temperature energy relaxation by establishing roton emission as the primary dissipation channel in strongly correlated quantum liquids.

</details>


### [128] [Breathing Modes as a Probe of Energy Fluctuations in a Unitary Fermi Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06594)
*Shi-Guo Peng,Jing Min,Kaijun Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在具有SO(2,1)动力学对称性的标度不变量子气体中，呼吸模式振幅可作为能量涨落的直接定量探针，建立了振荡振幅与能量涨落之间的精确普适关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接测量相互作用量子多体系统中的能量涨落，特别是在远离平衡态的情况下，一直是长期存在的挑战。该研究旨在通过集体动力学来直接探测这些能量涨落。

Method: 利用具有SO(2,1)动力学对称性的标度不变量子气体，建立呼吸模式振幅与能量涨落之间的精确关系。该方法基于SU(1,1)代数的不可约表示，由Bargmann指数k标记。

Result: 建立了振荡振幅与能量涨落之间的精确普适关系，其无量纲比值仅由Bargmann指数k固定。该关系完全由对称性决定，与微观细节和激发协议无关。呼吸模式态的激发遵循由单一参数控制的普适统计分布。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通常编码在多体谱中的能量涨落可以通过集体动力学直接获取，为探测强相互作用量子系统中的非平衡能量统计提供了一条基于对称性的途径。

Abstract: Directly accessing energy fluctuations in interacting quantum many-body systems remains a long-standing challenge, especially far from equilibrium. Here we show that in scale-invariant quantum gases with SO$(2,1)$ dynamical symmetry, the amplitude of the breathing mode provides a direct and quantitative probe of energy fluctuations. We establish an exact and universal relation between the oscillation amplitude and the energy fluctuation, with a dimensionless ratio fixed solely by the Bargmann index $k$, which labels the irreducible representation of the underlying SU$(1,1)$ algebra and thereby determines the structure of the many-body spectrum and dynamics. As a consequence, this relation is fully dictated by symmetry and remains independent of microscopic details and excitation protocols. Furthermore, we show that the excitation of breathing-mode states follows a universal statistical distribution governed by a single parameter, independent of the specific driving protocol. Our findings demonstrate that energy fluctuations, typically encoded in the many-body spectrum, can be directly accessed through collective dynamics, offering a symmetry-based route to probe nonequilibrium energy statistics in strongly interacting quantum systems.

</details>


### [129] [In-situ Observation of Magnetostriction Crossover in a Strongly Dipolar Two-Dimensional Bose Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07194)
*Yifei He,Xin-Yuan Gao,Haoting Zhen,Mithilesh K. Parit,Yangqian Yan,Gyu-Boong Jo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁致伸缩作为具有强长程相互作用的偶极气体的特征性各向异性空间形变现象，其原位表征面临挑战。研究旨在解决这一表征难题，并为强偶极超流和热力学研究提供新途径。

Method: 采用准二维166Er气体的原位成像技术观测磁致伸缩交叉现象，并开发准二维Hartree-Fock平均场（Hartree-Fock-mean-field）框架作为相互作用感知的温度测量工具，通过单次拟合确定所有偶极取向下的温度和化学势。

Result: 观测到从强各向异性超流相到近各向同性正常相的磁致伸缩交叉，验证了低密度翼区有效遵循局域密度状态方程（local-density equation of state），并在单次原位图像中揭示了从各向同性热翼区到各向异性相干核心的交叉现象。

Conclusion: 该研究为未来二维强偶极超流和热力学的精确研究提供了新路径，开发的相互作用感知温度测量框架能够从单次拟合中获取全面的热力学参数信息。

Abstract: Magnetostriction, the anisotropic spatial deformation, is a hallmark of dipolar gases with strong long-range interactions, yet it poses a challenge for in-situ characterization. Here, we observe a magnetostriction crossover from the strongly anisotropic superfluid phase to the nearly isotropic normal phase using in-situ imaging of quasi-two-dimensional 166Er gases. Then, we develop a quasi-2D Hartree-Fock-mean-field framework that provides a robust tool for interaction-aware thermometry, enabling the determination of temperature and chemical potential across all dipole orientations from a single fit. We further demonstrate that the low-density wings effectively obey a local-density equation of state. Finally, we reveals the crossover from the isotropic thermal wings to the anisotropic coherent core in a single in-situ image, providing a pathway for future accurate studies of strongly dipolar superfluidity and thermodynamics in 2D.

Training physicists on containerization technologies is of utmost importance in today's research landscape. ### [131] [Solar Neutrino Flux Fluctuations Caused by Solar Gravity Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06535)
*Yoshiki Hatta,Yuuki Nakano,Sho Sugama,Masanobu Kunitomo,Hiroshi Ito,Takashi Sekii*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 该研究评估了太阳引力模式（g-modes）引起的中微子通量涨落，发现一阶涨落为零，二阶涨落包含时变和非时变成分。时变成分振幅极小（~10⁻⁹），难以通过当前探测器检测，但非时变成分导致的平均通量净增加可能不可忽略，且可能随太阳活动周期（~11年）变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估太阳引力模式（g-modes）对中微子通量涨落的影响，探讨通过中微子测量探测太阳g-modes的可能性。太阳g-modes是太阳内部的重要振荡模式，但其直接探测一直面临挑战。

Method: 基于球对称恒星的线性绝热振荡分析，评估了太阳g-modes引起的中微子通量涨落。假设g-mode振幅参数A_{nℓ}为10⁻⁵，这对应于太阳内部假定的最大相对温度扰动。

Result: 一阶涨落因几何抵消为零；二阶涨落包含时变和非时变成分。对于⁸B中微子，时变成分相对差异振幅极小（~10⁻⁹），远低于当前探测器探测极限。但非时变成分导致的平均中微子通量净增加可能不可忽略，且与A_{nℓ}²成正比。

Conclusion: 通过中微子通量测量探测单个太阳g-modes几乎不可能，但非时变成分导致的长期变化（~11年）可能提供证据。理论预测与Super-Kamiokande等实验数据的比较，可能对太阳g-modes激发机制理论施加约束。

Abstract: We have evaluated fluctuations in neutrino fluxes caused by solar gravity (g) modes based on the analysis of linear adiabatic oscillation of a spherically symmetric star. We find that the first-order fluctuation is zero due to geometrical cancellation. We still find that the second-order fluctuation is non-zero, which consists of time-varying and non-time-varying components. The amplitude of the time-varying component is small (${\sim} 10^{-9}$ in relative difference, in the case of $\mathrm{^{8}B}$ neutrino) and well below the detection limits of the current neutrino detectors, when we assume the g-mode amplitude parameter $A_{n \ell}$ to be $10^{-5}$, which corresponds to the assumed maximum relative temperature perturbation inside the Sun. Thus, it is at the moment fair to say that detecting individual solar g-modes via the solar neutrino flux measurement is almost impossible. However, the net increase in the mean neutrino flux that originates from the non-time-varying component could be non-negligible. In particular, since $A_{n \ell}$ may be related to convection amplitude, which could change in accordance with the solar magnetic activity, the total net increase in the neutrino flux, which is proportional to $A_{n \ell}^2$, should also change with the solar activity cycle. Such a long-period variation~(${\sim} 11$~years) in the neutrino flux could thus be interpreted as evidence for a bunch of solar g-modes. Comparison of the theoretical prediction with the solar neutrino measurements by, e.g., Super-Kamiokande, may have a potential to put constraints on the theory of the excitation mechanism of solar g-modes.

</details>

### [132] [Improved Implementation of Approximate Full Mass Matrix Inverse Methods into Material Point Method Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07307)
*John A. Nairn*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出改进的FMPM(k)方法，简化了材料点法（MPM）中的全质量矩阵近似计算实现，并解决了FMPM与其他基于集中质量MPM功能之间的兼容性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料点法（Material Point Method, MPM）中的近似全质量矩阵方法FMPM(k)虽然能改进网格速度计算，但在与基于集中质量（lumped mass）的其他MPM功能混合使用时会产生兼容性问题。这些功能包括基于网格的速度边界条件、多材料接触计算、裂纹接触计算和不完美界面等。

Method: 首先推导了修订的FMPM(k)实现方案，简化并澄清了可添加到MPM代码中的"FMPM循环（FMPM Loop）"。然后修改该循环，使FMPM(k)即使在需要其他先前引起冲突的MPM功能的模拟中也能良好工作。

Result: 提出的改进实现简化了FMPM循环，使其能在每个时间步仅需计算一次，刚好在更新粒子位置和速度之前。该方法解决了FMPM与基于集中质量MPM功能之间的兼容性问题，使两者能协同工作。

Conclusion: 本文提供了修订的FMPM(k)实现方案，解决了与基于集中质量MPM功能的兼容性问题。同时分析了高阶k时稳定性损失和计算成本问题，讨论了时间稳定性与阶数k的关系以及提高效率的选项。

Abstract: Approximate full mass matrix methods for the material point method, known as FMPM(k) of order k, can improve the calculation of grid velocities from grid momentum. It can be implemented in any MPM code by inserting a new calculation task whenever grid velocities are needed. The implementation recommended in this paper only needs these calculations once per time step just before when updating particle positions and velocities. FMPM implementation issues arise, however, when its methods are mixed with other MPM feature that rely on lumped mass calculations. Some common lumped-mass MPM features are grid-based, velocity boundary condition, multimaterial contact calculations, crack contact calculations, and imperfect interfaces. This paper first derives a revised FMPM(k) implementation that both simplifies and clarifies the "FMPM Loop" that can be added to MPM codes. Next, that loop is modified to allow FMPM(k) to work well even in simulations that need other MPM features that previously caused conflicts. Two other FMPM(k) issues are apparent loss of stability at very higher order k and inherent computational cost. These issues are discussed in an analysis of temporal stability as a function of order k and in consideration of options to improve efficiency.

</details>
