### [133] [Plasma Dynamics of Radiative Cooling Accretion Flow in AM Herculis with XRISM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06591)
*Yukikatsu Terada,Kaya Mori,Takayuki Hayashi,Gabriel L. Bridges,Manabu Ishida,Axel D. Schwope,Mariko Kimura,Masayoshi Nobukawa,David A. H. Buckley,Solen Balman,Taichi Ichikawa,Atsuto Matsumura,Mai Takeo,Charles J. Hailey,Gavin Ramsay,Antonio Rodriguez,Samantha Walker*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 利用XRISM/Resolve高分辨率X射线光谱对磁激变双星AM Herculis进行研究，揭示了激波等离子体中的速度梯度、温度梯度以及共振线各向异性，并首次提供了吸积柱密度的诊断方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过高分辨率X射线光谱分析，深入理解磁激变双星（magnetic cataclysmic variable）AM Herculis中吸积柱（accretion column）的物理特性，包括激波等离子体的速度场、温度分布和密度结构。

Method: 采用XRISM/Resolve高分辨率X射线光谱仪观测AM Herculis，结合同步NuSTAR数据，利用PSAC/MCVSPEC等离子体模型进行自洽分析，并通过共振线（resonance lines）的辐射转移模拟约束吸积柱密度。

Result: 所有高电离态Fe的卫星线（satellite lines）均被完全分辨；Fe XXV和Fe XXVI谱线显示明显的自旋相位调制（spin-phase-resolved modulations），揭示了激波等离子体中的体速度梯度（bulk velocity gradients）和温度梯度；共振线各向异性（resonance anisotropy）与振荡强度（oscillator strengths）呈正相关；获得自洽的激波温度（shock temperature）为24.0±0.1 keV，激波速度（shock velocity）为1,116±2 km s⁻¹，吸积柱密度约为(5-6)×10¹⁵ cm⁻³。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为吸积柱密度提供了新的诊断方法，并确定了吸积柱的几何结构：高度为200-300 km，半径为200-400 km，为理解磁激变双星中吸积过程的物理机制提供了关键观测约束。

Abstract: We present XRISM/Resolve high-resolution X-ray spectroscopy of the prototypical magnetic cataclysmic variable AM Herculis. All satellite lines of highly ionized Fe are fully resolved. Lighter element lines (Si, S, Ca) show 2 - 3 eV widths consistent with purely thermal broadening, while the broader 6 - 7 eV Fe lines require additional bulk Doppler broadening. Spin-phase-resolved modulations are clearly detected in the Fe XXV and Fe XXVI lines, with semi-amplitudes of $81.8\pm6$ km s$^{-1}$ and $132.5\pm9$ km s$^{-1}$, and mean velocities of $143.6\pm6$ km s$^{-1}$ and $225.6\pm8$ km s$^{-1}$, respectively. After removing these bulk Doppler shifts, we obtain intrinsic Doppler widths of $5.23_{-0.15}^{+0.16}$ eV for Fe XXV and $6.23_{-0.18}^{+0.19}$ eV for Fe XXVI, directly revealing gradients of bulk velocity and temperature in the cooling-flow plasma. We additionally examined the resonance anisotropy predicted by Terada et al. (1999, 2001): the equivalent widths of the Fe XXV and Fe XXVI resonance lines increase at the pole-on phase by factors of 1.30 - 1.35, in positive correlation with their oscillator strengths. Combining XRISM with simultaneous NuSTAR data and PSAC/MCVSPEC plasma models, we derive a self-consistent shock temperature of $24.0\pm0.1$ keV and shock velocity of $1,116\pm2$ km s$^{-1}$. Radiative transfer simulations of the resonance lines further constrain the shock density to about $(5 - 6)\times10^{15}$ cm$^{-3}$, providing a new density diagnostic for accretion columns. The resulting accretion column geometry has a height of 200 - 300 km and a radius of 200 - 400 km.

</details>

# eess.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [134] [Inference-Sufficient Representations for High-Throughput Measurement: Lessons from Lossless Compression Benchmarks in 4D-STEM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06221)
*Ondrej Dyck,Andrew R. Lupini,Albina Borisevich,Miaofang Chi,Rama K. Vasudevan,Stephen Jesse*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了13种无损压缩算法在4D-STEM大数据集上的性能，发现blosc_zstd在保持与gzip-9相近压缩率（平均13.5× vs 12.3×）的同时，压缩速度快19-69倍，读取速度快1.9-2.6倍。压缩性能与数据稀疏度呈幂律关系，4D-STEM数据可常规压缩超过10倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-STEM）产生多GB级数据集，导致数据采集速率与存储、传输及交互可视化能力之间的不匹配日益加剧。需要评估现有无损压缩方案以缓解这一瓶颈。

Method: 系统性地对13种无损压缩实现进行基准测试，涵盖5个代表性数据集（8 MiB至8 GiB，稀疏度49.5%-92.8%），每种方法进行10次独立运行。评估包括HDF5内置的gzip压缩以及通过hdf5plugin提供的广泛可用替代方案（如Blosc系列）。

Result: blosc_zstd实现与gzip-9相当的压缩比（平均13.5× vs 12.3×），同时压缩速度快19-69倍，读取速度快1.9-2.6倍。压缩性能与稀疏度呈幂律关系（R²=0.99），从适度稀疏数据的5×到高度稀疏数据的35×。识别出六种针对不同用例优化的顶级实现，证明4D-STEM数据可常规压缩超过10倍。

Conclusion: 虽然研究结果为无损压缩选择提供了实用指导，但更广泛的结论是：无损压缩虽能保留测量数据，但本身不能保证可持续的高通量工作流程。随着探测器速率提升，数据处理将越来越需要推理驱动的表示方法——即决定必须保留哪些数据以支持科学推理，而非默认存储完全密集的原始测量数据。

Abstract: Four-dimensional scanning transmission electron microscopy (4D-STEM) generates multi-gigabyte datasets, creating a growing mismatch between acquisition rates and practical storage, transfer, and interactive visualization capabilities. We systematically benchmark 13 lossless compression implementations across 5 representative datasets (8~MiB to 8~GiB, 49.5--92.8\% sparsity), with 10 independent runs per method. HDF5 provides built-in gzip compression, of which gzip-9 typically achieves the highest compression ratio but is slow. We therefore evaluate widely available alternatives (via hdf5plugin), including the Blosc family. As a representative comparison, blosc\_zstd achieves compression comparable to gzip-9 (mean 13.5$\times$ vs 12.3$\times$) while compressing 19--69$\times$ faster and reading 1.9--2.6$\times$ faster across datasets. Compression ratios are deterministic, and timing measurements are highly reproducible (CV $<$2\%). Compression performance follows a power law with sparsity ($R^2 = 0.99$), ranging from 5$\times$ for moderately sparse data to 35$\times$ for highly sparse data. We identify six top-performing implementations optimized for different use cases and demonstrate that 4D-STEM data can be routinely compressed by $>$10$\times$. While these results provide practical guidance for lossless compression selection, the broader conclusion is that lossless compression preserves measurements but does not by itself guarantee sustainable high-throughput workflows. As detector rates rise, data handling will increasingly require inference-driven representations -- i.e., deciding what must be preserved to support a scientific inference, rather than defaulting to storing fully dense raw measurements.

</details>

### [135] [How acausal equations emerge from causal dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07031)
*Lorenzo Gavassino*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个因果且协变稳定的动力学模型，其谱在实波数k处能够通过微观自由度的适当初始化来重现任何静止框架稳定的耗散色散关系ω(k)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在挑战微观因果性单独约束实波数k处色散关系解析形式的传统观念。通过构建一个能够重现任意线性演化方程的模型，研究者希望证明仅基于色散关系解析结构的约束（如hydrohedron界限）需要额外的假设。

Method: 研究者构建了一个因果且协变稳定（covariantly stable）的动力学模型，该模型通过适当初始化微观自由度（microscopic degrees of freedom），使其在实波数k处的谱能够重现任何静止框架稳定的耗散色散关系ω(k)。

Result: 该模型提供了一个明确的反对例，表明微观因果性（microscopic causality）本身并不约束实波数k处色散关系的解析形式。宏观可观测量可以服从任意线性演化方程，而底层动力学保持因果性，所有表观传播都编码在初始数据中。

Conclusion: 仅基于色散关系ω(k)解析结构的约束（如hydrohedron界限）需要关于复波数k平面中ω(k)对应物理模式的区域的额外假设。微观因果性单独不足以确定色散关系的具体形式。

Abstract: We construct a causal and covariantly stable kinetic model whose spectrum at real wavenumbers $k$ reproduces any rest-frame stable dissipative dispersion relation $ω(k)$ via suitable initialization of the microscopic degrees of freedom. Macroscopic observables can therefore obey arbitrary linear evolution equations (including forms that would be acausal if taken as fundamental), while the underlying dynamics remains causal, and all apparent propagation is encoded in the initial data. This provides an explicit counterexample to the idea that microscopic causality alone constrains the analytic form of dispersion relations at real $k$. In particular, bounds on transport coefficients based solely on the analytic structure of $ω(k)$, such as the hydrohedron bounds, require additional assumptions about the region in the complex $k$-plane where $ω(k)$ corresponds to physical modes.

</details>


### [136] [Relativistic Barnett effect and Curie law in a rigidly rotating free Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06248)
*M. Abedlou Ahadi,N. Sadooghi*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文结合热场论与统计力学方法，重新研究了刚性旋转费米气体中相对论性巴尼特效应引起的自旋极化。通过引入特定正则化方案计算角动量量子数求和，分离热压与热力学量，并引入自旋-化学-旋转比η调控自旋极化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新审视刚性旋转费米气体中的相对论性巴尼特效应（relativistic Barnett effect）引起的自旋极化。研究动机源于理解旋转介质中轨道角动量-旋转耦合与自旋-旋转耦合对热力学性质的贡献。

Method: 结合热场论（thermal field theory）与统计力学方法，引入特定正则化方案（regularization scheme）对角动量量子数进行求和。通过引入有效化学势（effective chemical potential）包含轨道角动量-旋转和自旋-旋转耦合贡献，并定义自旋-化学-旋转比η≡Ω⁽⁰⁾/2μ⁽⁰⁾来调控自旋极化。

Result: 研究发现热压与所有热力学量可分离为仅自旋逸度（spin fugacities）不同的两部分。自旋向下费米子的费米能（Fermi energy）低于自旋向上费米子，这一差异源于自旋-旋转耦合，与巴尼特效应一致。旋转费米气体的自旋向下组分在较低温度下稀释，磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）与转动惯量I成正比，且I在高温极限下呈现1/T行为，类似于顺磁性的居里定律（Curie law）。

Conclusion: 研究证实了刚性旋转费米气体中自旋-旋转耦合导致的自旋极化效应，与巴尼特效应一致。引入的自旋-化学-旋转比η有效调控了自旋极化程度，而转动惯量的温度依赖关系在高温下呈现类似居里定律的行为，为旋转量子系统的热力学性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: By combining methods from thermal field theory and statistical mechanics, we reexamine the spin polarization caused by the relativistic Barnett effect in a rigidly rotating Fermi gas. We determine the pressure of this medium and show that it depends on an effective chemical potential, which includes contributions from orbital angular momentum-rotation and spin-rotation coupling. We introduce a specific regularization scheme to sum over the angular momentum quantum numbers. As a result, the thermal pressure and all thermodynamic quantities are separated into two parts that differ only in the spin fugacities of spin-up and spin-down fermions. We calculate the Fermi energy for both components and show that the Fermi energy of the spin-down fermions is lower than that of the spin-up ones. This difference arises from the spin-rotation coupling and leads to a spin polarization consistent with the Barnett effect. In particular, we introduce the spin-chemicorotational ratio $η\equiv Ω^{(0)}/2μ^{(0)}$, which adjusts the spin polarization of the Fermi gas. Here, $Ω^{(0)}$ and $μ^{(0)}$ represent the angular velocity and chemical potential at zero temperature, respectively. The factor $1/2$ accounts for the fermion's spin. We explore the temperature dependence of $μ$ and $Ω$, while assuming that the number of spin-up and spin-down fermions remains temperature independent. Our findings indicate that the spin-down component of the rotating Fermi gas dilutes at lower temperatures compared to the spin-up component. Additionally, we calculate the magnetic susceptibility arising from the Barnett magnetization and demonstrate that it is proportional to the moment of inertia $I$ of the rotating Fermi gas. Finally, we prove that $I$ exhibits a $1/T$ behavior in the high-temperature limit, similar to the Curie law of paramagnetism.

</details>

### [137] [Universal Ladder Structure Across Scales: From Quantum to Black Hole Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06249)
*Rajes Ghosh,Rajendra Prasad Bhatt,Sumanta Chakraborty,Sukanta Bose*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于对称性的统一框架，用于判断二阶常线性微分方程何时具有层次阶梯结构，并在存在时显式构造该阶梯。该方法揭示了与超对称量子力学（supersymmetric quantum mechanics）的深层联系，并通过量子谐振子和克尔黑洞（Kerr black holes）的动力学潮汐响应展示了其应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二阶常线性微分方程（second-order ordinary linear differential equations）在物理学中普遍存在，从量子世界的原子到经典世界的引力天体。然而，缺乏统一的框架来判断这些系统何时具有层次阶梯结构（hierarchical ladder structure），并在存在时显式构造该阶梯。

Method: 提出了一种基于对称性的统一框架，提供了一个"试金石准则"（litmus-test criterion）来判断系统是否允许层次阶梯结构。该方法能够显式构造阶梯，并揭示了与超对称量子力学的深层联系。

Result: 该方法揭示了先前未被充分认识的与超对称量子力学的联系，以及不同物理问题之间的深层共性。通过量子谐振子（quantum harmonic oscillator）和克尔黑洞的动力学潮汐响应（dynamical tidal response）两个应用实例展示了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该对称性框架为分析二阶常线性微分方程的层次阶梯结构提供了统一的方法，揭示了不同物理系统之间的深层数学共性，并展示了在量子力学和广义相对论等领域的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Second-order ordinary linear differential equations appear ubiquitously across physics, describing the behavior of systems from the quantum world of atoms to the classical world of gravitating bodies. We present a unified symmetry-based framework that provides a ``litmus-test criterion'' to determine when such a system admits a hierarchical ladder structure, and, whenever it does, explicitly constructs the ladder. This approach uncovers a previously underappreciated connection to supersymmetric quantum mechanics and a deep commonality among diverse physical problems. Applications to the quantum harmonic oscillator and dynamical tidal response of Kerr black holes are presented to illustrate the framework.

</details>


### [138] [Shadow, Sparsity of Radiation and Energy Emission Rate in Skyrmion Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06259)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Skyrmion黑洞的光学特性，包括光子球、黑洞阴影和光子轨迹，并探讨了Skyrme项对Hawking辐射稀疏性和能量发射谱的影响，为非线性场效应提供了可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索Skyrmion黑洞的光学特性，特别是Skyrme项如何影响光子球位置和黑洞阴影形状，以寻找非线性场效应在标准黑洞几何中的可观测偏离特征。

Method: 通过分析Skyrmion黑洞的光子球、黑洞阴影和光子轨迹，研究Skyrme项及其他时空几何参数对这些光学特性的影响，并计算Hawking辐射的稀疏性和能量发射谱。

Result: 参数变化导致与标准黑洞几何的可观测偏离，Skyrme耦合和背景参数显著影响Hawking辐射稀疏性和能量发射谱，揭示了非线性场贡献与黑洞光学特性之间的关联。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了非线性场贡献与黑洞光学特性之间的联系，对修正引力（modified gravity）场景的观测和理论研究具有重要意义，为探测非线性场效应提供了潜在特征。

Abstract: We examine several observable optical properties of a Skyrmion black hole (BH), focusing on the photon sphere, BH shadow, and photon trajectories. The Skyrme term, along with other geometric parameters of the spacetime, determines the photon sphere location and shapes the resulting BH shadow. Parameter variations produce observable departures from standard BH geometries, offering potential signatures of nonlinear field effects. We also analyze the sparsity of Hawking radiation and the associated energy emission spectra, showing how these quantities respond to the Skyrme coupling and background parameters. Our findings illuminate the connection between nonlinear field contributions and BH optics, with implications for observational and theoretical studies of modified gravity scenarios.

</details>


### [139] [Late-Transition Interacting Thawer Dark Energy: Physics and Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06261)
*Slava G. Turyshev,Diogo H. F. de Souza*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种晚期过渡相互作用解冻模型（LTIT），这是一种晚期激活、可变耦合的耦合精质实现，其中标量场仅与冷暗物质共形耦合。该模型旨在区分膨胀历史的真实低红移形变与重组前校准区域的偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分离晚期暗能量分析中常被混淆的两个问题：膨胀历史的真实低红移形变与重组前校准区域的偏移。通过构建LTIT模型，可以更清晰地分析这些效应。

Method: 方法包括构建晚期激活、可变耦合的耦合精质（coupled quintessence）实现，其中规范标量场仅与冷暗物质共形耦合。推导了精确的背景方程、冷暗物质标度恒等式 $\rhoc(a)=ρ_{c0}a^{-3}C[φ(a)]/C(φ_0)$，以及适用于爱因斯坦-玻尔兹曼求解器的同步规范下的线性标量扰动方程。

Result: 对于代表性基准测试，发现 $Ω_φ(z_*)\sim10^{-9}$ 和 $|Δr_d/r_d|<4\times10^{-3}$，低红移背景偏移保持在亚百分比水平，近似增长响应范围从亚百分比到几个百分比，具体取决于渐近耦合振幅。

Conclusion: 结论表明LTIT不是一个灵活的 $w(z)$ 参数化形式，而是一个受约束的相互作用暗能量框架，其中任何表面上的背景成功都必须通过扰动层面的闭合检验。

Abstract: We formulate the late-transition interacting thawer (LTIT) as a late-activating, variable-coupling realization of coupled quintessence in which a canonical scalar field couples conformally only to cold dark matter. The construction is designed to separate two issues that are often mixed in late-time dark-energy analyses: a genuine low-redshift deformation of the expansion history and a shift of the pre-recombination calibration sector. We derive the exact background equations, the exact CDM scaling identity $\rhoc(a)=ρ_{c0}a^{-3}C[φ(a)]/C(φ_0)$, and the linear scalar perturbation equations in synchronous gauge in a form suitable for Einstein--Boltzmann solvers. For representative benchmarks we find $Ω_φ(z_*)\sim10^{-9}$ and $|Δr_d/r_d|<4\times10^{-3}$, while the low-redshift background shift remains sub-percent and the approximate growth response ranges from sub-percent to several percent, depending on the asymptotic coupling amplitude. LTIT is therefore not a flexible $w(z)$ ansatz but a constrained interacting-dark-energy framework in which any apparent background success must survive perturbation-level closure tests.

</details>

Method: 研究采用理论分析方法，对arXiv:2201.12295中的线性不稳定性结果进行轻微但关键的强化，这一强化结果随后被应用于arXiv:2604.04877中的非线性不稳定性证明。

Result: 成功获得了克尔柯西视界线性不稳定性的强化版本，该强化结果在arXiv:2604.04877中被有效利用，最终证明了克尔柯西视界的非线性不稳定性。

Conclusion: 通过强化线性不稳定性结果，该研究为克尔黑洞柯西视界的非线性不稳定性证明提供了关键支持，深化了对克尔黑洞内部结构稳定性的理解。

Abstract: This note slightly strengthens the result of arXiv:2201.12295 on the linear instability of the Kerr Cauchy horizon. This strengthened result is used in the proof arXiv:2604.04877 of the non-linear instability of the Kerr Cauchy horizon.

### [141] [Reply to 'Comment on "Ideal clocks -- a convenient fiction'' '](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06292)
*Krzysztof Lorek,Jorma Louko,Andrzej Dragan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文是对先前量子场论研究的回复，重新推导了加速腔中量子标量场的退激发概率公式，完全在加速腔的Rindler楔形区域内进行计算，以回应关于使用两个因果不连通Rindler楔形区域的质疑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期有评论文章质疑先前研究中加速腔量子标量场退激发概率公式的推导方法，特别是该计算同时使用了加速腔所在Rindler楔形区域和因果不连通的相对Rindler楔形区域的Rindler模。本文旨在通过完全在加速腔Rindler楔形区域内重新推导该公式，回应这一质疑。

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbation theory）计算，完全在加速腔所在的Rindler楔形（Rindler wedge）内进行推导，避免了使用因果不连通的相对Rindler楔形区域。该方法是对原始研究中计算方法的修正和完善。

Result: 成功重新推导出与原始研究相同的退激发概率公式（de-excitation probability formula），验证了该公式的正确性。同时澄清了原始计算中两组Rindler模的作用。

Conclusion: 通过完全在加速腔Rindler楔形区域内的微扰理论计算，确认了先前研究中退激发概率公式的有效性，并回应了关于使用两个因果不连通Rindler楔形区域的质疑，澄清了相关概念。

Abstract: For a quantum scalar field that is confined in a uniformly linearly accelerated cavity in Minkowski spacetime and interacts linearly with a scalar field that is not confined in the cavity, a de-excitation probability formula was obtained in [1] [K. Lorek et al, Class. Quant. Grav. 32, 175003 (2015) [arXiv:1503.01025]] by a first-order perturbation theory calculation. A recent Comment [2] [V. Toussaint, Class. Quant. Grav. 43, 068001 (2026)] questions this formula on the grounds that the calculation in [1] invokes Rindler modes both in the Rindler wedge of the accelerated cavity and in the opposing, causally disconnected Rindler wedge. In the present Reply we rederive the de-excitation formula given in [1] by a perturbation theory calculation that is formulated entirely within the Rindler wedge of the accelerated cavity. We also take the opportunity to comment on the role of the two sets of Rindler modes in the calculation presented in [1].

</details>


### [142] [Black Hole-Boson Star Binaries: Gravitational Wave Signals and Tidal Disruption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06312)
*Gareth Arturo Marks,Seppe J. Staelens,Ulrich Sperhake*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对包含黑洞和玻色子星（boson star）的双星系统进行了详细的全非线性研究，考虑了标量场的四次自相互作用（quartic self-interaction）和孤子势（solitonic potential）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞-玻色子星双星系统的动机在于理解不同标量势对系统动力学的影响，特别是对引力波（gravitational waveforms）产生的影响，并为构建模型无关的奇异致密天体（exotic compact objects）波形模板库提供参考。

Method: 采用全非线性数值模拟方法，首先强调使用平衡构型（equilibrated configuration）的玻色子星初始数据以获得精确引力波波形，并讨论了改进初始数据约束违反（constraint violations）的方法。随后进行了一系列正碰（head-on collisions）和初步的旋进（inspiral）构型研究。

Result: 研究发现即使在简化的正碰情景中，辐射效率（radiative efficiency）也显著依赖于所选的标量势。此外，适当的标量自相互作用可以抑制潮汐瓦解（tidal disruption），而初始数据的平衡状态对获得准确引力波波形至关重要。

Conclusion: 研究强调了标量势选择对黑洞-玻色子星双星系统动力学的显著影响，为构建模型无关的奇异致密天体波形模板库提供了重要见解，表明需要考虑不同标量相互作用对引力波信号的影响。

Abstract: We present a detailed, fully nonlinear study of binary systems involving one black hole and one boson star, considering the effects of both a quartic self-interaction and a solitonic potential for the scalar field. First, we show the importance of using initial data for which the boson star is in an equilibrated configuration to obtain accurate gravitational waveforms, and discuss methods to further improve constraint violations in the initial data. We then present a series of head-on collisions, showing that even in this simplified scenario the radiative efficiency varies significantly with the scalar potential chosen. In addition to this, we present a preliminary study of inspiral configurations, showing that an appropriate scalar self-interaction can suppress tidal disruption. We comment throughout on implications for attempts to build model-agnostic waveform template banks for exotic compact objects.

</details>

This construction yields a rigorous definition of geometric drift, a coordinate-independent scalar measuring the intrinsic instability of the detector noise floor. The central result is the flatness theorem, which proves that the curvature of the connection vanishes for scalar fields. This establishes a holonomic update law, guaranteeing that the optimal filter correction is path-independent and determined solely by the instantaneous noise state, free from geometric phase or hysteresis. This framework unifies the static theory of Wiener-Hopf factorization with the dynamic requirements of real-time control, providing a rigorous certification for the stability of zero-latency calibration routines and establishing a foundation for gauge-theoretic signal processing (GTSP) in next-generation detector networks.

Abstract: The quantum field theory for a massless scalar field on a two-dimensional non-singular black hole spacetime gives a non-vanishing probability for a particle to tunnel out of the black hole. The black hole spacetime contains an outer and an inner horizon, and the transition amplitude between a one-particle state localized inside the inner horizon, and a one-particle state localized outside the outer horizon is non-zero, even when the regions where the states are localized are causally disconnected. The total tunnelling probability asymptotes to a maximal value that depends on the background spacetime geometry only through the surface gravity of the two horizons, and is polynomially suppressed by the sum of the inverse surface gravities of the inner and outer horizons.

Abstract: This work constructs a new class of traversable wormhole solutions with a double-throat topology, modeled as a localized perturbation of the Ellis-Bronnikov metric in a string cloud background. Embedding diagrams and the analysis of curvature invariants, including the Kretschmann scalar and the Weyl invariant, illustrate the geometric transition from single to double-throat structures as a function of the perturbation amplitude. By imposing the zero-tidal condition, we derive analytical expressions for the energy density and pressures, showing an asymptotic $r^{-2}$ decay characteristic of a string cloud, endowed with the topology of a global monopole.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先推导任意球对称场的一般偏转角，然后建立基于标准广义相对论的观测基线。假设光学关系适用于修正的有效势，将该形式应用于深MOND（deep-MOND）、汤川型（Yukawa-type）和幂律f(R)模型，提供偏转角和爱因斯坦半径的封闭解析表达式。

Result: 获得了深MOND、汤川型和幂律f(R)模型的偏转角和爱因斯坦半径的封闭解析表达式。数值光线追踪模拟验证了这些解析结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架作为通向当代研究的概念桥梁，为学生提供计算经验和对引力透镜基础的批判性认识，使修正引力理论的探索变得可及。

Abstract: We present a framework that reformulates gravitational lensing as an optical phenomenon governed by an effective refractive index, enabling exploration of modified gravity theories using undergraduate-level mathematics and optics. After deriving the general deflection angle for arbitrary spherically symmetric fields, we establish the observational baseline using standard general relativity, including the lens equation and Einstein ring properties. Assuming the optical relation holds for modified effective potentials, we apply the formalism to deep-MOND, Yukawa-type, and power-law ($f(R)$) models, providing closed-form analytical expressions for the deflection angle and Einstein radius. Numerical ray-tracing simulations validate these analytical results. This framework serves as a conceptual bridge to contemporary research, offering students computational experience and critical awareness of gravitational lensing foundations.

Abstract: We propose a novel laboratory test of gravity combining seismic-wave measurements with cosmic-ray muon detections.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现应变信号对陷阱位置有强烈的非对称依赖性，当传感器位于输入镜附近时最大化；关键新结果是输入镜位移对应变信号的噪声耦合可相对于末端镜位移和共模镜运动被高度抑制。

Abstract: Optically levitated sensors inside a Fabry-Pérot cavity have been proposed for high-frequency gravitational-wave (GW) detection, though their configuration for gravitational wave sensitivity exhibits counterintuitive features. We provide a new detailed general relativistic derivation of the interaction between a gravitational wave and a levitated object in an optical cavity, demonstrating gauge independence of the observable response. We find a strong asymmetric dependence of the strain signal on trap position, maximized when the sensor is located near the input mirror, in agreement with previous results. A key new result of this work is the consequence of this asymmetry on the noise coupling: the coupling of input-mirror displacements to the strain signal can be highly suppressed relative to that of end-mirror displacements and common-mode mirror motion. These results clarify the physical origin of the gravitational wave interaction with such a sensor and establish crucial design principles for optical levitation based high-frequency GW detectors.

### [154] [Continuum dynamics from quantised interaction rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06947)
*Park Junhu,Yongsoo Ha,Myungjoo Kang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种直接通过量化相互作用规则（quantised interaction rules）计算保守动力学的快速量化数值方法（Fast Quantised Numerical Method, FQNM），该方法通过反对称整数转移（antisymmetric integer transfer）执行动力学，物理场仅在重构后出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统保守动力学计算通常采用浮点近似连续微分算子（continuum differential operators），这会因舍入误差（rounding）和离散化伪影（discretisation artefacts）而掩盖守恒性。因此需要一种更直接的保守演化计算方法。

Method: 该方法将保守演化直接表述为作用于可数状态（countable states）的量化相互作用规则，通过反对称整数转移执行动力学，物理场仅在重构后出现，形成快速量化数值方法（FQNM）。

Result: 在高频输运（high-frequency transport）中，该方法在深入奈奎斯特区域（Nyquist regime）时仍保持准确，而标准高阶浮点基线（high-order floating-point baseline）会恶化。在非线性激波形成（nonlinear shock formation）中，它保持网格级结构（grid-level structure），对单元漂移（cell drifting）保持鲁棒性，同时保持精确的离散守恒。

Conclusion: 保守动力学可以直接通过离散相互作用规则执行，连续行为仅作为底层量化状态的重构而出现，这为保守动力学计算提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Conservative dynamics are typically computed as floating-point approximations to continuum differential operators, which can obscure conservation through rounding and discretisation artefacts. Here we instead formulate conservative evolution directly as quantised interaction rules acting on countable states. The resulting Fast Quantised Numerical Method (FQNM) executes dynamics through antisymmetric integer transfer, with physical fields appearing only after reconstruction. In high-frequency transport, the method remains accurate deep into the Nyquist regime where a standard high-order floating-point baseline deteriorates. In nonlinear shock formation, it preserves grid-level structure and remains robust to cell drifting while maintaining exact discrete conservation. These results show that conservative dynamics can be executed directly through discrete interaction rules, with continuum behaviour emerging only as a reconstruction of underlying quantised states.

</details>

### [155] [Viscous Bending Mitigates the Spontaneous Meandering of Rivulets in Hele-Shaw Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07222)
*Grégoire Le Lay,Adrian Daerr*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了Hele-Shaw槽中细长溪流自发蜿蜒的物理机制，解决了15年来关于最不稳定波数选择和绝对/对流不稳定性判别的开放性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决Hele-Shaw槽中溪流蜿蜒不稳定性机制中的关键未解问题：最不稳定波数的选择机制，以及该不稳定性是绝对还是对流性质。自Daerr等人2011年发现不稳定性阈值以来，这些核心问题已悬而未决15年。

Method: 通过将粘性弯曲效应纳入深度平均的Navier-Stokes方程，并基于低粘度假设推导了更简洁的不稳定性判据。该方法建立了粘性弯曲与波长选择之间的直接联系。

Result: 研究确定了粘性弯曲效应是选择最快增长模式的关键机制，解决了波长选择问题。同时明确了蜿蜒不稳定性为绝对性质而非对流性质，并提供了基于摩擦效应的新物理解释，替代了传统的惯性力解释。

Conclusion: 该研究完善了受限几何中溪流蜿蜒的线性稳定性理论框架，确立了粘性弯曲作为波长选择的关键参数。这些结果为未来探索自发蜿蜒不稳定性的非线性特征奠定了基础。

Abstract: We investigate the spontaneous meandering of slender rivulets in Hele-Shaw cells and identify the physical mechanism that selects the most unstable wavenumber, a quantity that has remained elusive even since the identification of the instability threshold [Daerr et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 106, 184501 (2011)]. Earlier criteria did not distinguish between wavelengths and thus predicted an undiscriminated amplification of arbitrarily short perturbations. By incorporating viscous bending into the depth-averaged Navier-Stokes equations, we show that this effect is responsible for the selection of a fastest-growing mode, answering a question that has remained open for 15 years. We answer the open question of whether the meandering instability is absolute or convective. Our analysis also provides a simpler alternative derivation of the instability criterion, based on a low-viscosity assumption, and finally it yields a new physical interpretation of the mechanism: the destabilization arises directly from friction effects, instead of being caused by inertial forces. Together, these results complete the linear-stability picture of rivulet meandering in confined geometries, and establish viscous bending as a key parameter governing wavelength selection. They lay the groundwork for future exploration of the nonlinear features of the spontaneous meandering instability.

Method: 采用晶格技术（lattice techniques）在软SU(N)胶子的热有效场论框架内进行计算，其中N=2,3，并在足够大的体积下覆盖从0.6到10^15 GeV的宽温度范围，同时计算了非微扰热轴子产生率。

Abstract: We report our new lattice results for the sphaleron rate calculated within a thermal effective field theory of soft SU(N) gluons, where $N=2,3$, for a wide range of temperatures spanning from $0.6$-$10^{15}$ GeV at sufficiently large volumes. Comparing these results with sphaleron rates in a non-thermal SU(N) plasma where the infrared gluons are over-occupied, we estimate the typical thermalization time for these ultra-soft gluons during the early stages of reheating after inflation. We have also calculated the non-perturbative thermal axion production rate using lattice techniques which shows significant deviation from its perturbative estimate even at the electroweak scale.

### [157] [The Roberge-Weiss transition as a probe for conformality in many-flavor QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07284)
*Massimo D'Elia,Marco Nacci,Kevin Zambello*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Roberge-Weiss转变温度$T_{RW}$来确定QCD共形窗口（conformal window）起始点的新方法，并通过$N_f=8$味夸克的格点模拟发现$T_{RW}$在手征极限下消失，表明8味QCD已进入共形窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于确定QCD中$N_f$种无质量味道夸克在基础表示下的共形窗口起始点。传统方法存在局限性，需要发展新的有效方法从格点模拟中精确确定这一临界点。

Method: 方法基于研究Roberge-Weiss转变温度$T_{RW}$，该温度出现在特定虚重子化学势值处，也可解释为有限盒子中电荷共轭对称性自发破缺的临界空间尺寸的倒数。采用stout改进的交错费米子和树级改进的Symanzik纯规范作用量对$N_f=8$味QCD进行离散化，在欧几里得时间维度$N_t=8,10,12,16,24$下进行格点模拟。

Result: 研究发现$N_f=8$味QCD的Roberge-Weiss转变温度$T_{RW}$在手征极限下已经消失。这一结果表明$N_f=8$已经处于共形窗口内，为确定共形窗口的起始点提供了直接证据。

Conclusion: 结论表明$T_{RW}$在手征极限下消失时的临界$N_f$值与共形窗口的起始点一致。基于$N_f=8$的模拟结果，该方法成功识别出共形窗口的边界，为QCD相结构研究提供了新的有效工具。

Abstract: We consider the problem of identifying the onset of the conformal window for QCD with $N_f$ massless flavors in the fundamental representation, and propose a new effective method to determine it from lattice simulations. This method is based on the investigation of the so-called Roberge-Weiss transition temperature $T_{RW}$, which is encountered at specific values of the imaginary baryon chemical potential, and can also be interpreted as the inverse of the critical spatial size at which charge conjugation is spontaneously broken in a finite box. Since $T_{RW}$ corresponds to a genuine phase transition for any value of the quark masses, it is a well-defined quantity; we argue that the critical $N_f$ at which $T_{RW}$ vanishes in the chiral limit coincides with the onset of the conformal window. We implement our proposal by investigating QCD with $N_f = 8$ flavors, discretized via stout improved staggered fermions and the tree-level improved Symanzik pure gauge action, at Euclidean temporal extents $N_t = 8, 10, 12, 16, 24$. In this case, we find evidence that $T_{RW}$ already vanishes in the chiral limit, indicating that $N_f = 8$ is already in the conformal window.

### [158] [Non-Monotonicity of Transverse Momentum Correlations in Au + Au Collisions at RHIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06434)
*STAR Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次测量了固定靶Au+Au碰撞中双粒子横向动量（p_T）关联，在中心碰撞中观察到预期标度行为的明显破坏，并识别出碰撞能量依赖关系的显著非单调性（约5σ显著性），为高重子密度下的状态方程提供了新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用STAR实验在束流能量扫描（Beam Energy Scan, BES）第二阶段程序中，测量了固定靶Au+Au碰撞在核子-核子质心能量√s_NN = 3.0-7.7 GeV范围内，中快度区域带电粒子的双粒子横向动量（p_T）关联。研究了标度关联子对参与核子数（N_part）的依赖关系，以检验独立源模型的预期。

Result: 在中心碰撞中观察到预期标度行为（1/√N_part）的明显破坏，并识别出p_T关联对碰撞能量依赖关系的统计显著非单调性（约5σ显著性）。相比之下，输运模型计算和中中心碰撞数据的显著性分别仅为2σ和1.4σ，不足以支持非单调性主张。

Conclusion: 这些观测结果为高重子密度下的状态方程提供了新约束，并可能对QCD临界点的存在敏感。研究结果揭示了中心碰撞中关联行为的异常特征，为进一步探索QCD相图提供了重要线索。

Abstract: Event-by-event transverse momentum correlations are sensitive to the equation of state of strongly interacting matter and are expected to exhibit anomalous fluctuations in the vicinity of the QCD critical point. We report the first measurements of two-particle transverse momentum ($p_T$) correlations for mid-rapidity charged particles in fixed-target Au+Au collisions at nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energies $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 3.0--7.7$ GeV, measured by the STAR experiment during the Beam Energy Scan (BES) Phase II program. The dependence of the scaled correlator on the number of participating nucleons ($N_{part}$) is studied to test expectations from an independent-source scenario, where the correlations are expected to scale as $1/\sqrt{N_{part}}$. We observe a clear breakdown of the expected scaling behavior in central collisions and identify a statistically significant non-monotonic dependence of the $p_T$ correlations on collision energy, with a significance of approximately $5σ$. In contrast, transport-model calculations and data from mid-central collisions yield significances of only $2σ$ and $1.4σ$, respectively, insufficient to support a claim of non-monotonicity. These observations provide new constraints on the equation of state at high baryon density and may be sensitive to the presence of a QCD critical point.

### [160] [Noether-Type Theorems and the Generalized Herglotz Principle in $q$-Contact Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06488)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展经典拉格朗日力学（classical Lagrangian mechanics）的范围，超越辛（symplectic）和单接触结构（single-contact structures），为复杂耗散系统（complex dissipative systems）提供统一的几何框架。

Method: 方法基于均匀q-接触流形（uniform q-contact manifolds），构建了扩展相空间并配备多个接触1-形式（contact 1-forms）。建立了哈密顿和拉格朗日形式体系，并通过广义Herglotz原理（generalized Herglotz principle）为q-接触拉格朗日系统提供了变分起源。

Result: 主要结果包括：建立了广义Noether型定理（generalized Noether-type theorem）描述对称性与耗散量的关系；推导了q-接触欧拉-拉格朗日方程（q-contact Euler-Lagrange equations）；证明了变分公式与几何q-接触哈密顿动力学（geometric q-contact Hamiltonian dynamics）的完全等价性。

Conclusion: 该理论为复杂耗散系统提供了有效的几何洞察，通过多参数依赖动力学的显式示例展示了其有效性，成功扩展了经典力学框架以处理更一般的耗散现象。

Abstract: We develop a unified geometric framework for dissipative mechanical systems based on uniform $q$-contact manifolds, which provide an extended phase space equipped with multiple contact $1$-forms. Within this setting, we construct both Hamiltonian and Lagrangian formalisms and establish a generalized Noether-type theorem describing the relationship between symmetries and dissipated quantities.
  We further show that $q$-contact Lagrangian systems admit a genuine variational origin through a generalized Herglotz principle involving multiple action variables. The resulting $q$-contact Euler--Lagrange equations naturally depend on the scalar combination $\sum_{i=1}^q \partial L/\partial z_i$, reflecting the intrinsic structure of uniform $q$-contact geometry. We prove that this variational formulation is fully equivalent to the geometric $q$-contact Hamiltonian dynamics generated by the energy function.
  Several explicit examples involving multi-parameter dependent dynamics illustrate the effectiveness of the theory and demonstrate its potential to provide geometric insight into complex dissipative systems, thereby extending the scope of classical Lagrangian mechanics beyond symplectic and single-contact structures.

</details>


### [161] [The clothoid helices obtained via the Lie-Darboux method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06577)
*H. C. Rosu,J. de la Cruz,P. Lemus-Basilio*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过李-达布方法（Lie-Darboux method）获得并详细研究了曲率和挠率都与弧长成正比的回旋螺旋线（clothoid helices），同时在同一方法框架下引入了其平移对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索具有特定几何特性的曲线，即曲率（curvature）和挠率（torsion）都与弧长（arclength）成正比的回旋螺旋线，这类曲线在几何学和微分几何中具有理论意义。

Method: 采用李-达布方法（Lie-Darboux method）来推导和构造这类特殊的回旋螺旋线，并将同一方法应用于引入其平移对应物（shifted counterparts）。

Result: 成功获得了曲率和挠率都与弧长成正比的回旋螺旋线，并对其进行了详细研究，同时在同一方法框架下构建了其平移版本。

Conclusion: 通过李-达布方法系统地研究了一类特殊的回旋螺旋线及其平移对应物，为具有特定曲率-挠率关系的空间曲线提供了理论分析框架。

Abstract: The clothoid helices that have both curvature and torsion directly proportional to the arclength are obtained via the Lie-Darboux method and studied in some detail. Shifted counterparts are also introduced and presented in the same approach.

</details>


### [162] [Variational derivation of the homogeneous Boltzmann equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06919)
*Giada Basile,Dario Benedetto,Carlo Orrieri*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为具有硬球截面的齐次玻尔兹曼方程引入了变分公式，该公式能唯一选择能量守恒解。研究证明该解源于微观动力学（Kac随机游走），并在初始分布满足熵混沌性的最小假设下，建立了熵混沌性的时间传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 齐次玻尔兹曼方程（homogeneous Boltzmann equation）通常存在多个解，需要确定唯一物理相关的能量守恒解。研究旨在建立微观动力学与宏观方程解之间的严格联系，并探讨初始熵混沌性在时间演化中的保持。

Method: 提出了一种变分公式（variational formulation）来刻画具有硬球截面（hard-sphere cross section）的齐次玻尔兹曼方程。该方法从微观动力学Kac随机游走（Kac's walk）出发，研究熵混沌性（entropic chaoticity）的传播特性。

Result: 证明了变分公式能唯一选择能量守恒解，且该解确实源于Kac随机游走的微观动力学。在初始分布满足熵混沌性的最小假设下，建立了熵混沌性在时间演化中的传播性质。

Conclusion: 研究为齐次玻尔兹曼方程提供了选择唯一物理解的变分框架，建立了微观动力学与宏观方程解之间的严格对应关系，并证明了熵混沌性在适当初始条件下的时间传播特性。

Abstract: We introduce a variational formulation of the homogeneous Boltzmann equation, with hard-sphere cross section, which selects the unique energy conserving solution. We prove that this solution arises from the microscopic dynamics, namely Kac's walk, and we establish the propagation in time of entropic chaoticity, under the minimal assumption that the initial distribution is entropically chaotic.

</details>


### [163] [Existence of a Phase Transition in the One-Dimensional Ising Spin Glass Model with Long-Range Interactions on the Nishimori Line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07130)
*Manaka Okuyama,Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将戴森（Dyson）关于长程相互作用一维伊辛模型（Ising model）相变存在的经典结果，扩展至西岛线（Nishimori line）上的伊辛自旋玻璃（spin glass）模型。对于相互作用形式为$r^{-α}$（$1 < α< 3/2$）的情况，作者严格证明了相变的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 戴森（Dyson）曾严格证明了一维长程相互作用伊辛模型（$r^{-α}$形式，$1 < α< 2$）存在相变。本研究旨在将这一经典结果推广到具有高斯无序（Gaussian disorder）的西岛线（Nishimori line）上的伊辛自旋玻璃模型。

Method: 研究方法遵循戴森（Dyson）的思路。首先，在西岛线（Nishimori line）上的戴森分层伊辛自旋玻璃模型（Dyson hierarchical Ising spin glass model）中，针对幂律相互作用$J(r) \sim r^{-α}$（$1 < α< 3/2$），证明有限低温下存在长程序（long-range order）。证明的关键工具包括：平均场自旋玻璃模型严格分析中发展的插值法（interpolation method）、西岛线上的吉布斯-博戈留波夫不等式（Gibbs--Bogoliubov inequality）以及齐雷尔松-伊布拉吉莫夫-苏达科夫不等式（Tsirelson--Ibragimov--Sudakov inequality，即高斯集中不等式）。

Result: 对于$1 < α< 3/2$的情况，作者严格证明了西岛线（Nishimori line）上具有长程相互作用的一维伊辛自旋玻璃模型存在相变。对于$α\ge 3/2$的情况，相变的存在性仍然是一个未解决的问题（open problem）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将戴森（Dyson）关于经典伊辛模型的相变结果推广到了西岛线（Nishimori line）上的伊辛自旋玻璃模型，为$1 < α< 3/2$的长程相互作用范围提供了严格的证明，并指出了$α\ge 3/2$时问题的开放性。

Abstract: Dyson [Commun. Math. Phys. 12, 91 (1969)] rigorously proved the existence of a phase transition in the one-dimensional Ising model with long-range interactions of the form $r^{-α}$ for $1 < α< 2$. In the present study, we extend this result to the Ising spin glass model with Gaussian disorder on the Nishimori line. Following Dyson's method, we first prove the existence of long-range order at finite low temperatures in the Dyson hierarchical Ising spin glass model on the Nishimori line, with power-law-like interactions $J(r) \sim r^{-α}$ for $1 < α< 3/2$. The key ingredients of the proof are the interpolation method developed in the rigorous analysis of mean-field spin glass models, the Gibbs--Bogoliubov inequality on the Nishimori line, and the Tsirelson--Ibragimov--Sudakov inequality (Gaussian concentration inequality). We then use the Griffiths inequality on the Nishimori line to rigorously establish the existence of a phase transition in the one-dimensional Ising spin glass model with long-range interactions on the Nishimori line for $1 < α< 3/2$. For $α\ge 3/2$, the existence of a phase transition remains an open problem.

</details>
